fuse_fiss_utils.f90       coverage:  81.82 %func     25.62 %block

     1) !==========================================================================================!
     2) !==========================================================================================!
     3) !  Module fuse_fiss_utils.                                                                 !
     4) !  Routines to terminate and fuse patches, and to terminate, fuse and split cohorts.       !
     5) !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
     6) module fuse_fiss_utils
     7) 
     8)    use ed_state_vars,only :   copy_patchtype        & ! subroutine
     9)                             , deallocate_patchtype  & ! subroutine
    10)                             , allocate_patchtype    & ! subroutine
    11)                             , allocate_sitetype     & ! subroutine
    12)                             , deallocate_sitetype   & ! subroutine
    13)                             , copy_sitetype_mask    & ! subroutine
    14)                             , copy_sitetype         & ! subroutine
    15)                             , copy_patchtype_mask   ! ! subroutine
    16) 
    17)    contains
    18)    !=======================================================================================!
    19)    !=======================================================================================!
    20)    !      This subroutine will sort the cohorts by size (1st = tallest, last = shortest.)  !
    21)    ! In case there is a tie (for example, when 2 cohorts have reached the maximum possible !
    22)    ! height, then we use DBH for tie breaking, and if they have the exact same DBH, then   !
    23)    ! we simply pick the lowest index (as they are exactly the same).  This could cause     !
    24)    ! some problems when the new grass allometry is implemented, though.                    !
    25)    !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
    26)    subroutine sort_cohorts(cpatch)
    27) 
    28)       use ed_state_vars,only :  patchtype   ! ! Structure
    29)       implicit none
    30)       !----- Arguments --------------------------------------------------------------------!
    31)       type(patchtype)              , target      :: cpatch    ! Current patch
    32)       !----- Local variables --------------------------------------------------------------!
    33)       type(patchtype)              , pointer     :: temppatch ! Scratch patch structure
    34)       integer                                    :: ico       ! Counters
    35)       integer                                    :: tallco    ! Index of tallest cohort
    36)       real                                       :: tophgt    ! Maximum height considered
    37)       logical                                    :: sorted    ! Patch is already sorted
    38)       logical        , dimension(:), allocatable :: attop     ! Top cohorts, for tie-break
    39)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
    40)       
    41)       !----- No need to sort an empty patch or a patch with a single cohort. --------------!
    42)       if (cpatch%ncohorts < 2) return
    43) 
    44) 
    45)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
    46)       !     Check whether this patch is already sorted.   We don't want to do the entire   !
    47)       ! deallocating/copying/allocating thing if it's not needed as this takes up too much !
    48)       ! time.                                                                              !
    49)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
    50)       sorted = .true.
    51)       sortcheck: do ico=1,cpatch%ncohorts-1
    52)          sorted = cpatch%hite(ico) >= cpatch%dbh(ico+1) .and.                              &
    53)                   cpatch%dbh(ico)  >= cpatch%dbh(ico+1)
    54)          if (.not. sorted) exit sortcheck
    55)       end do sortcheck
    56)       if (sorted) return
    57)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
    58) 
    59) 
    60) 
    61)       !----- Assign a scratch patch. ------------------------------------------------------!
    62)       nullify(temppatch)
    63)       allocate(temppatch)
    64)       call allocate_patchtype(temppatch,cpatch%ncohorts)
    65) 
    66)       !----- Allocate the logical flag for tie-breaking. ----------------------------------!
    67)       allocate(attop(cpatch%ncohorts))
    68) 
    69)       ico = 0
    70)       !---- Loop until all cohorts were sorted. -------------------------------------------!
    71)       do while(ico < cpatch%ncohorts)
    72)          ico = ico + 1
    73) 
    74)          !----- Find the maximum height. --------------------------------------------------!
    75)          tophgt = maxval(cpatch%hite)
    76) 
    77)          !----- Find all cohorts that are at this height. ---------------------------------!
    78)          attop  = cpatch%hite == tophgt
    79) 
    80)          !----- Find the fattest cohort at a given height. --------------------------------!
    81)          tallco = maxloc(cpatch%dbh,dim=1,mask=attop)
    82) 
    83)          !----- Copy to the scratch structure. --------------------------------------------!
    84)          call copy_patchtype(cpatch,temppatch,tallco,tallco,ico,ico)
    85) 
    86)          !----- Put a non-sense DBH so this will never "win" again. -----------------------!
    87)          cpatch%hite(tallco) = -huge(1.)
    88)          cpatch%dbh (tallco) = -huge(1.)
    89) 
    90)       end do
    91) 
    92)       !------ Copy the scratch patch to the regular one and deallocate it. ----------------!
    93)       call copy_patchtype(temppatch,cpatch,1,cpatch%ncohorts,1,cpatch%ncohorts)
    94)       call deallocate_patchtype(temppatch)
    95)       deallocate(temppatch)
    96) 
    97)       !----- De-allocate the logical flag. ------------------------------------------------!
    98)       deallocate(attop)
    99) 
   100)       return
   101) 
   102)    end subroutine sort_cohorts
   103)    !=======================================================================================!
   104)    !=======================================================================================!
   105) 
   106) 
   107) 
   108) 
   109) 
   110) 
   111)    !=======================================================================================!
   112)    !=======================================================================================!
   113)    !    This subroutine will eliminate cohorts based on their sizes. This is intended to   !
   114)    ! eliminate cohorts that have little contribution and thus we can speed up the run.     !
   115)    !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   116)    subroutine terminate_cohorts(csite,ipa,elim_nplant,elim_lai)
   117)       use pft_coms           , only : min_cohort_size  & ! intent(in)
   118)                                     , l2n_stem         & ! intent(in)
   119)                                     , c2n_stem         & ! intent(in)
   120)                                     , c2n_storage      & ! intent(in), lookup table
   121)                                     , c2n_leaf         ! ! intent(in), lookup table
   122) 
   123)       use decomp_coms        , only : f_labile         ! ! intent(in), lookup table
   124) 
   125)       use ed_state_vars      , only : patchtype        & ! structure
   126)                                     , sitetype         ! ! structure
   127)       implicit none
   128)       !----- Arguments --------------------------------------------------------------------!
   129)       type(sitetype)       , target      :: csite        ! Current site
   130)       integer              , intent(in)  :: ipa          ! Current patch ID
   131)       real                 , intent(out) :: elim_nplant  ! Nplants eliminated here
   132)       real                 , intent(out) :: elim_lai     ! LAI eliminated here
   133)       !----- Local variables --------------------------------------------------------------!
   134)       type(patchtype)      , pointer     :: cpatch       ! Current patch
   135)       type(patchtype)      , pointer     :: temppatch    ! Scratch patch structure
   136)       logical, dimension(:), allocatable :: remain_table ! Flag: this cohort will remain.
   137)       integer                            :: ico          ! Counter
   138)       integer                            :: ipft         ! PFT size
   139)       real                               :: csize        ! Size of current cohort
   140)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   141)       
   142)       cpatch => csite%patch(ipa)
   143)       elim_nplant = 0.
   144)       elim_lai    = 0.
   145) 
   146)       !----- Initialize the temporary patch structures and the remain/terminate table -----!
   147)       nullify(temppatch)
   148)       allocate(temppatch)
   149)       allocate(remain_table(cpatch%ncohorts))
   150)       remain_table(:) = .true.
   151)      
   152)       !----- Main loop --------------------------------------------------------------------!
   153)       do ico = 1,cpatch%ncohorts
   154) 
   155)          !----- Save the PFT type in a convenient alias. ----------------------------------!
   156)          ipft = cpatch%pft(ico)
   157) 
   158)          !----- Checking whether the cohort size is too small -----------------------------!
   159)          csize = cpatch%nplant(ico)                                                        &
   160)                * (cpatch%balive(ico) + cpatch%bdead(ico) + cpatch%bstorage(ico))
   161) 
   162)          if ( csize < min_cohort_size(ipft) ) then
   163)             !----- Cohort is indeed too small, it won't remain ----------------------------!
   164)             remain_table(ico) = .false.
   165)             elim_nplant = elim_nplant + cpatch%nplant(ico) * csite%area(ipa)
   166)             elim_lai    = elim_lai    + cpatch%lai(ico)    * csite%area(ipa)
   167) 
   168)             !----- Update litter pools ----------------------------------------------------!
   169)             csite%fsc_in(ipa) = csite%fsc_in(ipa) + cpatch%nplant(ico)                     &
   170)                               * (f_labile(ipft)*cpatch%balive(ico) + cpatch%bstorage(ico))
   171) 
   172)             csite%fsn_in(ipa) = csite%fsn_in(ipa) + cpatch%nplant(ico)                     &
   173)                               * ( f_labile(ipft) * cpatch%balive(ico) / c2n_leaf(ipft)     &
   174)                                 + cpatch%bstorage(ico) / c2n_storage)
   175)             
   176)             csite%ssc_in(ipa) = csite%ssc_in(ipa) + cpatch%nplant(ico)                     &
   177)                               * ( (1.0 - f_labile(ipft)) * cpatch%balive(ico)              &
   178)                                 + cpatch%bdead(ico))
   179)             
   180)             csite%ssl_in(ipa) = csite%ssl_in(ipa) + cpatch%nplant(ico)                     &
   181)                               * ( (1.0 - f_labile(ipft)) * cpatch%balive(ico)              &
   182)                                 + cpatch%bdead(ico) ) * l2n_stem/c2n_stem(ipft)
   183) 
   184)          end if
   185)       end do
   186) 
   187)       !----- Copy the remaining cohorts to a temporary patch ------------------------------!
   188)       call allocate_patchtype(temppatch,count(remain_table))
   189)       call copy_patchtype_mask(cpatch,temppatch,remain_table,size(remain_table)            &
   190)                               ,count(remain_table))
   191) 
   192)       !----- Reallocate the new patch and populate with the saved cohorts -----------------!
   193)       call deallocate_patchtype(cpatch)
   194)       call allocate_patchtype(cpatch,count(remain_table))
   195)       call copy_patchtype(temppatch,cpatch,1,cpatch%ncohorts,1,cpatch%ncohorts)
   196)       call sort_cohorts(cpatch)
   197)      
   198)       !----- Deallocate the temporary patch -----------------------------------------------!     
   199)       call deallocate_patchtype(temppatch)
   200)       deallocate(temppatch)
   201)       deallocate(remain_table)
   202) 
   203)       !----- Update the cohort census at the site level -----------------------------------!
   204)       csite%cohort_count(ipa) = cpatch%ncohorts
   205)       if (elim_lai < 0. .or. elim_nplant < 0.) then
   206)          write (unit=*,fmt='(a,1x,es12.5)') 'TERMINATE: ELIM_LAI=',elim_lai
   207)          write (unit=*,fmt='(a,1x,es12.5)') 'TERMINATE: ELIM_NPLANT=',elim_nplant
   208)       end if
   209)       return
   210)    end subroutine terminate_cohorts
   211)    !=======================================================================================!
   212)    !=======================================================================================!
   213) 
   214) 
   215) 
   216) 
   217) 
   218) 
   219)    !=======================================================================================!
   220)    !=======================================================================================!
   221)    !    This subroutine will eliminate tiny or empty patches. This is intended to          !
   222)    ! eliminate patches that have little contribution and thus we can speed up the run.     !
   223)    !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   224)    subroutine terminate_patches(csite)
   225) 
   226)       use ed_state_vars, only : polygontype        & ! Structure
   227)                               , sitetype           & ! Structure
   228)                               , patchtype          ! ! Structure
   229)       use disturb_coms , only : min_patch_area     ! ! intent(in)
   230)       implicit none
   231)       !----- Arguments --------------------------------------------------------------------!
   232)       type(sitetype)       , target      :: csite        ! Current site
   233)       !----- Local variables --------------------------------------------------------------!
   234)       type(sitetype)       , pointer     :: tempsite     ! Scratch site
   235)       integer                            :: ipa          ! Counters
   236)       logical, dimension(:), allocatable :: remain_table ! Flag: this patch will remain.
   237)       real                               :: total_area   ! Area of removed patches
   238)       real                               :: elim_area    ! Area of removed patches
   239)       real                               :: new_area     ! Just to make sure area is 1.
   240)       real                               :: area_scale   ! Scaling area factor.
   241)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   242) 
   243)       allocate (remain_table(csite%npatches))
   244)       remain_table(:) = .true.
   245) 
   246)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   247)       !     Loop through all the patches in this site and determine which of these patches !
   248)       ! is too small in area to be valid. Remove these patches via the mask function.      !
   249)       ! Realocate a new site with only the valid patches, and normalize their areas and    !
   250)       ! plant densities to reflect the area loss.                                          !
   251)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   252)       elim_area  = 0.0
   253)       total_area = 0.0
   254)       do ipa = 1,csite%npatches
   255)          if (csite%area(ipa) < min_patch_area) then
   256)             elim_area = elim_area + csite%area(ipa)
   257)             remain_table(ipa) = .false.
   258)          end if
   259)          total_area = total_area + csite%area(ipa)
   260)       end do
   261) 
   262)       !----- Use the mask to resize the patch vectors in the current site. ----------------!
   263)       allocate(tempsite)
   264)       call allocate_sitetype(tempsite,count(remain_table))
   265)       call copy_sitetype_mask(csite,tempsite,remain_table,size(remain_table)               &
   266)                              ,count(remain_table))
   267)       call deallocate_sitetype(csite)
   268)       call allocate_sitetype(csite,count(remain_table))
   269) 
   270)       remain_table(:)                   = .false.
   271)       remain_table(1:tempsite%npatches) = .true.
   272)       call copy_sitetype_mask(tempsite,csite,remain_table(1:tempsite%npatches)             &
   273)                              ,count(remain_table),count(remain_table))
   274)       call deallocate_sitetype(tempsite)
   275)       deallocate(tempsite)
   276)       deallocate(remain_table)
   277) 
   278)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   279)       !    Renormalize the total area.                                                     !
   280)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   281)       new_area   = 0.
   282)       area_scale = 1.0 / (total_area - elim_area)
   283)       do ipa = 1,csite%npatches
   284)          csite%area(ipa) = csite%area(ipa) * area_scale
   285)          new_area        = new_area + csite%area(ipa)
   286)       end do
   287) 
   288)       if (abs(new_area-1.0) > 1.e-5) then
   289)          write (unit=*,fmt='(a,1x,es12.5)') ' + ELIM_AREA:',elim_area
   290)          write (unit=*,fmt='(a,1x,es12.5)') ' + NEW_AREA: ',new_area
   291)          call fatal_error('New_area should be 1 but it isn''t!!!','terminate_patches'      &
   292)                          ,'fuse_fiss_utils.f90')
   293)       end if 
   294)       
   295)       return
   296)    end subroutine terminate_patches
   297)    !=======================================================================================!
   298)    !=======================================================================================!
   299) 
   300) 
   301) 
   302) 
   303) 
   304) 
   305)    !=======================================================================================!
   306)    !=======================================================================================!
   307)    !     This subroutine will rescale the area of the patches.  This is almost the same as !
   308)    ! the terminate_patches subroutine, except that no patch is removed.                    !
   309)    !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   310)    subroutine rescale_patches(csite)
   311)       use update_derived_props_module
   312)       use ed_state_vars, only : polygontype        & ! Structure
   313)                               , sitetype           & ! Structure
   314)                               , patchtype          ! ! Structure
   315)       use disturb_coms , only : min_patch_area     ! ! intent(in)
   316)       use allometry    , only : size2bl        ! ! function
   317)       use ed_max_dims  , only : n_dist_types       & ! intent(in)
   318)                               , n_pft              ! ! intent(in)
   319)       
   320)       implicit none
   321)       !----- Arguments --------------------------------------------------------------------!
   322)       type(sitetype)         , target      :: csite        ! Current site
   323)       !----- Local variables --------------------------------------------------------------!
   324)       type(patchtype)        , pointer     :: cpatch       ! Pointer to current site
   325)       type(sitetype)         , pointer     :: tempsite     ! Scratch site
   326)       integer                              :: ipa          ! Counter
   327)       integer                              :: ico          ! Counter
   328)       integer                              :: ilu          ! Counter
   329)       integer                              :: ipft         ! Counter
   330)       logical                              :: onlyone      ! Is this a single patch?
   331)       logical, dimension  (:), allocatable :: remain_table ! Flag: this patch shall remain.
   332)       real   , dimension  (:), allocatable :: old_area     ! Area before rescaling
   333)       real   , dimension  (:), allocatable :: elim_area    ! Area of removed patches
   334)       real                                 :: laimax       ! Max. LAI for current cohort
   335)       real   , dimension  (:), allocatable :: lu_area      ! Area of disturbance type
   336)       real                                 :: n_scale      ! Scaling nplant factor.
   337)       real                                 :: site_area    ! Total site area (must be 1).
   338)       real   , dimension  (:), allocatable :: patch_laimax ! Total LAI_max per patch
   339)       real   , dimension  (:), allocatable :: lu_laimax    ! total bleaf per land use type
   340)       integer, dimension  (:), allocatable :: lu_npatch    ! # of patches per land use type
   341)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   342) 
   343) 
   344)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   345)       !     No need to re-scale patches if there is a single patch left.                   !
   346)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   347)       onlyone = csite%npatches == 1
   348)       if (onlyone .and. csite%area(1) == 1.) return
   349)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   350) 
   351) 
   352)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   353)       !     Loop through all the patches in this site and determine which of these patches !
   354)       ! is too small in area to be valid. These will be removed and the remaining patches  !
   355)       ! will be rescaled later to account for this change and changes in biomass           !
   356)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   357)       allocate (remain_table(csite%npatches))
   358)       remain_table(:) = .true.
   359) 
   360)       allocate (elim_area(n_dist_types))
   361)       elim_area (:) = 0.0
   362) 
   363)       !Manfredo: inefficient: (.not. onlyone) should be checked outside the do loop
   364)       do ipa = 1,csite%npatches
   365)          if (csite%area(ipa) < min_patch_area .and. (.not. onlyone)) then
   366)             ilu = csite%dist_type(ipa)
   367)             elim_area(ilu)= elim_area (ilu) + csite%area(ipa)
   368)             remain_table(ipa) = .false.
   369)          end if
   370)       end do
   371)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   372) 
   373) 
   374)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   375)       !     Remove patches that are smaller than the minimum non-negligible area.          !
   376)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   377)       if ( sum(elim_area) > 0.0 ) then
   378)          !----- Use the mask to resize the patch vectors in the current site. -------------!
   379)          allocate(tempsite)
   380)          call allocate_sitetype(tempsite,count(remain_table))
   381)          call copy_sitetype_mask(csite,tempsite,remain_table,size(remain_table)            &
   382)                                 ,count(remain_table))
   383)          call deallocate_sitetype(csite)
   384)          call allocate_sitetype(csite,count(remain_table))
   385) 
   386)          remain_table(:)                   = .false.
   387)          remain_table(1:tempsite%npatches) = .true.
   388)          call copy_sitetype_mask(tempsite,csite,remain_table(1:tempsite%npatches)          &
   389)                                 ,count(remain_table),count(remain_table))
   390)          call deallocate_sitetype(tempsite)
   391)          deallocate(tempsite)
   392)       end if
   393)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   394) 
   395) 
   396)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   397)       !     Allocate a temporary array that will contain the potential leaf biomass of     !
   398)       ! each patch.  This is done so phenology doesn't impact the area.                    !
   399)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   400)       allocate (patch_laimax(csite%npatches))
   401)       allocate (old_area    (csite%npatches))
   402)       patch_laimax (:) = 0.0
   403)       old_area     (:) = 0.0
   404)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   405) 
   406) 
   407) 
   408)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   409)       !     Loop through land use types, total area per disturbance type will remain       !
   410)       !  unchanged.  Area of the patches (PFTs) within a disturbance type will be rescaled !
   411)       !  based on their area.                                                              !
   412)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   413)       allocate (lu_npatch(n_dist_types))
   414)       allocate (lu_laimax(n_dist_types))
   415)       allocate (lu_area  (n_dist_types))
   416)       lu_npatch (:) = 0
   417)       lu_area   (:) = 0.0
   418)       lu_laimax (:) = 0.0
   419)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   420) 
   421) 
   422) 
   423)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   424)       !     Add the leaf biomass of all sites.                                             !
   425)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   426)       site_area = 0.0
   427)       do ipa=1,csite%npatches
   428)          !----- This patch. ---------------------------------------------------------------!
   429)          cpatch => csite%patch(ipa)
   430)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   431) 
   432)          !----- Find the disturbance type. ------------------------------------------------!
   433)          ilu = csite%dist_type(ipa)
   434)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   435) 
   436)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   437)          !      Determine the maximum attainable leaf area index for each PFT, which will  !
   438)          ! be used to rescale the relative area of the patch.                              !
   439)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   440)          do ico = 1,cpatch%ncohorts
   441)             ipft              = cpatch%pft(ico)
   442)             laimax            = cpatch%nplant(ico) * cpatch%sla(ico)                       &
   443)                               * size2bl(cpatch%dbh(ico),cpatch%hite(ico),ipft)
   444)             patch_laimax(ipa) = patch_laimax(ipa) + laimax * csite%area(ipa)
   445)          end do
   446) 
   447)          lu_area  (ilu) = lu_area  (ilu) + csite%area  (ipa)
   448)          lu_laimax(ilu) = lu_laimax(ilu) + patch_laimax(ipa)
   449)          lu_npatch(ilu) = lu_npatch(ilu) + 1
   450) 
   451)          site_area      = site_area + csite%area(ipa) 
   452)       end do
   453)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   454) 
   455) 
   456) 
   457)       !------ Normalise the area of each land use type so the total is going to be one. ---!
   458)       lu_area(:) = lu_area(:) / site_area
   459)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   460) 
   461) 
   462) 
   463)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   464)       !    Renormalize the total area.                                                     !
   465)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   466)       site_area = 0.0
   467)       do ipa = 1,csite%npatches
   468) 
   469)          !----- Find the disturbance type. ------------------------------------------------!
   470)          ilu = csite%dist_type(ipa)
   471)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   472) 
   473) 
   474)          !----- Find the new area, based on the fraction of biomass. ----------------------!
   475)          old_area(ipa)   = csite%area(ipa)
   476)          csite%area(ipa) = patch_laimax(ipa) / lu_laimax(ilu) * lu_area(ilu)
   477)          site_area       = site_area + csite%area(ipa)
   478)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   479) 
   480) 
   481)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   482)          !     We must change the scale for nplant (and all "extensive" cohort-level       !
   483)          ! variables) so the site-level maximum LAI and maximum biomass stay the same.     !
   484)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   485)          n_scale = old_area(ipa) / csite%area(ipa)
   486)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   487) 
   488)          cpatch => csite%patch(ipa)
   489)          call update_cohort_extensive_props(cpatch,1,cpatch%ncohorts,n_scale)
   490)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   491)       end do
   492)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   493) 
   494) 
   495) 
   496) 
   497) 
   498) 
   499)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   500)       !     Sanity check: total new area must be 1.0.                                      !
   501)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   502)       if (abs(site_area-1.0) > 1.e-5) then
   503)          write (unit=*,fmt='(a)'          ) '---------------------------------------------'
   504)          write (unit=*,fmt='(a)'          ) ' PATCH BIOMASS:'
   505)          write (unit=*,fmt='(a)'          ) ' '
   506)          write (unit=*,fmt='(7(1x,a))'    ) '       PATCH','     LU_TYPE','PATCH_LAIMAX'   &
   507)                                            ,'   LU_LAIMAX','     LU_AREA','    OLD_AREA'   &
   508)                                            ,'    NEW_AREA'
   509)          do ipa=1,csite%npatches
   510)             ilu = csite%dist_type(ipa)
   511)             write(unit=*,fmt='(2(1x,i12),5(1x,es12.5))')                                   &
   512)                     ipa,ilu,patch_laimax(ipa),lu_laimax(ilu),lu_area(ilu),old_area(ipa)    &
   513)                    ,csite%area(ipa)
   514)          end do
   515)          write (unit=*,fmt='(a,1x,es12.5)') ' SITE LAIMAX  :',sum(lu_laimax)
   516)          write (unit=*,fmt='(a,1x,es12.5)') ' SITE_AREA    :',site_area
   517)          write (unit=*,fmt='(a)'          ) '---------------------------------------------'
   518)          call fatal_error('New_area should be 1 but it isn''t!!!','rescale_patches'        &
   519)                          ,'fuse_fiss_utils.f90')
   520)       end if 
   521)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   522) 
   523) 
   524) 
   525)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   526)       !     Free memory before we leave the sub-routine.                                   !
   527)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   528)       deallocate(patch_laimax)
   529)       deallocate(remain_table)
   530)       deallocate(old_area    )
   531)       deallocate(lu_area     )
   532)       deallocate(lu_laimax   )
   533)       deallocate(lu_npatch   )
   534)       deallocate(elim_area   )
   535)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   536)       return
   537)    end subroutine rescale_patches
   538)    !=======================================================================================!
   539)    !=======================================================================================!
   540) 
   541) 
   542) 
   543) 
   544) 
   545) 
   546)    !=======================================================================================!
   547)    !=======================================================================================!
   548)    !   This subroutine will perform cohort fusion based on various similarity criteria to  !
   549)    ! determine whether they can be fused with no significant loss of information. The user !
   550)    ! is welcome to set up a benchmark, but should be aware that no miracles will happen    !
   551)    ! here. If there are more very distinct cohorts than maxcohort, then the user will need !
   552)    ! to live with that and accept life is not always fair with those with limited          !
   553)    ! computational resources.                                                              !
   554)    !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   555)    subroutine fuse_cohorts(csite,ipa, lsl, fuse_initial)
   556) 
   557)       use ed_state_vars       , only : sitetype            & ! Structure
   558)                                      , patchtype           ! ! Structure
   559)       use pft_coms            , only : hgt_max             & ! intent(in)
   560)                                      , is_grass            ! ! intent(in)
   561)       use fusion_fission_coms , only : fusetol_h           & ! intent(in)
   562)                                      , fusetol             & ! intent(in)
   563)                                      , lai_fuse_tol        & ! intent(in)
   564)                                      , fuse_relax          & ! intent(in)
   565)                                      , coh_tolerance_max   ! ! intent(in)
   566)       use ed_max_dims         , only : n_pft               ! ! intent(in)
   567)       use mem_polygons        , only : maxcohort           ! ! intent(in)
   568)       use allometry           , only : size2bl         ! ! function
   569)       use ed_misc_coms        , only : igrass              ! ! intent(in)
   570)       implicit none
   571)       !----- Arguments --------------------------------------------------------------------!
   572)       type(sitetype)         , target      :: csite             ! Current site
   573)       integer                , intent(in)  :: ipa               ! Current patch ID
   574)       integer                , intent(in)  :: lsl               ! Lowest soil level
   575)       logical                , intent(in)  :: fuse_initial      ! Initialisation step?
   576)       !----- Local variables --------------------------------------------------------------!
   577)       logical, dimension(:)  , allocatable :: fuse_table     ! Flag, remaining cohorts
   578)       type(patchtype)        , pointer     :: cpatch         ! Current patch
   579)       type(patchtype)        , pointer     :: temppatch      ! Scratch patch
   580)       integer                              :: donc,recc,ico3 ! Counters
   581)       logical                              :: fusion_test    ! Flag: proceed with fusion?
   582)       real                                 :: newn           ! new nplants of merged coh.
   583)       real                                 :: lai_max        ! Maximum LAI the fused 
   584)                                                              !    cohort could have.
   585)       real                                 :: total_size     ! Total size
   586)       real                                 :: tolerance_mult ! Multiplication factor
   587)       integer                              :: ncohorts_old   ! # of coh. before fusion test
   588)       real                                 :: mean_dbh       ! Mean DBH           (???)
   589)       real                                 :: mean_hite      ! Mean height        (???)
   590)       real                                 :: new_size       ! New size
   591)       integer                              :: ntall          ! # of tall cohorts  (???)
   592)       integer                              :: nshort         ! # of short cohorts (???)
   593)       logical                              :: any_fusion     ! Flag: was there any fusion?
   594)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   595) 
   596) 
   597)       !----- Start with no factor ---------------------------------------------------------!
   598)       tolerance_mult = 1.0
   599) 
   600)       cpatch => csite%patch(ipa)
   601) 
   602)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   603)       !     Return if maxcohort is 0 (flag for no cohort fusion), or if the patch is empty !
   604)       ! or has a single cohort.                                                            !
   605)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   606)       if (maxcohort == 0 .or. cpatch%ncohorts < 2) return
   607) 
   608)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   609)       !    Calculate mean DBH and HITE to help with the normalization of differences mean  !
   610)       ! hite is not being used right now, but can be optioned in the future if it seems    !
   611)       ! advantageous.                                                                      !
   612)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   613)       mean_dbh  = 0.0
   614)       mean_hite = 0.0
   615)       nshort    = 0
   616)       ntall     = 0
   617)       do ico3 = 1,cpatch%ncohorts
   618)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   619)          !    Get fusion height threshold.  Height is a good predictor when plants are     !
   620)          ! growing in height, but it approaches the maximum height DBH becomes the only    !
   621)          ! possible predictor because height saturates.                                    !
   622)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   623)          if (cpatch%hite(ico3) < (0.95 * hgt_max(cpatch%pft(ico3))) ) then
   624)             mean_hite = mean_hite + cpatch%hite(ico3)
   625)             nshort    = nshort + 1
   626)          else
   627)             mean_dbh  = mean_dbh + cpatch%dbh(ico3)
   628)             ntall     = ntall + 1
   629)          end if
   630)       end do 
   631)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   632)       if (ntall  > 0) mean_dbh = mean_dbh   / real(ntall)
   633)       if (nshort > 0) mean_hite= mean_hite  / real(nshort)
   634) 
   635)       !----- Initialize table. In principle, all cohorts stay. ----------------------------!
   636)       allocate(fuse_table(cpatch%ncohorts))
   637)       fuse_table(:) = .true.
   638) 
   639)       force_fusion: do
   640)          
   641)          ncohorts_old =  count(fuse_table) ! Save current number of cohorts ---------------!
   642)          
   643)          donloop:do donc = 1,cpatch%ncohorts-1
   644)             if (.not. fuse_table(donc)) cycle donloop ! This one is gone, move to next.
   645) 
   646)             recloop: do recc = donc+1,cpatch%ncohorts
   647)                if (.not. fuse_table(recc)) cycle recloop ! This one is gone, move to next.
   648)                                                          ! Hope it never happens...
   649) 
   650)                !---------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   651)                !     Test for similarity.  Again, we use height to assess similarity only  !
   652)                ! when the cohort is not approaching the maximum height.  If this is the    !
   653)                ! case, then we use DBH to test.                                            !
   654)                !---------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   655)                if (cpatch%hite(donc) >= (0.95 * hgt_max(cpatch%pft(donc))) ) then
   656)                   mean_dbh=0.5*(cpatch%dbh(donc)+cpatch%dbh(recc))
   657)                   fusion_test = ( abs(cpatch%dbh(donc) - cpatch%dbh(recc)))/mean_dbh       &
   658)                               < fusetol * tolerance_mult
   659)                elseif (fuse_relax) then
   660)                   fusion_test = ( abs(cpatch%hite(donc) - cpatch%hite(recc))               &
   661)                                      / (0.5*(cpatch%hite(donc) + cpatch%hite(recc)))  <    &
   662)                                 fusetol * tolerance_mult)  
   663)                else
   664)                   fusion_test = (abs(cpatch%hite(donc) - cpatch%hite(recc))  <             &
   665)                                 fusetol_h * tolerance_mult)
   666)                end if
   667) 
   668)                if (fusion_test) then
   669) 
   670)                   !----- New cohort has the total number of plants ------------------------!
   671)                   newn = cpatch%nplant(donc) + cpatch%nplant(recc)
   672) 
   673)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   674)                   !     We now check the maximum LAI the fused cohorts could have.  We     !
   675)                   ! don't want the cohort to have a very large LAI.  If both cohorts have  !
   676)                   ! leaves fully flushed, this is the same as adding the individual LAIs,  !
   677)                   ! but if they are not, we need to consider that LAI may grow...          !
   678)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   679)                   if (is_grass(cpatch%pft(donc)) .and. igrass==1) then
   680)                       !--use actual bleaf for grass
   681)                       lai_max = ( cpatch%nplant(recc) * cpatch%bleaf(recc)                 &
   682)                                 + cpatch%nplant(donc) * cpatch%bleaf(donc) )               &
   683)                                 * cpatch%sla(recc)
   684)                   else
   685)                       !--use dbh for trees
   686)                       lai_max = ( cpatch%nplant(recc)                                      &
   687)                                 * size2bl(cpatch%dbh(recc),cpatch%hite(recc)               &
   688)                                          ,cpatch%pft(recc))                                &
   689)                                 + cpatch%nplant(donc)                                      &
   690)                                 * size2bl(cpatch%dbh(donc),cpatch%hite(donc)               &
   691)                                          ,cpatch%pft(donc)))                               &
   692)                                 * cpatch%sla(recc)
   693)                   end if
   694) 
   695)                   !----- Checking the total size of this cohort before and after fusion. --!
   696)                   total_size = cpatch%nplant(donc) * ( cpatch%balive(donc)                 &
   697)                                                      + cpatch%bdead(donc)                  &
   698)                                                      + cpatch%bstorage(donc) )             &
   699)                              + cpatch%nplant(recc) * ( cpatch%balive(recc)                 &
   700)                                                      + cpatch%bdead(recc)                  &
   701)                                                      + cpatch%bstorage(recc) )
   702) 
   703)                   
   704)                   
   705)                   
   706)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   707)                   !    Six conditions must be met to allow two cohorts to be fused:        !
   708)                   ! 1. Both cohorts must have the same PFT;                                !
   709)                   ! 2. Combined LAI won't be too large.                                    !
   710)                   ! 3. Both cohorts must have the same status with respect to the first    !
   711)                   !    census.                                                             !
   712)                   ! 4. Both cohorts must have the same recruit status with respect to the  !
   713)                   !    first census.                                                       !
   714)                   ! 5. Both cohorts must have the same recruitment status with respect to  !
   715)                   !    the DBH.                                                            !
   716)                   ! 6. Both cohorts must have the same recruitment status with respect to  !
   717)                   !    the census.                                                         !
   718)                   ! 7. Both cohorts must have the same phenology status.                   !
   719)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   720)                   if (     cpatch%pft(donc)              == cpatch%pft(recc)               &
   721)                      .and. lai_max                        < lai_fuse_tol*tolerance_mult    &
   722)                      .and. cpatch%first_census(donc)     == cpatch%first_census(recc)      &
   723)                      .and. cpatch%new_recruit_flag(donc) == cpatch%new_recruit_flag(recc)  &
   724)                      .and. cpatch%recruit_dbh     (donc) == cpatch%recruit_dbh(recc)       &
   725)                      .and. cpatch%census_status   (donc) == cpatch%census_status(recc)     &
   726)                      .and. cpatch%phenology_status(donc) == cpatch%phenology_status(recc)  &
   727)                      ) then
   728) 
   729)                      !----- Proceed with fusion -------------------------------------------!
   730)                      call fuse_2_cohorts(cpatch,donc,recc,csite%can_prss(ipa)              &
   731)                                         ,csite%can_shv(ipa),lsl,fuse_initial)
   732) 
   733)                      !----- Flag donating cohort as gone, so it won't be checked again. ---!
   734)                      fuse_table(donc) = .false.
   735)                      
   736)                      !----- Check whether total size and LAI are conserved. ---------------!
   737)                      new_size = cpatch%nplant(recc) * ( cpatch%balive(recc)                &
   738)                                                       + cpatch%bdead(recc)                 &
   739)                                                       + cpatch%bstorage(recc) )
   740)                      if (new_size < 0.99* total_size .or. new_size > 1.01* total_size )    &
   741)                      then
   742)                         write (unit=*,fmt='(a,1x,es14.7)') 'OLD SIZE: ',total_size
   743)                         write (unit=*,fmt='(a,1x,es14.7)') 'NEW SIZE: ',new_size
   744)                         call fatal_error('Cohort fusion didn''t conserve plant size!!!'    &
   745)                                         &,'fuse_2_cohorts','fuse_fiss_utils.f90')
   746)                      end if
   747)                      !---------------------------------------------------------------------!
   748) 
   749) 
   750)                      !---------------------------------------------------------------------!
   751)                      !    Recalculate the means                                            !
   752)                      !---------------------------------------------------------------------!
   753)                      mean_dbh  = 0.0
   754)                      mean_hite = 0.0
   755)                      nshort    = 0
   756)                      ntall     = 0
   757)                      recalcloop: do ico3 = 1,cpatch%ncohorts
   758)                         if (.not. fuse_table(ico3)) cycle recalcloop
   759)                         !----- Get fusion height threshold --------------------------------!
   760)                         if (cpatch%hite(ico3) < (0.95 * hgt_max(cpatch%pft(ico3))) ) then
   761)                            mean_hite = mean_hite + cpatch%hite(ico3)
   762)                            nshort = nshort+1
   763)                         else
   764)                            mean_dbh = mean_dbh + cpatch%dbh(ico3)
   765)                            ntall=ntall+1
   766)                         end if
   767)                      end do recalcloop
   768)                      !---------------------------------------------------------------------!
   769)                      cycle donloop
   770)                   end if
   771)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   772)                end if
   773)             end do recloop
   774)          end do donloop
   775) 
   776)          !------ If we are under maxcohort, no need to continue fusing. -------------------!
   777)          if ( count(fuse_table) <= abs(maxcohort)) exit force_fusion
   778)          !------ If no fusion happened and the tolerance exceeded the maximum, I give up. -!
   779)          if ( count(fuse_table) == ncohorts_old .and. tolerance_mult > coh_tolerance_max ) &
   780)             exit force_fusion
   781) 
   782)          tolerance_mult = tolerance_mult * 1.01
   783)          ncohorts_old = count(fuse_table)
   784)       end do force_fusion
   785) 
   786)       !----- If any fusion has happened, then we need to rearrange cohorts. ---------------!
   787)       any_fusion = .not. all(fuse_table)
   788)       if (any_fusion) then
   789) 
   790)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   791)          !     Now copy the merged patch to a temporary patch using the fuse_table as a    !
   792)          ! mask.  Then allocate a temporary patch, copy the remaining cohorts there.       !
   793)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   794)          nullify (temppatch)
   795)          allocate(temppatch)
   796)          call allocate_patchtype(temppatch,cpatch%ncohorts)
   797)          call copy_patchtype_mask(cpatch,temppatch,fuse_table,size(fuse_table)             &
   798)                                  ,count(fuse_table))
   799) 
   800)          !----- Now I reallocate the current patch with its new reduced size. -------------!
   801)          call deallocate_patchtype(cpatch)  
   802)          call allocate_patchtype(cpatch,count(fuse_table))
   803)   
   804)          !----- Make fuse_table true to all remaining cohorts. ----------------------------!
   805)          fuse_table(:)                 = .false.
   806)          fuse_table(1:cpatch%ncohorts) = .true.
   807)          call copy_patchtype_mask(temppatch,cpatch,fuse_table,size(fuse_table)             &
   808)                                  ,count(fuse_table))
   809) 
   810)          !----- Discard the scratch patch. ------------------------------------------------!
   811)          call deallocate_patchtype(temppatch)
   812)          deallocate(temppatch)  
   813) 
   814)          !----- Sort cohorts by size again, and update the cohort census for this patch. --!
   815)          call sort_cohorts(cpatch)
   816)          csite%cohort_count(ipa) = count(fuse_table)
   817)       end if
   818) 
   819)       !----- Deallocate the aux. table ----------------------------------------------------!
   820)       deallocate(fuse_table)
   821)      
   822)       return
   823)    end subroutine fuse_cohorts
   824)    !=======================================================================================!
   825)    !=======================================================================================!
   826) 
   827) 
   828) 
   829) 
   830) 
   831) 
   832)    !=======================================================================================!
   833)    !=======================================================================================!
   834)    !   This subroutine will split two cohorts if its LAI has become too large.  This is    !
   835)    ! only necessary when we solve radiation cohort by cohort rather than layer by layer.   !
   836)    !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   837)    subroutine split_cohorts(cpatch, green_leaf_factor)
   838)       use update_derived_props_module
   839)       use ed_state_vars        , only : patchtype              & ! structure
   840)                                       , copy_patchtype         ! ! sub-routine
   841)       use pft_coms             , only : q                      & ! intent(in), lookup table
   842)                                       , qsw                    & ! intent(in), lookup table
   843)                                       , is_grass               ! ! intent(in)
   844)       use fusion_fission_coms  , only : lai_tol                ! ! intent(in)
   845)       use ed_max_dims          , only : n_pft                  ! ! intent(in)
   846)       use allometry            , only : dbh2h                  & ! function
   847)                                       , bd2dbh                 & ! function
   848)                                       , bl2dbh                 & ! function
   849)                                       , bl2h                   & ! function
   850)                                       , dbh2bd                 ! ! function
   851)       use ed_misc_coms         , only : igrass                 ! ! intent(in)
   852)       implicit none
   853)       !----- Constants --------------------------------------------------------------------!
   854)       real                   , parameter   :: epsilon=0.0001    ! Tweak factor...
   855)       !----- Arguments --------------------------------------------------------------------!
   856)       type(patchtype)        , target      :: cpatch            ! Current patch
   857)       real, dimension(n_pft) , intent(in)  :: green_leaf_factor !
   858)       !----- Local variables --------------------------------------------------------------!
   859)       type(patchtype)        , pointer     :: temppatch         ! Temporary patch
   860)       logical, dimension(:)  , allocatable :: split_mask        ! Flag: split this cohort
   861)       integer                              :: ico               ! Counter
   862)       integer                              :: inew              ! Counter
   863)       integer                              :: ncohorts_new      ! New # of cohorts
   864)       integer                              :: tobesplit         ! # of cohorts to be split
   865)       integer                              :: ipft              ! PFT type
   866)       real                                 :: stai              ! Potential TAI
   867)       real                                 :: old_nplant        ! Old nplant
   868)       real                                 :: new_nplant        ! New nplant
   869)       real                                 :: old_size          ! Old size
   870)       real                                 :: new_size          ! New size
   871)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   872) 
   873) 
   874)       !----- Initialize the vector with splitting table -----------------------------------!
   875)       allocate(split_mask(cpatch%ncohorts))
   876)       split_mask(:) = .false.
   877)       old_nplant = 0.
   878)       old_size   = 0.
   879)       !----- Loop through cohorts ---------------------------------------------------------!
   880)       do ico = 1,cpatch%ncohorts
   881)          ipft = cpatch%pft(ico)
   882) 
   883)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------! 
   884)          !     STAI is the potential TAI that this cohort has when its leaves are fully    !
   885)          ! flushed.                                                                        !
   886)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------! 
   887)          stai = cpatch%nplant(ico) * cpatch%balive(ico) * green_leaf_factor(ipft)          &
   888)               * q(ipft) / ( 1.0 + q(ipft) + qsw(ipft) * cpatch%hite(ico) )                 &
   889)               * cpatch%sla(ico) + cpatch%wai(ico)
   890) 
   891)          !----- If the resulting TAI is too large, split this cohort. ---------------------!
   892)          split_mask(ico) = stai > lai_tol
   893)          
   894)          old_nplant = old_nplant + cpatch%nplant(ico)
   895)          old_size   = old_size   + cpatch%nplant(ico) * ( cpatch%balive(ico)               &
   896)                                                         + cpatch%bdead(ico)                &
   897)                                                         + cpatch%bstorage(ico) )
   898)       end do
   899) 
   900)       !----- Compute the new number of cohorts. -------------------------------------------!
   901)       tobesplit    = count(split_mask)
   902)       ncohorts_new = cpatch%ncohorts + tobesplit
   903)       
   904)       if (tobesplit > 0) then
   905) 
   906)          !----- Allocate the temppatch. ---------------------------------------------------!
   907)          nullify(temppatch)
   908)          allocate(temppatch)
   909)          call allocate_patchtype(temppatch,cpatch%ncohorts)
   910) 
   911)          !----- Fill the temp space with the current patches. -----------------------------!
   912)          call copy_patchtype(cpatch,temppatch,1,cpatch%ncohorts,1,cpatch%ncohorts)
   913) 
   914)          !----- Deallocate the current patch. ---------------------------------------------!
   915)          call deallocate_patchtype(cpatch)
   916) 
   917)          !----- Re-allocate the current patch. --------------------------------------------!
   918)          call allocate_patchtype(cpatch,ncohorts_new)
   919) 
   920)          !----- Transfer the temp values back in. -----------------------------------------!
   921)          call copy_patchtype(temppatch,cpatch,1,temppatch%ncohorts,1,temppatch%ncohorts)
   922) 
   923)          !----- Remove the temporary patch. -----------------------------------------------!
   924)          call deallocate_patchtype(temppatch)
   925)          deallocate(temppatch)
   926)      
   927)          inew = size(split_mask)
   928)          do ico = 1,size(split_mask)
   929) 
   930)             if (split_mask(ico)) then
   931) 
   932)                !---------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   933)                !   Half the densities of the original cohort.  All "extensive" variables   !
   934)                ! must be rescaled.                                                         !
   935)                !---------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   936)                call update_cohort_extensive_props(cpatch,ico,ico,0.5)
   937)                !---------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   938) 
   939) 
   940)                !----- Apply these values to the new cohort. -------------------------------!
   941)                inew = inew+1
   942)                call copy_patchtype(cpatch,cpatch,ico,ico,inew,inew)
   943)                !---------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   944) 
   945)                !----- Tweaking bdead, to ensure carbon is conserved. ----------------------!
   946)                if (is_grass(cpatch%pft(ico)) .and. igrass==1) then 
   947)                    !-- use bleaf for grass
   948)                    cpatch%bleaf(ico)  = cpatch%bleaf(ico) * (1.-epsilon)
   949)                    cpatch%dbh  (ico)  = bl2dbh(cpatch%bleaf(ico), cpatch%pft(ico))
   950)                    cpatch%hite (ico)  = bl2h(cpatch%bleaf(ico), cpatch%pft(ico))
   951) 
   952)                    cpatch%bleaf(inew)  = cpatch%bleaf(inew) * (1.+epsilon)
   953)                    cpatch%dbh  (inew)  = bl2dbh(cpatch%bleaf(inew), cpatch%pft(inew))
   954)                    cpatch%hite (inew)  = bl2h(cpatch%bleaf(inew), cpatch%pft(inew))
   955)                else
   956)                    !-- use bdead for trees
   957)                    cpatch%bdead(ico)  = cpatch%bdead(ico) * (1.-epsilon)
   958)                    cpatch%dbh  (ico)  = bd2dbh(cpatch%pft(ico), cpatch%bdead(ico))
   959)                    cpatch%hite (ico)  = dbh2h(cpatch%pft(ico), cpatch%dbh(ico))
   960) 
   961)                    cpatch%bdead(inew) = cpatch%bdead(inew) * (1.+epsilon)
   962)                    cpatch%dbh  (inew) = bd2dbh(cpatch%pft(inew), cpatch%bdead(inew))
   963)                    cpatch%hite (inew) = dbh2h(cpatch%pft(inew), cpatch%dbh(inew))
   964)                end if
   965)                !---------------------------------------------------------------------------!
   966) 
   967)             end if
   968)          end do
   969) 
   970)          !----- After splitting, cohorts may need to be sorted again... -------------------!
   971)          call sort_cohorts(cpatch)
   972) 
   973)          !----- Checking whether the total # of plants is conserved... --------------------!
   974)          new_nplant = 0.
   975)          new_size   = 0.
   976)          do ico=1,cpatch%ncohorts
   977)             new_nplant = new_nplant + cpatch%nplant(ico)
   978)             new_size   = new_size   + cpatch%nplant(ico) * ( cpatch%balive(ico)            &
   979)                                                            + cpatch%bdead(ico)             &
   980)                                                            + cpatch%bstorage(ico) )
   981)          end do
   982)          if (new_nplant < 0.99 * old_nplant .or. new_nplant > 1.01 * old_nplant .or.       &
   983)              new_size   < 0.99 * old_size   .or. new_size   > 1.01 * old_size) then
   984)             write (unit=*,fmt='(a,1x,es14.7)') 'OLD NPLANT: ',old_nplant
   985)             write (unit=*,fmt='(a,1x,es14.7)') 'NEW NPLANT: ',new_nplant
   986)             write (unit=*,fmt='(a,1x,es14.7)') 'OLD SIZE:   ',old_size
   987)             write (unit=*,fmt='(a,1x,es14.7)') 'NEW SIZE:   ',new_size
   988)             call fatal_error('Cohort splitting didn''t conserve plants!!!'                 &
   989)                                         &,'split_cohorts','fuse_fiss_utils.f90')
   990)          end if
   991)          
   992)       end if
   993)       deallocate(split_mask)
   994)       return
   995)    end subroutine split_cohorts
   996)    !=======================================================================================!
   997)    !=======================================================================================!
   998) 
   999) 
  1000) 
  1001) 
  1002) 
  1003) 
  1004)    !=======================================================================================!
  1005)    !=======================================================================================!
  1006)    !     This subroutine will merge two cohorts into 1. The donating cohort (donc) is the  !
  1007)    ! one that will be deallocated, while the receptor cohort (recc) will contain the       !
  1008)    !  information from both cohorts.                                                       !
  1009)    !                                                                                       !
  1010)    !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1011)    subroutine fuse_2_cohorts(cpatch,donc,recc,can_prss,can_shv,lsl &
  1012)                             ,fuse_initial)
  1013)       use ed_state_vars      , only : patchtype              ! ! Structure
  1014)       use pft_coms           , only : is_grass               ! ! intent(in)
  1015)       use therm_lib          , only : uextcm2tl              & ! subroutine
  1016)                                     , vpdefil                & ! subroutine
  1017)                                     , qslif                  ! ! function
  1018)       use allometry          , only : dbh2krdepth            & ! function
  1019)                                     , bd2dbh                 & ! function
  1020)                                     , bl2dbh                 & ! function
  1021)                                     , bl2h                   & ! function
  1022)                                     , dbh2h                  ! ! function
  1023)       use ed_max_dims        , only : n_mort                 ! ! intent(in)
  1024)       use ed_misc_coms       , only : writing_long           & ! intent(in)
  1025)                                     , writing_eorq           & ! intent(in)
  1026)                                     , writing_dcyc           & ! intent(in)
  1027)                                     , ndcycle                & ! intent(in)
  1028)                                     , igrass                 ! ! intent(in)
  1029)       use consts_coms        , only : lnexp_min              & ! intent(in)
  1030)                                     , lnexp_max              & ! intent(in)
  1031)                                     , tiny_num               ! ! intent(in)
  1032)       use fusion_fission_coms, only : corr_cohort
  1033)       implicit none
  1034)       !----- Arguments --------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1035)       type(patchtype) , target     :: cpatch            ! Current patch
  1036)       integer                      :: donc              ! Donating cohort.
  1037)       integer                      :: recc              ! Receptor cohort.
  1038)       real            , intent(in) :: can_prss          ! Canopy air pressure
  1039)       real            , intent(in) :: can_shv           ! Canopy air specific humidity
  1040)       integer         , intent(in) :: lsl               ! Lowest soil level
  1041)       logical         , intent(in) :: fuse_initial      ! Called from initialisation
  1042)       !----- Local variables --------------------------------------------------------------!
  1043)       integer                      :: imon              ! Month for cb loop
  1044)       integer                      :: t                 ! Time of day for dcycle loop
  1045)       integer                      :: imty              ! Mortality type
  1046)       real                         :: newni             ! Inverse of new nplants
  1047)       real                         :: exp_mort_donc     ! Exp(mortality) donor
  1048)       real                         :: exp_mort_recc     ! Exp(mortality) receptor
  1049)       real                         :: rlai              ! LAI of receiver
  1050)       real                         :: dlai              ! LAI of donor
  1051)       real                         :: rwai              ! WAI of receiver
  1052)       real                         :: dwai              ! WAI of donor
  1053)       real                         :: rnplant           ! nplant of receiver
  1054)       real                         :: dnplant           ! nplant of donor
  1055)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1056) 
  1057) 
  1058) 
  1059)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1060)       !    Find the scaling factor for variables that are not "extensive".                 !
  1061)       !  - If the unit is X/plant, then we scale by nplant.                                !
  1062)       !  - If the unit is X/m2_leaf, then we scale by LAI.                                 !
  1063)       !  - If the unit is X/m2_wood, then we scale by WAI.                                 !
  1064)       !  - If the unit is X/m2_gnd, then we add, since they are "extensive".               !
  1065)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1066)       newni   = 1.0 / (cpatch%nplant(recc) + cpatch%nplant(donc))
  1067)       rnplant = cpatch%nplant(recc) / (cpatch%nplant(recc) + cpatch%nplant(donc))
  1068)       dnplant = 1.d0 - dble(rnplant)
  1069)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1070) 
  1071) 
  1072)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1073)       !    This is a fix for when two cohorts with very very low LAI are fused             !
  1074)       ! it prevents numerical errors (RGK 8-18-2014).                                      !
  1075)       ! (MLO 11-24-2014): turned rlai and dlai relative weights, so it works in all cases. !
  1076)       ! Also, applied the same idea to WAI-dependent variables.                            !
  1077)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1078)       if (cpatch%lai(recc) + cpatch%lai(donc) > 0 ) then
  1079)          rlai    = cpatch%lai(recc) / ( cpatch%lai(recc) + cpatch%lai(donc) )
  1080)          dlai    = 1.0 - rlai
  1081)       else
  1082)          rlai    = 0.5
  1083)          dlai    = 0.5
  1084)       end if
  1085)       if (cpatch%wai(recc) + cpatch%wai(donc) > 0 ) then
  1086)          rwai    = cpatch%wai(recc) / ( cpatch%wai(recc) + cpatch%wai(donc) )
  1087)          dwai    = 1.0 - rwai
  1088)       else
  1089)          rwai    = 0.5
  1090)          dwai    = 0.5
  1091)       end if
  1092)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1093) 
  1094) 
  1095) 
  1096) 
  1097)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1098)       !      Find DBH and height.  Make sure that carbon is conserved.                     !
  1099)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1100)       if (is_grass(cpatch%pft(donc)) .and. igrass == 1) then
  1101)           !----- New grass scheme, use bleaf then find DBH and height. --------------------!
  1102)           cpatch%bleaf(recc) = cpatch%bleaf(recc) * rnplant + cpatch%bleaf(donc) * dnplant
  1103)           cpatch%dbh(recc)   = bl2dbh(cpatch%bleaf(recc), cpatch%pft(recc))
  1104)           cpatch%hite(recc)  = bl2h  (cpatch%bleaf(recc), cpatch%pft(recc))
  1105)           !--------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1106)       else
  1107)           !----- Trees, or old grass scheme.  Use bdead then find DBH and height. ---------!
  1108)           cpatch%bdead(recc) = cpatch%bdead(recc) * rnplant + cpatch%bdead(donc) * dnplant
  1109)           cpatch%dbh(recc)   = bd2dbh(cpatch%pft(recc), cpatch%bdead(recc))
  1110)           cpatch%hite(recc)  = dbh2h(cpatch%pft(recc),  cpatch%dbh(recc))
  1111)           !--------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1112)       end if
  1113)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1114) 
  1115) 
  1116) 
  1117)       !----- Rooting depth. ---------------------------------------------------------------!
  1118)       cpatch%krdepth(recc) = dbh2krdepth(cpatch%hite(recc),cpatch%dbh(recc)                &
  1119)                                         ,cpatch%pft(recc),lsl)
  1120)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1121) 
  1122) 
  1123) 
  1124) 
  1125) 
  1126)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1127)       !     Conserving carbon to get balive, bleaf, and bstorage.                          !
  1128)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1129)       cpatch%balive           (recc) = cpatch%balive          (recc) * rnplant             &
  1130)                                      + cpatch%balive          (donc) * dnplant
  1131)       cpatch%broot            (recc) = cpatch%broot           (recc) * rnplant             &
  1132)                                      + cpatch%broot           (donc) * dnplant
  1133)       cpatch%bsapwooda        (recc) = cpatch%bsapwooda       (recc) * rnplant             &
  1134)                                      + cpatch%bsapwooda       (donc) * dnplant
  1135)       cpatch%bsapwoodb        (recc) = cpatch%bsapwoodb       (recc) * rnplant             &
  1136)                                      + cpatch%bsapwoodb       (donc) * dnplant
  1137)       cpatch%bstorage         (recc) = cpatch%bstorage        (recc) * rnplant             &
  1138)                                      + cpatch%bstorage        (donc) * dnplant
  1139)       cpatch%bseeds           (recc) = cpatch%bseeds          (recc) * rnplant             &
  1140)                                      + cpatch%bseeds          (donc) * dnplant
  1141)       cpatch%leaf_maintenance (recc) = cpatch%leaf_maintenance(recc) * rnplant             &
  1142)                                      + cpatch%leaf_maintenance(donc) * dnplant
  1143)       cpatch%root_maintenance (recc) = cpatch%root_maintenance(recc) * rnplant             &
  1144)                                      + cpatch%root_maintenance(donc) * dnplant
  1145)       cpatch%leaf_drop        (recc) = cpatch%leaf_drop       (recc) * rnplant             &
  1146)                                      + cpatch%leaf_drop       (donc) * dnplant
  1147)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1148) 
  1149) 
  1150) 
  1151)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1152)       !    Bleaf must be zero if phenology status is 2.  This is probably done correctly   !
  1153)       ! throughout the code, but being safe here.                                          !
  1154)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1155)       if (cpatch%phenology_status(recc) /= -2) then
  1156)          cpatch%bleaf(recc)  = rnplant * cpatch%bleaf(recc) + dnplant * cpatch%bleaf(donc)
  1157)       else
  1158)          cpatch%bleaf(recc)  = 0.
  1159)       end if
  1160)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1161) 
  1162) 
  1163) 
  1164)       !------ Energy, water, and heat capacity are extensive, add them. -------------------!
  1165)       cpatch%leaf_energy(recc) = cpatch%leaf_energy(recc) + cpatch%leaf_energy(donc)
  1166)       cpatch%leaf_water (recc) = cpatch%leaf_water (recc) + cpatch%leaf_water (donc)
  1167)       cpatch%leaf_hcap  (recc) = cpatch%leaf_hcap  (recc) + cpatch%leaf_hcap  (donc)
  1168)       cpatch%wood_energy(recc) = cpatch%wood_energy(recc) + cpatch%wood_energy(donc)
  1169)       cpatch%wood_water (recc) = cpatch%wood_water (recc) + cpatch%wood_water (donc)
  1170)       cpatch%wood_hcap  (recc) = cpatch%wood_hcap  (recc) + cpatch%wood_hcap  (donc)
  1171)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1172) 
  1173) 
  1174) 
  1175) 
  1176)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1177)       !      We update temperature and liquid water fraction.  We check whether the heat   !
  1178)       ! capacity is non-zero.  If it is a normal number, use the standard thermodynamic    !
  1179)       ! library, otherwise, average temperature, this is probably a blend of tiny cohorts  !
  1180)       ! that couldn't be solved, or the wood is not solved.                                !
  1181)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1182)       if ( cpatch%leaf_hcap(recc) > 0. ) then
  1183)          !----- Update temperature using the standard thermodynamics. ---------------------!
  1184)          call uextcm2tl(cpatch%leaf_energy(recc),cpatch%leaf_water(recc)                   &
  1185)                        ,cpatch%leaf_hcap(recc),cpatch%leaf_temp(recc)                      &
  1186)                        ,cpatch%leaf_fliq(recc))
  1187)          
  1188)          
  1189)       else 
  1190)          !----- Leaf temperature cannot be found using uextcm2tl, this is a singularity. --!
  1191)          cpatch%leaf_temp(recc)  = cpatch%leaf_temp(recc) * rnplant                        &
  1192)                                  + cpatch%leaf_temp(donc) * dnplant
  1193)          cpatch%leaf_fliq(recc)  = 0.0
  1194)       end if
  1195) 
  1196) 
  1197)       if ( cpatch%wood_hcap(recc) > 0. ) then
  1198)          !----- Update temperature using the standard thermodynamics. ---------------------!
  1199)          call uextcm2tl(cpatch%wood_energy(recc),cpatch%wood_water(recc)                   &
  1200)                        ,cpatch%wood_hcap(recc),cpatch%wood_temp(recc)                      &
  1201)                        ,cpatch%wood_fliq(recc))
  1202)       else 
  1203)          !----- Wood temperature cannot be found using uextcm2tl, this is a singularity. --!
  1204)          cpatch%wood_temp(recc)  = cpatch%wood_temp(recc) * rnplant                        &
  1205)                                  + cpatch%wood_temp(donc)  * dnplant
  1206)          cpatch%wood_fliq(recc)  = 0.0
  1207)       end if
  1208)       
  1209)       !----- Set time-steps temperatures as the current. ----------------------------------!
  1210)       cpatch%leaf_temp_pv(recc) = cpatch%leaf_temp(recc)
  1211)       cpatch%wood_temp_pv(recc) = cpatch%wood_temp(recc)
  1212)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1213) 
  1214)       !------ Find the intercellular value assuming saturation. ---------------------------!
  1215)       cpatch%lint_shv(recc) = qslif(can_prss,cpatch%leaf_temp(recc))
