  1216)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1217) 
  1218)       !------ Find the vapour pressure deficit. -------------------------------------------!
  1219)       cpatch%leaf_vpdef(recc) = vpdefil(can_prss,cpatch%leaf_temp(recc),can_shv,.true.)
  1220)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1221) 
  1222) 
  1223)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1224)       !     CB and CB_Xmax are scaled by population, as they are in kgC/plant/yr.          !
  1225)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1226)       ! RK: I think the below comment is no longer true. Per gh-24 reverting again to      !
  1227)       ! calculate CBR from running means of CB and CB_Xmax. 
  1228)       ! "The relative carbon balance, however, is no longer derived from the annual values !
  1229)       ! of CB, CB_LightMax, and CB_MoistMax, but tracked independently as it used to be    !
  1230)       ! done in ED-1.0."                                                                   !
  1231)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1232)       do imon = 1,13
  1233)          cpatch%cb         (imon,recc) = cpatch%cb          (imon,recc) * rnplant          &
  1234)                                        + cpatch%cb          (imon,donc) * dnplant
  1235)          cpatch%cb_lightmax(imon,recc) = cpatch%cb_lightmax (imon,recc) * rnplant          &
  1236)                                        + cpatch%cb_lightmax (imon,donc) * dnplant
  1237)          cpatch%cb_moistmax(imon,recc) = cpatch%cb_moistmax (imon,recc) * rnplant          &
  1238)                                        + cpatch%cb_moistmax (imon,donc) * dnplant
  1239)          cpatch%cb_mlmax   (imon,recc) = cpatch%cb_mlmax    (imon,recc) * rnplant          &
  1240)                                        + cpatch%cb_mlmax    (imon,donc) * dnplant
  1241)       end do
  1242)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1243) 
  1244) 
  1245) 
  1246)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1247)       !     Relative carbon balance is also averaged between the cohorts, to avoid wild    !
  1248)       ! oscillations in mortality when cohorts are fused.  This is the original method     !
  1249)       ! used in ED-1.0.                                                                    !
  1250)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1251)       cpatch%cbr_bar(recc) = cpatch%cbr_bar(recc) * rnplant + cpatch%cbr_bar(donc) * dnplant
  1252)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1253) 
  1254) 
  1255) 
  1256)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1257)       !    Today variables are extensive.                                                  !
  1258)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1259)       cpatch%today_gpp          (recc) = cpatch%today_gpp          (recc)                  &
  1260)                                        + cpatch%today_gpp          (donc)
  1261)                                   
  1262)       cpatch%today_nppleaf      (recc) = cpatch%today_nppleaf      (recc)                  &
  1263)                                        + cpatch%today_nppleaf      (donc)
  1264)                                   
  1265)       cpatch%today_nppfroot     (recc) = cpatch%today_nppfroot     (recc)                  &
  1266)                                        + cpatch%today_nppfroot     (donc)
  1267)                                   
  1268)       cpatch%today_nppsapwood   (recc) = cpatch%today_nppsapwood   (recc)                  &
  1269)                                        + cpatch%today_nppsapwood   (donc)
  1270)                                   
  1271)       cpatch%today_nppcroot     (recc) = cpatch%today_nppcroot     (recc)                  &
  1272)                                        + cpatch%today_nppcroot     (donc)
  1273)                                   
  1274)       cpatch%today_nppseeds     (recc) = cpatch%today_nppseeds     (recc)                  &
  1275)                                        + cpatch%today_nppseeds     (donc)
  1276)                                   
  1277)       cpatch%today_nppwood      (recc) = cpatch%today_nppwood      (recc)                  &
  1278)                                        + cpatch%today_nppwood      (donc)
  1279)                                   
  1280)       cpatch%today_nppdaily     (recc) = cpatch%today_nppdaily     (recc)                  &
  1281)                                        + cpatch%today_nppdaily     (donc)
  1282)                                   
  1283)       cpatch%today_gpp_pot      (recc) = cpatch%today_gpp_pot      (recc)                  &
  1284)                                        + cpatch%today_gpp_pot      (donc)
  1285) 
  1286)       cpatch%today_gpp_lightmax (recc) = cpatch%today_gpp_lightmax (recc)                  &
  1287)                                        + cpatch%today_gpp_lightmax (donc)
  1288) 
  1289)       cpatch%today_gpp_moistmax (recc) = cpatch%today_gpp_moistmax (recc)                  &
  1290)                                        + cpatch%today_gpp_moistmax (donc)
  1291) 
  1292)       cpatch%today_gpp_mlmax    (recc) = cpatch%today_gpp_mlmax    (recc)                  &
  1293)                                        + cpatch%today_gpp_mlmax    (donc)
  1294) 
  1295)       cpatch%today_leaf_resp    (recc) = cpatch%today_leaf_resp    (recc)                  &
  1296)                                        + cpatch%today_leaf_resp    (donc)
  1297) 
  1298)       cpatch%today_root_resp    (recc) = cpatch%today_root_resp    (recc)                  &
  1299)                                        + cpatch%today_root_resp    (donc)
  1300)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1301) 
  1302) 
  1303)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1304)       !    Fuse the leaf surface and intenal properties.  Since they are intensive         !
  1305)       ! properties, they are scaled by the number of plants.  These numbers are diagnostic !
  1306)       ! and this should be used for the output only.                                       !
  1307)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1308)       cpatch%lsfc_shv_open  (recc) = cpatch%lsfc_shv_open  (recc)  * rlai                  &
  1309)                                    + cpatch%lsfc_shv_open  (donc)  * dlai
  1310)       cpatch%lsfc_shv_closed(recc) = cpatch%lsfc_shv_closed(recc)  * rlai                  &
  1311)                                    + cpatch%lsfc_shv_closed(donc)  * dlai
  1312)       cpatch%lsfc_co2_open  (recc) = cpatch%lsfc_co2_open  (recc)  * rlai                  &
  1313)                                    + cpatch%lsfc_co2_open  (donc)  * dlai
  1314)       cpatch%lsfc_co2_closed(recc) = cpatch%lsfc_co2_closed(recc)  * rlai                  &
  1315)                                    + cpatch%lsfc_co2_closed(donc)  * dlai
  1316)       cpatch%lint_co2_open  (recc) = cpatch%lint_co2_open  (recc)  * rlai                  &
  1317)                                    + cpatch%lint_co2_open  (donc)  * dlai
  1318)       cpatch%lint_co2_closed(recc) = cpatch%lint_co2_closed(recc)  * rlai                  &
  1319)                                    + cpatch%lint_co2_closed(donc)  * dlai
  1320)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1321) 
  1322) 
  1323) 
  1324)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1325)       !    Fuse mortality rates.  By definition, mortality rate M for is given by:         !
  1326)       !                                                                                    !
  1327)       !                                    ln(A) - ln(N)                                   !
  1328)       !                               m = ---------------                                  !
  1329)       !                                          dt                                        !
  1330)       !                                                                                    !
  1331)       ! where A is the population that was previously alive, and N is the population that  !
  1332)       ! survived the mortality.  The cohorts represent a group of individuals with the     !
  1333)       ! same size and PFT, so they don't mix new recruits and old plants. Therefore, we    !
  1334)       ! can assume that N is actually nplant.  We don't know A, if the mortality rate is   !
  1335)       ! assumed constant during the interval dt, A = N * exp(m dt).                        !
  1336)       !                                                                                    !
  1337)       ! For fusion we don't really care about dt, so any number will do as long as it is   !
  1338)       ! the same for both cohorts.  With these assumptions, the mortality rate for the     !
  1339)       ! fused cohort mf is:                                                                !
  1340)       !                                                                                    !
  1341)       !  mf   =  ln (Ad+Ar) - ln(Nd+Nr) = ln[Nd*exp(md) + Nr*exp(mr)] - ln[Nd+Nr]          !
  1342)       !                                                                                    !
  1343)       !             / Nd*exp(md) + Nr*exp(mr) \                                            !
  1344)       !  mf   =  ln |-------------------------|                                            !
  1345)       !             \        Nd + Nr          /                                            !
  1346)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1347)       do imty=1,n_mort
  1348)          exp_mort_donc = exp(max(lnexp_min,min(lnexp_max,cpatch%mort_rate(imty,donc))))
  1349)          exp_mort_recc = exp(max(lnexp_min,min(lnexp_max,cpatch%mort_rate(imty,recc))))
  1350) 
  1351)          cpatch%mort_rate(imty,recc) = log( rnplant * exp_mort_recc                        &
  1352)                                           + dnplant * exp_mort_donc )
  1353)       end do
  1354)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1355) 
  1356) 
  1357) 
  1358)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1359)       !    Light level.  Using the intensive way of fusing.                                !
  1360)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1361)       cpatch%light_level     (recc) = cpatch%light_level      (recc) * rnplant             &
  1362)                                     + cpatch%light_level      (donc) * dnplant
  1363)       cpatch%light_level_beam(recc) = cpatch%light_level_beam (recc) * rnplant             &
  1364)                                     + cpatch%light_level_beam (donc) * dnplant
  1365)       cpatch%light_level_diff(recc) = cpatch%light_level_diff (recc) * rnplant             &
  1366)                                     + cpatch%light_level_diff (donc) * dnplant
  1367)       cpatch%par_level_beam  (recc) = cpatch%par_level_beam   (recc) * rnplant             &
  1368)                                     + cpatch%par_level_beam   (donc) * dnplant
  1369)       cpatch%par_level_diffd (recc) = cpatch%par_level_diffd  (recc) * rnplant             &
  1370)                                     + cpatch%par_level_diffd  (donc) * dnplant
  1371)       cpatch%par_level_diffu (recc) = cpatch%par_level_diffu  (recc) * rnplant             &
  1372)                                     + cpatch%par_level_diffu  (donc) * dnplant
  1373)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1374) 
  1375) 
  1376) 
  1377)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1378)       !    Long-trm respiration terms are in kgC/plant/yr, use nplant to fuse them.        !
  1379)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1380)       cpatch%leaf_growth_resp   (recc) = cpatch%leaf_growth_resp   (recc) * rnplant        &
  1381)                                        + cpatch%leaf_growth_resp   (donc) * dnplant
  1382)       cpatch%root_growth_resp   (recc) = cpatch%root_growth_resp   (recc) * rnplant        &
  1383)                                        + cpatch%root_growth_resp   (donc) * dnplant
  1384)       cpatch%sapa_growth_resp   (recc) = cpatch%sapa_growth_resp   (recc) * rnplant        &
  1385)                                        + cpatch%sapa_growth_resp   (donc) * dnplant
  1386)       cpatch%sapb_growth_resp   (recc) = cpatch%sapb_growth_resp   (recc) * rnplant        &
  1387)                                        + cpatch%sapb_growth_resp   (donc) * dnplant
  1388)       cpatch%leaf_storage_resp  (recc) = cpatch%leaf_storage_resp  (recc) * rnplant        &
  1389)                                        + cpatch%leaf_storage_resp  (donc) * dnplant
  1390)       cpatch%root_storage_resp  (recc) = cpatch%root_storage_resp  (recc) * rnplant        &
  1391)                                        + cpatch%root_storage_resp  (donc) * dnplant
  1392)       cpatch%sapa_storage_resp  (recc) = cpatch%sapa_storage_resp  (recc) * rnplant        &
  1393)                                        + cpatch%sapa_storage_resp  (donc) * dnplant
  1394)       cpatch%sapb_storage_resp  (recc) = cpatch%sapb_storage_resp  (recc) * rnplant        &
  1395)                                        + cpatch%sapb_storage_resp  (donc) * dnplant
  1396)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1397) 
  1398) 
  1399) 
  1400) 
  1401)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1402)       !    Water demand is in kg/m2_leaf/s, so we scale them by LAI.  Water supply is in   !
  1403)       ! kg/m2_ground/s, so we just add them.                                               !
  1404)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1405)       cpatch%psi_open    (recc) = cpatch%psi_open  (recc) * rlai                           &
  1406)                                 + cpatch%psi_open  (donc) * dlai
  1407)       cpatch%psi_closed  (recc) = cpatch%psi_closed(recc) * rlai                           &
  1408)                                 + cpatch%psi_closed(donc) * dlai
  1409)       cpatch%water_supply(recc) = cpatch%water_supply(recc) + cpatch%water_supply(donc)
  1410)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1411) 
  1412) 
  1413)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1414)       !    Carbon demand is in kg_C/m2_leaf/s, so we scale them by LAI.  FSW and FSN are   !
  1415)       ! really related to leaves, so we scale them by LAI.                                 !
  1416)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1417)       cpatch%A_open  (recc)     = cpatch%A_open  (recc) * rlai                             &
  1418)                                 + cpatch%A_open  (donc) * dlai
  1419)       cpatch%A_closed(recc)     = cpatch%A_closed(recc) * rlai                             &
  1420)                                 + cpatch%A_closed(donc) * dlai
  1421)       cpatch%A_light (recc)     = cpatch%A_light (donc) * rlai                             &
  1422)                                 + cpatch%A_light (recc) * dlai
  1423)       cpatch%A_rubp  (recc)     = cpatch%A_rubp  (donc) * rlai                             &
  1424)                                 + cpatch%A_rubp  (recc) * dlai
  1425)       cpatch%A_co2   (recc)     = cpatch%A_co2   (donc) * rlai                             &
  1426)                                 + cpatch%A_co2   (recc) * dlai
  1427)       cpatch%fsw     (recc)     = cpatch%fsw     (recc) * rlai                             &
  1428)                                 + cpatch%fsw     (donc) * dlai
  1429)       cpatch%fsn     (recc)     = cpatch%fsn     (recc) * rlai                             &
  1430)                                 + cpatch%fsn     (donc) * dlai
  1431)       cpatch%fs_open (recc)     = cpatch%fsw(recc) * cpatch%fsn(recc)
  1432)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1433) 
  1434) 
  1435) 
  1436)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1437)       !    Merge biomass and basal area.  Contrary to the patch/site/polygon levels,       !
  1438)       ! these variables are "intensive" (or per plant) at the cohort level, so we must     !
  1439)       ! average them.                                                                      !
  1440)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1441)       cpatch%agb      (recc) = cpatch%agb      (recc) * rnplant                            &
  1442)                              + cpatch%agb      (donc) * dnplant
  1443)       cpatch%basarea  (recc) = cpatch%basarea  (recc) * rnplant                            &
  1444)                              + cpatch%basarea  (donc) * dnplant
  1445)       cpatch%dagb_dt  (recc) = cpatch%dagb_dt  (recc) * rnplant                            &
  1446)                              + cpatch%dagb_dt  (donc) * dnplant
  1447)       cpatch%dba_dt   (recc) = cpatch%dba_dt   (recc) * rnplant                            &
  1448)                              + cpatch%dba_dt   (donc) * dnplant
  1449)       cpatch%dlndbh_dt(recc) = cpatch%dlndbh_dt(recc) * rnplant                            &
  1450)                              + cpatch%dlndbh_dt(donc) * dnplant
  1451)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1452) 
  1453) 
  1454) 
  1455)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1456)       !     Updating the tendency of plant density and the relative mortality rate.  The   !
  1457)       ! first is extensive (i.e. per unit of area), so it must be added, not scaled.  The  !
  1458)       ! second is intensive so it must be scaled.                                          !
  1459)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1460)       cpatch%monthly_dndt  (recc) = cpatch%monthly_dndt  (recc)                            &
  1461)                                   + cpatch%monthly_dndt  (donc)
  1462)       cpatch%monthly_dlnndt(recc) = cpatch%monthly_dlnndt(recc) * rnplant                  &
  1463)                                   + cpatch%monthly_dlnndt(donc) * dnplant
  1464)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1465) 
  1466) 
  1467) 
  1468)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1469)       !     Update the carbon fluxes. They are fluxes per unit of area, so they should be  !
  1470)       ! added, not scaled.                                                                 !
  1471)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1472)       cpatch%gpp             (recc) = cpatch%gpp             (recc)                        &
  1473)                                     + cpatch%gpp             (donc)
  1474)       cpatch%leaf_respiration(recc) = cpatch%leaf_respiration(recc)                        &
  1475)                                     + cpatch%leaf_respiration(donc)
  1476)       cpatch%root_respiration(recc) = cpatch%root_respiration(recc)                        &
  1477)                                     + cpatch%root_respiration(donc)
  1478)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1479) 
  1480) 
  1481)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1482)       !     Potential available water and elongation factor can be consider "intensive"    !
  1483)       ! variable water.                                                                    !
  1484)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1485)       cpatch%paw_avg(recc) = cpatch%paw_avg(recc) * rnplant + cpatch%paw_avg(donc) * dnplant
  1486)       cpatch%elongf (recc) = cpatch%elongf(recc)  * rnplant + cpatch%elongf (donc) * dnplant
  1487)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1488) 
  1489) 
  1490)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1491)       !    Light-phenology characteristics (MLO I am not sure if they should be scaled by  !
  1492)       ! nplant or LAI, it seems LAI would make more sense...).                             !
  1493)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1494)       cpatch%turnover_amp(recc) = cpatch%turnover_amp(recc) * rnplant                      &
  1495)                                 + cpatch%turnover_amp(donc) * dnplant
  1496)       cpatch%llspan      (recc) = cpatch%llspan      (recc) * rnplant                      &
  1497)                                 + cpatch%llspan      (donc) * dnplant
  1498)       cpatch%vm_bar      (recc) = cpatch%vm_bar      (recc) * rnplant                      &
  1499)                                 + cpatch%vm_bar      (donc) * dnplant
  1500)       cpatch%sla         (recc) = cpatch%sla         (recc) * rnplant                      &
  1501)                                 + cpatch%sla         (donc) * dnplant
  1502)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1503) 
  1504) 
  1505) 
  1506)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1507)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1508)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1509)       !    Fast averages.                                                                  !
  1510)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1511)       if (.not. fuse_initial) then
  1512)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1513)          !    Intensive variables, scaled by plant density.                                !
  1514)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1515)          cpatch%fmean_gpp             (recc) = cpatch%fmean_gpp             (recc)         &
  1516)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  1517)                                              + cpatch%fmean_gpp             (donc)         &
  1518)                                              * dnplant
  1519)          cpatch%fmean_npp             (recc) = cpatch%fmean_npp             (recc)         &
  1520)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  1521)                                              + cpatch%fmean_npp             (donc)         &
  1522)                                              * dnplant
  1523)          cpatch%fmean_leaf_resp       (recc) = cpatch%fmean_leaf_resp       (recc)         &
  1524)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  1525)                                              + cpatch%fmean_leaf_resp       (donc)         &
  1526)                                              * dnplant
  1527)          cpatch%fmean_root_resp       (recc) = cpatch%fmean_root_resp       (recc)         &
  1528)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  1529)                                              + cpatch%fmean_root_resp       (donc)         &
  1530)                                              * dnplant
  1531)          cpatch%fmean_leaf_growth_resp(recc) = cpatch%fmean_leaf_growth_resp(recc)         &
  1532)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  1533)                                              + cpatch%fmean_leaf_growth_resp(donc)         &
  1534)                                              * dnplant
  1535)          cpatch%fmean_root_growth_resp(recc) = cpatch%fmean_root_growth_resp(recc)         &
  1536)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  1537)                                              + cpatch%fmean_root_growth_resp(donc)         &
  1538)                                              * dnplant
  1539)          cpatch%fmean_sapa_growth_resp(recc) = cpatch%fmean_sapa_growth_resp(recc)         &
  1540)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  1541)                                              + cpatch%fmean_sapa_growth_resp(donc)         &
  1542)                                              * dnplant
  1543)          cpatch%fmean_sapb_growth_resp(recc) = cpatch%fmean_sapb_growth_resp(recc)         &
  1544)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  1545)                                              + cpatch%fmean_sapb_growth_resp(donc)         &
  1546)                                              * dnplant
  1547)          cpatch%fmean_leaf_storage_resp(recc)= cpatch%fmean_leaf_storage_resp(recc)        &
  1548)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  1549)                                              + cpatch%fmean_leaf_storage_resp(donc)        &
  1550)                                              * dnplant
  1551)          cpatch%fmean_root_storage_resp(recc)= cpatch%fmean_root_storage_resp(recc)        &
  1552)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  1553)                                              + cpatch%fmean_root_storage_resp(donc)        &
  1554)                                              * dnplant
  1555)          cpatch%fmean_sapa_storage_resp(recc)= cpatch%fmean_sapa_storage_resp(recc)        &
  1556)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  1557)                                              + cpatch%fmean_sapa_storage_resp(donc)        &
  1558)                                              * dnplant
  1559)          cpatch%fmean_sapb_storage_resp(recc)= cpatch%fmean_sapb_storage_resp(recc)        &
  1560)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  1561)                                              + cpatch%fmean_sapb_storage_resp(donc)        &
  1562)                                              * dnplant
  1563)          cpatch%fmean_plresp          (recc) = cpatch%fmean_plresp          (recc)         &
  1564)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  1565)                                              + cpatch%fmean_plresp          (donc)         &
  1566)                                              * dnplant
  1567)          cpatch%fmean_light_level     (recc) = cpatch%fmean_light_level     (recc)         &
  1568)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  1569)                                              + cpatch%fmean_light_level     (donc)         &
  1570)                                              * dnplant
  1571)          cpatch%fmean_light_level_beam(recc) = cpatch%fmean_light_level_beam(recc)         &
  1572)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  1573)                                              + cpatch%fmean_light_level_beam(donc)         &
  1574)                                              * dnplant
  1575)          cpatch%fmean_light_level_diff(recc) = cpatch%fmean_light_level_diff(recc)         &
  1576)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  1577)                                              + cpatch%fmean_light_level_diff(donc)         &
  1578)                                              * dnplant
  1579)          cpatch%fmean_par_level_beam  (recc) = cpatch%fmean_par_level_beam  (recc)         &
  1580)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  1581)                                              + cpatch%fmean_par_level_beam  (donc)         &
  1582)                                              * dnplant
  1583)          cpatch%fmean_par_level_diffd (recc) = cpatch%fmean_par_level_diffd (recc)         &
  1584)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  1585)                                              + cpatch%fmean_par_level_diffd (donc)         &
  1586)                                              * dnplant
  1587)          cpatch%fmean_par_level_diffu (recc) = cpatch%fmean_par_level_diffu (recc)         &
  1588)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  1589)                                              + cpatch%fmean_par_level_diffu (donc)         &
  1590)                                              * dnplant
  1591)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1592) 
  1593) 
  1594) 
  1595) 
  1596)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1597)          !    Intensive variables, scaled by LAI.                                          !
  1598)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1599)          cpatch%fmean_leaf_gsw        (recc) = cpatch%fmean_leaf_gsw        (recc) * rlai  &
  1600)                                              + cpatch%fmean_leaf_gsw        (donc) * dlai
  1601)          cpatch%fmean_leaf_gbw        (recc) = cpatch%fmean_leaf_gbw        (recc) * rlai  &
  1602)                                              + cpatch%fmean_leaf_gbw        (donc) * dlai
  1603)          cpatch%fmean_fs_open         (recc) = cpatch%fmean_fs_open         (recc) * rlai  &
  1604)                                              + cpatch%fmean_fs_open         (donc) * dlai
  1605)          cpatch%fmean_fsw             (recc) = cpatch%fmean_fsw             (recc) * rlai  &
  1606)                                              + cpatch%fmean_fsw             (donc) * dlai
  1607)          cpatch%fmean_fsn             (recc) = cpatch%fmean_fsn             (recc) * rlai  &
  1608)                                              + cpatch%fmean_fsn             (donc) * dlai
  1609)          cpatch%fmean_A_open          (recc) = cpatch%fmean_A_open          (recc) * rlai  &
  1610)                                              + cpatch%fmean_A_open          (donc) * dlai
  1611)          cpatch%fmean_A_closed        (recc) = cpatch%fmean_A_closed        (recc) * rlai  &
  1612)                                              + cpatch%fmean_A_closed        (donc) * dlai
  1613)          cpatch%fmean_A_net           (recc) = cpatch%fmean_A_net           (recc) * rlai  &
  1614)                                              + cpatch%fmean_A_net           (donc) * dlai
  1615)          cpatch%fmean_A_light         (recc) = cpatch%fmean_A_light         (recc) * rlai  &
  1616)                                              + cpatch%fmean_A_light         (donc) * dlai
  1617)          cpatch%fmean_A_rubp          (recc) = cpatch%fmean_A_rubp          (recc) * rlai  &
  1618)                                              + cpatch%fmean_A_rubp          (donc) * dlai
  1619)          cpatch%fmean_A_co2           (recc) = cpatch%fmean_A_co2           (recc) * rlai  &
  1620)                                              + cpatch%fmean_A_co2           (donc) * dlai
  1621)          cpatch%fmean_psi_open        (recc) = cpatch%fmean_psi_open        (recc) * rlai  &
  1622)                                              + cpatch%fmean_psi_open        (donc) * dlai
  1623)          cpatch%fmean_psi_closed      (recc) = cpatch%fmean_psi_closed      (recc) * rlai  &
  1624)                                              + cpatch%fmean_psi_closed      (donc) * dlai
  1625)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1626) 
  1627) 
  1628) 
  1629) 
  1630)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1631)          !    Intensive variables, scaled by WAI.                                          !
  1632)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1633)          cpatch%fmean_wood_gbw        (recc) = cpatch%fmean_wood_gbw        (recc) * rwai  &
  1634)                                              + cpatch%fmean_wood_gbw        (donc) * dwai
  1635)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1636) 
  1637) 
  1638) 
  1639) 
  1640)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1641)          !    Extensive variables.                                                         !
  1642)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1643)          cpatch%fmean_leaf_energy     (recc) = cpatch%fmean_leaf_energy     (recc)         &
  1644)                                              + cpatch%fmean_leaf_energy     (donc)
  1645)          cpatch%fmean_leaf_water      (recc) = cpatch%fmean_leaf_water      (recc)         &
  1646)                                              + cpatch%fmean_leaf_water      (donc)
  1647)          cpatch%fmean_leaf_hcap       (recc) = cpatch%fmean_leaf_hcap       (recc)         &
  1648)                                              + cpatch%fmean_leaf_hcap       (donc)
  1649)          cpatch%fmean_wood_energy     (recc) = cpatch%fmean_wood_energy     (recc)         &
  1650)                                              + cpatch%fmean_wood_energy     (donc)
  1651)          cpatch%fmean_wood_water      (recc) = cpatch%fmean_wood_water      (recc)         &
  1652)                                              + cpatch%fmean_wood_water      (donc)
  1653)          cpatch%fmean_wood_hcap       (recc) = cpatch%fmean_wood_hcap       (recc)         &
  1654)                                              + cpatch%fmean_wood_hcap       (donc)
  1655)          cpatch%fmean_water_supply    (recc) = cpatch%fmean_water_supply    (recc)         &
  1656)                                              + cpatch%fmean_water_supply    (donc)
  1657)          cpatch%fmean_par_l           (recc) = cpatch%fmean_par_l           (recc)         &
  1658)                                              + cpatch%fmean_par_l           (donc)
  1659)          cpatch%fmean_par_l_beam      (recc) = cpatch%fmean_par_l_beam      (recc)         &
  1660)                                              + cpatch%fmean_par_l_beam      (donc)
  1661)          cpatch%fmean_par_l_diff      (recc) = cpatch%fmean_par_l_diff      (recc)         &
  1662)                                              + cpatch%fmean_par_l_diff      (donc)
  1663)          cpatch%fmean_rshort_l        (recc) = cpatch%fmean_rshort_l        (recc)         &
  1664)                                              + cpatch%fmean_rshort_l        (donc)
  1665)          cpatch%fmean_rlong_l         (recc) = cpatch%fmean_rlong_l         (recc)         &
  1666)                                              + cpatch%fmean_rlong_l         (donc)
  1667)          cpatch%fmean_sensible_lc     (recc) = cpatch%fmean_sensible_lc     (recc)         &
  1668)                                              + cpatch%fmean_sensible_lc     (donc)
  1669)          cpatch%fmean_vapor_lc        (recc) = cpatch%fmean_vapor_lc        (recc)         &
  1670)                                              + cpatch%fmean_vapor_lc        (donc)
  1671)          cpatch%fmean_transp          (recc) = cpatch%fmean_transp          (recc)         &
  1672)                                              + cpatch%fmean_transp          (donc)
  1673)          cpatch%fmean_intercepted_al  (recc) = cpatch%fmean_intercepted_al  (recc)         &
  1674)                                              + cpatch%fmean_intercepted_al  (donc)
  1675)          cpatch%fmean_wshed_lg        (recc) = cpatch%fmean_wshed_lg        (recc)         &
  1676)                                              + cpatch%fmean_wshed_lg        (donc)
  1677)          cpatch%fmean_rshort_w        (recc) = cpatch%fmean_rshort_w        (recc)         &
  1678)                                              + cpatch%fmean_rshort_w        (donc)
  1679)          cpatch%fmean_rlong_w         (recc) = cpatch%fmean_rlong_w         (recc)         &
  1680)                                              + cpatch%fmean_rlong_w         (donc)
  1681)          cpatch%fmean_rad_profile   (:,recc) = cpatch%fmean_rad_profile   (:,recc)         &
  1682)                                              + cpatch%fmean_rad_profile   (:,donc)
  1683)          cpatch%fmean_sensible_wc     (recc) = cpatch%fmean_sensible_wc     (recc)         &
  1684)                                              + cpatch%fmean_sensible_wc     (donc)
  1685)          cpatch%fmean_vapor_wc        (recc) = cpatch%fmean_vapor_wc        (recc)         &
  1686)                                              + cpatch%fmean_vapor_wc        (donc)
  1687)          cpatch%fmean_intercepted_aw  (recc) = cpatch%fmean_intercepted_aw  (recc)         &
  1688)                                              + cpatch%fmean_intercepted_aw  (donc)
  1689)          cpatch%fmean_wshed_wg        (recc) = cpatch%fmean_wshed_wg        (recc)         &
  1690)                                              + cpatch%fmean_wshed_wg        (donc)
  1691)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1692) 
  1693) 
  1694) 
  1695)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1696)          !      We update temperature and liquid water fraction.  We check whether the     !
  1697)          ! heat capacity is non-zero.  If it is a normal number, use the standard thermo-  !
  1698)          ! dynamic library, otherwise, average temperature, this is probably a blend of    !
  1699)          ! tiny cohorts that couldn't be solved, or the wood is not solved.                !
  1700)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1701)          !------ Leaf. --------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1702)          if ( cpatch%fmean_leaf_hcap(recc) > 0. ) then
  1703)             !----- Update temperature and liquid fraction using standard thermodynamics. --!
  1704)             call uextcm2tl(cpatch%fmean_leaf_energy(recc),cpatch%fmean_leaf_water(recc)    &
  1705)                           ,cpatch%fmean_leaf_hcap  (recc),cpatch%fmean_leaf_temp (recc)    &
  1706)                           ,cpatch%fmean_leaf_fliq  (recc))
  1707)             !------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1708) 
  1709) 
  1710)             !----- Scale vapour pressure deficit using LAI. -------------------------------!
  1711)             cpatch%fmean_leaf_vpdef   (recc) = cpatch%fmean_leaf_vpdef      (recc) * rlai  &
  1712)                                              + cpatch%fmean_leaf_vpdef      (donc) * dlai
  1713)             !------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1714)          else
  1715)             !----- None of the cohorts has leaf biomass use nplant to scale them. ---------!
  1716)             cpatch%fmean_leaf_temp (recc) = cpatch%fmean_leaf_temp (recc) * rnplant        &
  1717)                                           + cpatch%fmean_leaf_temp (donc) * dnplant
  1718)             cpatch%fmean_leaf_fliq (recc) = 0.0
  1719)             cpatch%fmean_leaf_vpdef(recc) = cpatch%fmean_leaf_vpdef(recc) * rnplant        &
  1720)                                           + cpatch%fmean_leaf_vpdef(donc) * dnplant
  1721)             !------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1722)          end if
  1723)          !------ Wood. --------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1724)          if ( cpatch%fmean_wood_hcap(recc) > 0. ) then
  1725)             !----- Update temperature using the standard thermodynamics. ------------------!
  1726)             call uextcm2tl(cpatch%fmean_wood_energy(recc),cpatch%fmean_wood_water(recc)    &
  1727)                           ,cpatch%fmean_wood_hcap  (recc),cpatch%fmean_wood_temp (recc)    &
  1728)                           ,cpatch%fmean_wood_fliq  (recc))
  1729)             !------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1730)          else                                                                              
  1731)             !----- Wood temperature can't be found using uextcm2tl (singularity). ---------!
  1732)             cpatch%fmean_wood_temp(recc) = cpatch%fmean_wood_temp(recc) * rnplant          &
  1733)                                          + cpatch%fmean_wood_temp(donc) * dnplant
  1734)             cpatch%fmean_wood_fliq(recc) = 0.0
  1735)             !------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1736)          end if
  1737)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1738)       end if
  1739)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1740) 
  1741) 
  1742) 
  1743) 
  1744)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1745)       !    Daily means.                                                                    !
  1746)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1747)       if (writing_long .and. (.not. fuse_initial)) then
  1748) 
  1749)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1750)          !    Intensive variables, scaled by plant density.                                !
  1751)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1752)          cpatch%dmean_nppleaf         (recc) = cpatch%dmean_nppleaf         (recc)         &
  1753)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  1754)                                              + cpatch%dmean_nppleaf         (donc)         &
  1755)                                              * dnplant
  1756)          cpatch%dmean_nppfroot        (recc) = cpatch%dmean_nppfroot        (recc)         &
  1757)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  1758)                                              + cpatch%dmean_nppfroot        (donc)         &
  1759)                                              * dnplant
  1760)          cpatch%dmean_nppsapwood      (recc) = cpatch%dmean_nppsapwood      (recc)         &
  1761)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  1762)                                              + cpatch%dmean_nppsapwood      (donc)         &
  1763)                                              * dnplant
  1764)          cpatch%dmean_nppcroot        (recc) = cpatch%dmean_nppcroot        (recc)         &
  1765)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  1766)                                              + cpatch%dmean_nppcroot        (donc)         &
  1767)                                              * dnplant
  1768)          cpatch%dmean_nppseeds        (recc) = cpatch%dmean_nppseeds        (recc)         &
  1769)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  1770)                                              + cpatch%dmean_nppseeds        (donc)         &
  1771)                                              * dnplant
  1772)          cpatch%dmean_nppwood         (recc) = cpatch%dmean_nppwood         (recc)         &
  1773)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  1774)                                              + cpatch%dmean_nppwood         (donc)         &
  1775)                                              * dnplant
  1776)          cpatch%dmean_nppdaily        (recc) = cpatch%dmean_nppdaily        (recc)         &
  1777)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  1778)                                              + cpatch%dmean_nppdaily        (donc)         &
  1779)                                              * dnplant
  1780)          cpatch%dmean_gpp             (recc) = cpatch%dmean_gpp             (recc)         &
  1781)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  1782)                                              + cpatch%dmean_gpp             (donc)         &
  1783)                                              * dnplant
  1784)          cpatch%dmean_npp             (recc) = cpatch%dmean_npp             (recc)         &
  1785)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  1786)                                              + cpatch%dmean_npp             (donc)         &
  1787)                                              * dnplant
  1788)          cpatch%dmean_leaf_resp       (recc) = cpatch%dmean_leaf_resp       (recc)         &
  1789)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  1790)                                              + cpatch%dmean_leaf_resp       (donc)         &
  1791)                                              * dnplant
  1792)          cpatch%dmean_root_resp       (recc) = cpatch%dmean_root_resp       (recc)         &
  1793)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  1794)                                              + cpatch%dmean_root_resp       (donc)         &
  1795)                                              * dnplant
  1796)          cpatch%dmean_leaf_growth_resp(recc) = cpatch%dmean_leaf_growth_resp(recc)         &
  1797)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  1798)                                              + cpatch%dmean_leaf_growth_resp(donc)         &
  1799)                                              * dnplant
  1800)          cpatch%dmean_root_growth_resp(recc) = cpatch%dmean_root_growth_resp(recc)         &
  1801)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  1802)                                              + cpatch%dmean_root_growth_resp(donc)         &
  1803)                                              * dnplant
  1804)          cpatch%dmean_sapa_growth_resp(recc) = cpatch%dmean_sapa_growth_resp(recc)         &
  1805)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  1806)                                              + cpatch%dmean_sapa_growth_resp(donc)         &
  1807)                                              * dnplant
  1808)          cpatch%dmean_sapb_growth_resp(recc) = cpatch%dmean_sapb_growth_resp(recc)         &
  1809)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  1810)                                              + cpatch%dmean_sapb_growth_resp(donc)         &
  1811)                                              * dnplant
  1812)          cpatch%dmean_leaf_storage_resp(recc)= cpatch%dmean_leaf_storage_resp(recc)        &
  1813)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  1814)                                              + cpatch%dmean_leaf_storage_resp(donc)        &
  1815)                                              * dnplant
  1816)          cpatch%dmean_root_storage_resp(recc)= cpatch%dmean_root_storage_resp(recc)        &
  1817)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  1818)                                              + cpatch%dmean_root_storage_resp(donc)        &
  1819)                                              * dnplant
  1820)          cpatch%dmean_sapa_storage_resp(recc)= cpatch%dmean_sapa_storage_resp(recc)        &
  1821)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  1822)                                              + cpatch%dmean_sapa_storage_resp(donc)        &
  1823)                                              * dnplant
  1824)          cpatch%dmean_sapb_storage_resp(recc)= cpatch%dmean_sapb_storage_resp(recc)        &
  1825)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  1826)                                              + cpatch%dmean_sapb_storage_resp(donc)        &
  1827)                                              * dnplant
  1828)          cpatch%dmean_plresp          (recc) = cpatch%dmean_plresp          (recc)         &
  1829)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  1830)                                              + cpatch%dmean_plresp          (donc)         &
  1831)                                              * dnplant
  1832)          cpatch%dmean_light_level     (recc) = cpatch%dmean_light_level     (recc)         &
  1833)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  1834)                                              + cpatch%dmean_light_level     (donc)         &
  1835)                                              * dnplant
  1836)          cpatch%dmean_light_level_beam(recc) = cpatch%dmean_light_level_beam(recc)         &
  1837)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  1838)                                              + cpatch%dmean_light_level_beam(donc)         &
  1839)                                              * dnplant
  1840)          cpatch%dmean_light_level_diff(recc) = cpatch%dmean_light_level_diff(recc)         &
  1841)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  1842)                                              + cpatch%dmean_light_level_diff(donc)         &
  1843)                                              * dnplant
  1844)          cpatch%dmean_par_level_beam  (recc) = cpatch%dmean_par_level_beam  (recc)         &
  1845)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  1846)                                              + cpatch%dmean_par_level_beam  (donc)         &
  1847)                                              * dnplant
  1848)          cpatch%dmean_par_level_diffd (recc) = cpatch%dmean_par_level_diffd (recc)         &
  1849)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  1850)                                              + cpatch%dmean_par_level_diffd (donc)         &
  1851)                                              * dnplant
  1852)          cpatch%dmean_par_level_diffu (recc) = cpatch%dmean_par_level_diffu (recc)         &
  1853)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  1854)                                              + cpatch%dmean_par_level_diffu (donc)         &
  1855)                                              * dnplant
  1856)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1857) 
  1858) 
  1859) 
  1860) 
  1861)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1862)          !    Intensive variables, scaled by LAI.                                          !
  1863)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1864)          cpatch%dmean_leaf_gsw        (recc) = cpatch%dmean_leaf_gsw        (recc) * rlai  &
  1865)                                              + cpatch%dmean_leaf_gsw        (donc) * dlai
  1866)          cpatch%dmean_leaf_gbw        (recc) = cpatch%dmean_leaf_gbw        (recc) * rlai  &
  1867)                                              + cpatch%dmean_leaf_gbw        (donc) * dlai
  1868)          cpatch%dmean_fs_open         (recc) = cpatch%dmean_fs_open         (recc) * rlai  &
  1869)                                              + cpatch%dmean_fs_open         (donc) * dlai
  1870)          cpatch%dmean_fsw             (recc) = cpatch%dmean_fsw             (recc) * rlai  &
  1871)                                              + cpatch%dmean_fsw             (donc) * dlai
  1872)          cpatch%dmean_fsn             (recc) = cpatch%dmean_fsn             (recc) * rlai  &
  1873)                                              + cpatch%dmean_fsn             (donc) * dlai
  1874)          cpatch%dmean_A_open          (recc) = cpatch%dmean_A_open          (recc) * rlai  &
  1875)                                              + cpatch%dmean_A_open          (donc) * dlai
  1876)          cpatch%dmean_A_closed        (recc) = cpatch%dmean_A_closed        (recc) * rlai  &
  1877)                                              + cpatch%dmean_A_closed        (donc) * dlai
  1878)          cpatch%dmean_A_net           (recc) = cpatch%dmean_A_net           (recc) * rlai  &
  1879)                                              + cpatch%dmean_A_net           (donc) * dlai
  1880)          cpatch%dmean_A_light         (recc) = cpatch%dmean_A_light         (recc) * rlai  &
  1881)                                              + cpatch%dmean_A_light         (donc) * dlai
  1882)          cpatch%dmean_A_rubp          (recc) = cpatch%dmean_A_rubp          (recc) * rlai  &
  1883)                                              + cpatch%dmean_A_rubp          (donc) * dlai
  1884)          cpatch%dmean_A_co2           (recc) = cpatch%dmean_A_co2           (recc) * rlai  &
  1885)                                              + cpatch%dmean_A_co2           (donc) * dlai
  1886)          cpatch%dmean_psi_open        (recc) = cpatch%dmean_psi_open        (recc) * rlai  &
  1887)                                              + cpatch%dmean_psi_open        (donc) * dlai
  1888)          cpatch%dmean_psi_closed      (recc) = cpatch%dmean_psi_closed      (recc) * rlai  &
  1889)                                              + cpatch%dmean_psi_closed      (donc) * dlai
  1890)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1891) 
  1892) 
  1893) 
  1894) 
  1895)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1896)          !    Intensive variables, scaled by WAI.                                          !
  1897)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1898)          cpatch%dmean_wood_gbw        (recc) = cpatch%dmean_wood_gbw        (recc) * rwai  &
  1899)                                              + cpatch%dmean_wood_gbw        (donc) * dwai
  1900)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1901) 
  1902) 
  1903) 
  1904) 
  1905)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1906)          !    Extensive variables.                                                         !
  1907)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1908)          cpatch%dmean_leaf_energy     (recc) = cpatch%dmean_leaf_energy     (recc)         &
  1909)                                              + cpatch%dmean_leaf_energy     (donc)
  1910)          cpatch%dmean_leaf_water      (recc) = cpatch%dmean_leaf_water      (recc)         &
  1911)                                              + cpatch%dmean_leaf_water      (donc)
  1912)          cpatch%dmean_leaf_hcap       (recc) = cpatch%dmean_leaf_hcap       (recc)         &
  1913)                                              + cpatch%dmean_leaf_hcap       (donc)
  1914)          cpatch%dmean_wood_energy     (recc) = cpatch%dmean_wood_energy     (recc)         &
  1915)                                              + cpatch%dmean_wood_energy     (donc)
  1916)          cpatch%dmean_wood_water      (recc) = cpatch%dmean_wood_water      (recc)         &
  1917)                                              + cpatch%dmean_wood_water      (donc)
  1918)          cpatch%dmean_wood_hcap       (recc) = cpatch%dmean_wood_hcap       (recc)         &
  1919)                                              + cpatch%dmean_wood_hcap       (donc)
  1920)          cpatch%dmean_water_supply    (recc) = cpatch%dmean_water_supply    (recc)         &
  1921)                                              + cpatch%dmean_water_supply    (donc)
  1922)          cpatch%dmean_par_l           (recc) = cpatch%dmean_par_l           (recc)         &
  1923)                                              + cpatch%dmean_par_l           (donc)
  1924)          cpatch%dmean_par_l_beam      (recc) = cpatch%dmean_par_l_beam      (recc)         &
  1925)                                              + cpatch%dmean_par_l_beam      (donc)
  1926)          cpatch%dmean_par_l_diff      (recc) = cpatch%dmean_par_l_diff      (recc)         &
  1927)                                              + cpatch%dmean_par_l_diff      (donc)
  1928)          cpatch%dmean_rshort_l        (recc) = cpatch%dmean_rshort_l        (recc)         &
  1929)                                              + cpatch%dmean_rshort_l        (donc)
  1930)          cpatch%dmean_rlong_l         (recc) = cpatch%dmean_rlong_l         (recc)         &
  1931)                                              + cpatch%dmean_rlong_l         (donc)
  1932)          cpatch%dmean_sensible_lc     (recc) = cpatch%dmean_sensible_lc     (recc)         &
  1933)                                              + cpatch%dmean_sensible_lc     (donc)
  1934)          cpatch%dmean_vapor_lc        (recc) = cpatch%dmean_vapor_lc        (recc)         &
  1935)                                              + cpatch%dmean_vapor_lc        (donc)
  1936)          cpatch%dmean_transp          (recc) = cpatch%dmean_transp          (recc)         &
  1937)                                              + cpatch%dmean_transp          (donc)
  1938)          cpatch%dmean_intercepted_al  (recc) = cpatch%dmean_intercepted_al  (recc)         &
  1939)                                              + cpatch%dmean_intercepted_al  (donc)
  1940)          cpatch%dmean_wshed_lg        (recc) = cpatch%dmean_wshed_lg        (recc)         &
  1941)                                              + cpatch%dmean_wshed_lg        (donc)
  1942)          cpatch%dmean_rshort_w        (recc) = cpatch%dmean_rshort_w        (recc)         &
  1943)                                              + cpatch%dmean_rshort_w        (donc)
  1944)          cpatch%dmean_rlong_w         (recc) = cpatch%dmean_rlong_w         (recc)         &
  1945)                                              + cpatch%dmean_rlong_w         (donc)
  1946)          cpatch%dmean_rad_profile   (:,recc) = cpatch%dmean_rad_profile   (:,recc)         &
  1947)                                              + cpatch%dmean_rad_profile   (:,donc)
  1948)          cpatch%dmean_sensible_wc     (recc) = cpatch%dmean_sensible_wc     (recc)         &
  1949)                                              + cpatch%dmean_sensible_wc     (donc)
  1950)          cpatch%dmean_vapor_wc        (recc) = cpatch%dmean_vapor_wc        (recc)         &
  1951)                                              + cpatch%dmean_vapor_wc        (donc)
  1952)          cpatch%dmean_intercepted_aw  (recc) = cpatch%dmean_intercepted_aw  (recc)         &
  1953)                                              + cpatch%dmean_intercepted_aw  (donc)
  1954)          cpatch%dmean_wshed_wg        (recc) = cpatch%dmean_wshed_wg        (recc)         &
  1955)                                              + cpatch%dmean_wshed_wg        (donc)
  1956)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1957) 
  1958) 
  1959) 
  1960)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1961)          !      We update temperature and liquid water fraction.  We check whether the     !
  1962)          ! heat capacity is non-zero.  If it is a normal number, use the standard thermo-  !
  1963)          ! dynamic library, otherwise, average temperature, this is probably a blend of    !
  1964)          ! tiny cohorts that couldn't be solved, or the wood is not solved.                !
  1965)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1966)          !------ Leaf. --------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1967)          if ( cpatch%dmean_leaf_hcap(recc) > 0. ) then
  1968)             !----- Update temperature and liquid fraction using standard thermodynamics. --!
  1969)             call uextcm2tl(cpatch%dmean_leaf_energy(recc),cpatch%dmean_leaf_water(recc)    &
  1970)                           ,cpatch%dmean_leaf_hcap  (recc),cpatch%dmean_leaf_temp (recc)    &
  1971)                           ,cpatch%dmean_leaf_fliq  (recc))                                                  
  1972)             !------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1973) 
  1974) 
  1975)             !----- Scale vapour pressure deficit using LAI. -------------------------------!
  1976)             cpatch%dmean_leaf_vpdef   (recc) = cpatch%dmean_leaf_vpdef      (recc) * rlai  &
  1977)                                              + cpatch%dmean_leaf_vpdef      (donc) * dlai
  1978)             !------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1979)          else
  1980)             !----- None of the cohorts has leaf biomass use nplant to scale them. ---------!
  1981)             cpatch%dmean_leaf_temp (recc) = cpatch%dmean_leaf_temp (recc) * rnplant        &
  1982)                                           + cpatch%dmean_leaf_temp (donc) * dnplant
  1983)             cpatch%dmean_leaf_fliq (recc) = 0.0
  1984)             cpatch%dmean_leaf_vpdef(recc) = cpatch%dmean_leaf_vpdef(recc) * rnplant        &
  1985)                                           + cpatch%dmean_leaf_vpdef(donc) * dnplant
  1986)             !------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1987)          end if                                                                            
  1988)          !------ Wood. --------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1989)          if ( cpatch%dmean_wood_hcap(recc) > 0. ) then                                     
  1990)             !----- Update temperature using the standard thermodynamics. ------------------!
  1991)             call uextcm2tl(cpatch%dmean_wood_energy(recc),cpatch%dmean_wood_water(recc)    &
  1992)                           ,cpatch%dmean_wood_hcap  (recc),cpatch%dmean_wood_temp (recc)    &
  1993)                           ,cpatch%dmean_wood_fliq  (recc))
  1994)             !------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  1995)          else                                                                              
  1996)             !----- Wood temperature can't be found using uextcm2tl (singularity). ---------!
  1997)             cpatch%dmean_wood_temp(recc) = cpatch%dmean_wood_temp(recc) * rnplant          &
  1998)                                          + cpatch%dmean_wood_temp(donc) * dnplant
  1999)             cpatch%dmean_wood_fliq(recc) = 0.0
  2000)             !------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2001)          end if
  2002)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2003)       end if
  2004)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2005) 
  2006) 
  2007) 
  2008) 
  2009)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2010)       !    Monthly means.                                                                  !
  2011)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2012)       if (writing_eorq .and. (.not. fuse_initial)) then
  2013)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2014)          !     First we merge the squares, as they require the means.                      !
  2015)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2016)          !----- Intensive. ----------------------------------------------------------------!
  2017)          cpatch%mmsqu_gpp        (recc) = fuse_msqu( cpatch%mmean_gpp        (recc)        &
  2018)                                                    , cpatch%mmsqu_gpp        (recc)        &
  2019)                                                    , rnplant                               &
  2020)                                                    , cpatch%mmean_gpp        (donc)        &
  2021)                                                    , cpatch%mmsqu_gpp        (donc)        &
  2022)                                                    , cpatch%nplant           (donc)        &
  2023)                                                    , corr_cohort, .false.)
  2024)          cpatch%mmsqu_npp        (recc) = fuse_msqu( cpatch%mmean_npp        (recc)        &
  2025)                                                    , cpatch%mmsqu_npp        (recc)        &
  2026)                                                    , rnplant                               &
  2027)                                                    , cpatch%mmean_npp        (donc)        &
  2028)                                                    , cpatch%mmsqu_npp        (donc)        &
  2029)                                                    , cpatch%nplant           (donc)        &
  2030)                                                    , corr_cohort, .false.)
  2031)          cpatch%mmsqu_plresp     (recc) = fuse_msqu( cpatch%mmean_plresp     (recc)        &
  2032)                                                    , cpatch%mmsqu_plresp     (recc)        &
  2033)                                                    , rnplant                               &
  2034)                                                    , cpatch%mmean_plresp     (donc)        &
  2035)                                                    , cpatch%mmsqu_plresp     (donc)        &
  2036)                                                    , dnplant                               &
  2037)                                                    , corr_cohort, .false.)
  2038)          !----- Extensive variables. ------------------------------------------------------!
  2039)          cpatch%mmsqu_sensible_lc(recc) = fuse_msqu( cpatch%mmean_sensible_lc(recc)        &
  2040)                                                    , cpatch%mmsqu_sensible_lc(recc)        &
  2041)                                                    , rnplant                               &
  2042)                                                    , cpatch%mmean_sensible_lc(donc)        &
  2043)                                                    , cpatch%mmsqu_sensible_lc(donc)        &
  2044)                                                    , dnplant                               &
  2045)                                                    , corr_cohort, .true. )
  2046)          cpatch%mmsqu_vapor_lc   (recc) = fuse_msqu( cpatch%mmean_vapor_lc   (recc)        &
  2047)                                                    , cpatch%mmsqu_vapor_lc   (recc)        &
  2048)                                                    , rnplant                               &
  2049)                                                    , cpatch%mmean_vapor_lc   (donc)        &
  2050)                                                    , cpatch%mmsqu_vapor_lc   (donc)        &
  2051)                                                    , dnplant                               &
  2052)                                                    , corr_cohort, .true. )
  2053)          cpatch%mmsqu_transp     (recc) = fuse_msqu( cpatch%mmean_transp     (recc)        &
  2054)                                                    , cpatch%mmsqu_transp     (recc)        &
  2055)                                                    , rnplant                               &
  2056)                                                    , cpatch%mmean_transp     (donc)        &
  2057)                                                    , cpatch%mmsqu_transp     (donc)        &
  2058)                                                    , dnplant                               &
  2059)                                                    , corr_cohort, .true. )
  2060)          cpatch%mmsqu_sensible_wc(recc) = fuse_msqu( cpatch%mmean_sensible_wc(recc)        &
  2061)                                                    , cpatch%mmsqu_sensible_wc(recc)        &
  2062)                                                    , rnplant                               &
  2063)                                                    , cpatch%mmean_sensible_wc(donc)        &
  2064)                                                    , cpatch%mmsqu_sensible_wc(donc)        &
  2065)                                                    , dnplant                               &
  2066)                                                    , corr_cohort, .true. )
  2067)          cpatch%mmsqu_vapor_wc   (recc) = fuse_msqu( cpatch%mmean_vapor_wc   (recc)        &
  2068)                                                    , cpatch%mmsqu_vapor_wc   (recc)        &
  2069)                                                    , rnplant                               &
  2070)                                                    , cpatch%mmean_vapor_wc   (donc)        &
  2071)                                                    , cpatch%mmsqu_vapor_wc   (donc)        &
  2072)                                                    , dnplant                               &
  2073)                                                    , corr_cohort, .true. )
  2074)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2075) 
  2076) 
  2077) 
  2078)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2079)          !    Intensive variables, scaled by plant density.                                !
  2080)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!

  2082)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  2083)                                              + cpatch%mmean_nppleaf         (donc)         &

  2092)                                              * dnplant

  2160)                                              * dnplant
  2161)          cpatch%mmean_light_level     (recc) = cpatch%mmean_light_level     (recc)         &

  2168)                                              * dnplant
  2169)          cpatch%mmean_light_level_diff(recc) = cpatch%mmean_light_level_diff(recc)         &
  2170)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  2171)                                              + cpatch%mmean_light_level_diff(donc)         &
  2172)                                              * dnplant
  2173)          cpatch%mmean_bleaf           (recc) = cpatch%mmean_bleaf           (recc)         &
  2174)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  2175)                                              + cpatch%mmean_bleaf           (donc)         &
  2176)                                              * dnplant
  2177)          cpatch%mmean_broot           (recc) = cpatch%mmean_broot           (recc)         &
  2178)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  2179)                                              + cpatch%mmean_broot           (donc)         &
  2180)                                              * dnplant

  2185)          cpatch%mmean_leaf_maintenance(recc) = cpatch%mmean_leaf_maintenance(recc)         &
  2186)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  2187)                                              + cpatch%mmean_leaf_maintenance(donc)         &
  2188)                                              * dnplant
  2189)          cpatch%mmean_root_maintenance(recc) = cpatch%mmean_root_maintenance(recc)         &
  2190)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  2191)                                              + cpatch%mmean_root_maintenance(donc)         &
  2192)                                              * dnplant
  2193)          cpatch%mmean_leaf_drop       (recc) = cpatch%mmean_leaf_drop       (recc)         &
  2194)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  2195)                                              + cpatch%mmean_leaf_drop       (donc)         &
  2196)                                              * dnplant
  2197)          cpatch%mmean_cb              (recc) = cpatch%mmean_cb              (recc)         &
  2198)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  2199)                                              + cpatch%mmean_cb              (donc)         &
  2200)                                              * dnplant
  2201)          cpatch%mmean_par_level_beam  (recc) = cpatch%mmean_par_level_beam  (recc)         &
  2202)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  2203)                                              + cpatch%mmean_par_level_beam  (donc)         &
  2204)                                              * dnplant
  2205)          cpatch%mmean_par_level_diffd (recc) = cpatch%mmean_par_level_diffd (recc)         &
  2206)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  2207)                                              + cpatch%mmean_par_level_diffd (donc)         &
  2208)                                              * dnplant
  2209)          cpatch%mmean_par_level_diffu (recc) = cpatch%mmean_par_level_diffu (recc)         &
  2210)                                              * rnplant                                     &
  2211)                                              + cpatch%mmean_par_level_diffu (donc)         &
  2212)                                              * dnplant
  2213)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2214) 
  2215) 
  2216) 
  2217) 
  2218)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2219)          !    Intensive variables, scaled by LAI.                                          !
  2220)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2221)          cpatch%mmean_leaf_gsw        (recc) = cpatch%mmean_leaf_gsw        (recc) * rlai  &
  2222)                                              + cpatch%mmean_leaf_gsw        (donc) * dlai
  2223)          cpatch%mmean_leaf_gbw        (recc) = cpatch%mmean_leaf_gbw        (recc) * rlai  &
  2224)                                              + cpatch%mmean_leaf_gbw        (donc) * dlai
  2225)          cpatch%mmean_fs_open         (recc) = cpatch%mmean_fs_open         (recc) * rlai  &
  2226)                                              + cpatch%mmean_fs_open         (donc) * dlai
  2227)          cpatch%mmean_fsw             (recc) = cpatch%mmean_fsw             (recc) * rlai  &
  2228)                                              + cpatch%mmean_fsw             (donc) * dlai
  2229)          cpatch%mmean_fsn             (recc) = cpatch%mmean_fsn             (recc) * rlai  &
  2230)                                              + cpatch%mmean_fsn             (donc) * dlai
  2231)          cpatch%mmean_A_open          (recc) = cpatch%mmean_A_open          (recc) * rlai  &
  2232)                                              + cpatch%mmean_A_open          (donc) * dlai
  2233)          cpatch%mmean_A_closed        (recc) = cpatch%mmean_A_closed        (recc) * rlai  &
  2234)                                              + cpatch%mmean_A_closed        (donc) * dlai
  2235)          cpatch%mmean_A_net           (recc) = cpatch%mmean_A_net           (recc) * rlai  &
  2236)                                              + cpatch%mmean_A_net           (donc) * dlai
  2237)          cpatch%mmean_A_light         (recc) = cpatch%mmean_A_light         (recc) * rlai  &
  2238)                                              + cpatch%mmean_A_light         (donc) * dlai
  2239)          cpatch%mmean_A_rubp          (recc) = cpatch%mmean_A_rubp          (recc) * rlai  &
  2240)                                              + cpatch%mmean_A_rubp          (donc) * dlai
  2241)          cpatch%mmean_A_co2           (recc) = cpatch%mmean_A_co2           (recc) * rlai  &
  2242)                                              + cpatch%mmean_A_co2           (donc) * dlai
  2243)          cpatch%mmean_psi_open        (recc) = cpatch%mmean_psi_open        (recc) * rlai  &
