  2244)                                              + cpatch%mmean_psi_open        (donc) * dlai
  2245)          cpatch%mmean_psi_closed      (recc) = cpatch%mmean_psi_closed      (recc) * rlai  &
  2246)                                              + cpatch%mmean_psi_closed      (donc) * dlai
  2247)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2248) 
  2249) 
  2250) 
  2251) 
  2252)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2253)          !    Intensive variables, scaled by WAI.                                          !
  2254)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2255)          cpatch%mmean_wood_gbw        (recc) = cpatch%mmean_wood_gbw        (recc) * rwai  &
  2256)                                              + cpatch%mmean_wood_gbw        (donc) * dwai
  2257)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2258) 
  2259) 
  2260) 
  2261) 
  2262)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2263)          !    Extensive variables.                                                         !
  2264)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2265)          cpatch%mmean_lai             (recc) = cpatch%mmean_lai             (recc)         &
  2266)                                              + cpatch%mmean_lai             (donc)
  2267)          cpatch%mmean_leaf_energy     (recc) = cpatch%mmean_leaf_energy     (recc)         &
  2268)                                              + cpatch%mmean_leaf_energy     (donc)
  2269)          cpatch%mmean_leaf_water      (recc) = cpatch%mmean_leaf_water      (recc)         &
  2270)                                              + cpatch%mmean_leaf_water      (donc)
  2271)          cpatch%mmean_leaf_hcap       (recc) = cpatch%mmean_leaf_hcap       (recc)         &
  2272)                                              + cpatch%mmean_leaf_hcap       (donc)
  2273)          cpatch%mmean_wood_energy     (recc) = cpatch%mmean_wood_energy     (recc)         &
  2274)                                              + cpatch%mmean_wood_energy     (donc)
  2275)          cpatch%mmean_wood_water      (recc) = cpatch%mmean_wood_water      (recc)         &
  2276)                                              + cpatch%mmean_wood_water      (donc)
  2277)          cpatch%mmean_wood_hcap       (recc) = cpatch%mmean_wood_hcap       (recc)         &
  2278)                                              + cpatch%mmean_wood_hcap       (donc)
  2279)          cpatch%mmean_water_supply    (recc) = cpatch%mmean_water_supply    (recc)         &
  2280)                                              + cpatch%mmean_water_supply    (donc)
  2281)          cpatch%mmean_par_l           (recc) = cpatch%mmean_par_l           (recc)         &
  2282)                                              + cpatch%mmean_par_l           (donc)
  2283)          cpatch%mmean_par_l_beam      (recc) = cpatch%mmean_par_l_beam      (recc)         &
  2284)                                              + cpatch%mmean_par_l_beam      (donc)
  2285)          cpatch%mmean_par_l_diff      (recc) = cpatch%mmean_par_l_diff      (recc)         &
  2286)                                              + cpatch%mmean_par_l_diff      (donc)
  2287) 
  2288)          cpatch%mmean_rshort_l        (recc) = cpatch%mmean_rshort_l        (recc)         &
  2289)                                              + cpatch%mmean_rshort_l        (donc)
  2290)          cpatch%mmean_rlong_l         (recc) = cpatch%mmean_rlong_l         (recc)         &
  2291)                                              + cpatch%mmean_rlong_l         (donc)
  2292)          cpatch%mmean_sensible_lc     (recc) = cpatch%mmean_sensible_lc     (recc)         &
  2293)                                              + cpatch%mmean_sensible_lc     (donc)
  2294)          cpatch%mmean_vapor_lc        (recc) = cpatch%mmean_vapor_lc        (recc)         &
  2295)                                              + cpatch%mmean_vapor_lc        (donc)
  2296)          cpatch%mmean_transp          (recc) = cpatch%mmean_transp          (recc)         &
  2297)                                              + cpatch%mmean_transp          (donc)
  2298)          cpatch%mmean_intercepted_al  (recc) = cpatch%mmean_intercepted_al  (recc)         &
  2299)                                              + cpatch%mmean_intercepted_al  (donc)
  2300)          cpatch%mmean_wshed_lg        (recc) = cpatch%mmean_wshed_lg        (recc)         &
  2301)                                              + cpatch%mmean_wshed_lg        (donc)
  2302)          cpatch%mmean_rshort_w        (recc) = cpatch%mmean_rshort_w        (recc)         &
  2303)                                              + cpatch%mmean_rshort_w        (donc)
  2304)          cpatch%mmean_rlong_w         (recc) = cpatch%mmean_rlong_w         (recc)         &
  2305)                                              + cpatch%mmean_rlong_w         (donc)
  2306)          cpatch%mmean_rad_profile   (:,recc) = cpatch%mmean_rad_profile   (:,recc)         &
  2307)                                              + cpatch%mmean_rad_profile   (:,donc)
  2308)          cpatch%mmean_sensible_wc     (recc) = cpatch%mmean_sensible_wc     (recc)         &
  2309)                                              + cpatch%mmean_sensible_wc     (donc)
  2310)          cpatch%mmean_vapor_wc        (recc) = cpatch%mmean_vapor_wc        (recc)         &
  2311)                                              + cpatch%mmean_vapor_wc        (donc)
  2312)          cpatch%mmean_intercepted_aw  (recc) = cpatch%mmean_intercepted_aw  (recc)         &
  2313)                                              + cpatch%mmean_intercepted_aw  (donc)
  2314)          cpatch%mmean_wshed_wg        (recc) = cpatch%mmean_wshed_wg        (recc)         &
  2315)                                              + cpatch%mmean_wshed_wg        (donc)
  2316)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2317) 
  2318) 
  2319) 
  2320)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2321)          !      We update temperature and liquid water fraction.  We check whether the     !
  2322)          ! heat capacity is non-zero.  If it is a normal number, use the standard thermo-  !
  2323)          ! dynamic library, otherwise, average temperature, this is probably a blend of    !
  2324)          ! tiny cohorts that couldn't be solved, or the wood is not solved.                !
  2325)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2326)          !------ Leaf. --------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2327)          if ( cpatch%mmean_leaf_hcap(recc) > 0. ) then
  2328)             !----- Update temperature and liquid fraction using standard thermodynamics. --!
  2329)             call uextcm2tl(cpatch%mmean_leaf_energy(recc),cpatch%mmean_leaf_water(recc)    &
  2330)                           ,cpatch%mmean_leaf_hcap  (recc),cpatch%mmean_leaf_temp (recc)    &
  2331)                           ,cpatch%mmean_leaf_fliq  (recc))                                                  
  2332)             !------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2333) 
  2334) 
  2335)             !----- Scale vapour pressure deficit using LAI. -------------------------------!
  2336)             cpatch%mmean_leaf_vpdef   (recc) = cpatch%mmean_leaf_vpdef      (recc) * rlai  &
  2337)                                              + cpatch%mmean_leaf_vpdef      (donc) * dlai
  2338)             !------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2339)          else
  2340)             !----- None of the cohorts has leaf biomass use nplant to scale them. ---------!
  2341)             cpatch%mmean_leaf_temp (recc) = cpatch%mmean_leaf_temp (recc) * rnplant        &
  2342)                                           + cpatch%mmean_leaf_temp (donc) * dnplant
  2343)             cpatch%mmean_leaf_fliq (recc) = 0.0
  2344)             cpatch%mmean_leaf_vpdef(recc) = cpatch%mmean_leaf_vpdef(recc) * rnplant        &
  2345)                                           + cpatch%mmean_leaf_vpdef(donc) * dnplant
  2346)             !------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2347)          end if                                                                            
  2348)          !------ Wood. --------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2349)          if ( cpatch%mmean_wood_hcap(recc) > 0. ) then                                     
  2350)             !----- Update temperature using the standard thermodynamics. ------------------!
  2351)             call uextcm2tl(cpatch%mmean_wood_energy(recc),cpatch%mmean_wood_water(recc)    &
  2352)                           ,cpatch%mmean_wood_hcap  (recc),cpatch%mmean_wood_temp (recc)    &
  2353)                           ,cpatch%mmean_wood_fliq  (recc))
  2354)             !------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2355)          else                                                                              
  2356)             !----- Wood temperature can't be found using uextcm2tl (singularity). ---------!
  2357)             cpatch%mmean_wood_temp(recc) = cpatch%mmean_wood_temp(recc) * rnplant          &
  2358)                                          + cpatch%mmean_wood_temp(donc) * dnplant
  2359)             cpatch%mmean_wood_fliq(recc) = 0.0
  2360)             !------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2361)          end if
  2362)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2363) 
  2364) 
  2365) 
  2366)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2367)          !    Fuse mortality rates.  By definition, mortality rate M for is given by:      !
  2368)          !                                                                                 !
  2369)          !                                    ln(A) - ln(N)                                !
  2370)          !                               m = ---------------                               !
  2371)          !                                          dt                                     !
  2372)          !                                                                                 !
  2373)          ! where A is the population that was previously alive, and N is the population    !
  2374)          ! that survived the mortality.  The cohorts represent a group of individuals with !
  2375)          ! the same size and PFT, so they don't mix new recruits and old plants. There-    !
  2376)          ! fore, we can assume that N is actually nplant.  We don't know A, if the         !
  2377)          ! mortality rate is assumed constant during the interval dt, A = N * exp(m dt).   !
  2378)          !                                                                                 !
  2379)          ! For fusion we don't really care about dt, so any number will do as long as it   !
  2380)          ! is the same for both cohorts.  With these assumptions, the mortality rate for   !
  2381)          ! the fused cohort mf is:                                                         !
  2382)          !                                                                                 !
  2383)          !  mf   =  ln (Ad+Ar) - ln(Nd+Nr) = ln[Nd*exp(md) + Nr*exp(mr)] - ln[Nd+Nr]       !
  2384)          !                                                                                 !
  2385)          !             / Nd*exp(md) + Nr*exp(mr) \                                         !
  2386)          !  mf   =  ln |-------------------------|                                         !
  2387)          !             \        Nd + Nr          /                                         !
  2388)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2389)          do imty=1,n_mort
  2390)             exp_mort_donc = exp(max(lnexp_min,min(lnexp_max                                &
  2391)                                                  ,cpatch%mmean_mort_rate(imty,donc))))
  2392)             exp_mort_recc = exp(max(lnexp_min,min(lnexp_max                                &
  2393)                                                  ,cpatch%mmean_mort_rate(imty,recc))))
  2394)             cpatch%mmean_mort_rate(imty,recc) = log( exp_mort_recc * rnplant               &
  2395)                                                    + exp_mort_donc * dnplant )
  2396)          end do
  2397)          !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2398)       end if
  2399)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2400) 
  2401) 
  2402) 
  2403) 
  2404)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2405)       !    Mean diel.                                                                      !
  2406)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2407)       if (writing_dcyc .and. (.not. fuse_initial)) then
  2408)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2409)          !     First we merge the squares, as they require the means.                      !
  2410)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2411)          do t=1,ndcycle
  2412)             !----- Intensive. -------------------------------------------------------------!
  2413)             cpatch%qmsqu_gpp        (t,recc) = fuse_msqu(cpatch%qmean_gpp        (t,recc)  &
  2414)                                                         ,cpatch%qmsqu_gpp        (t,recc)  &
  2415)                                                         ,rnplant                           &
  2416)                                                         ,cpatch%qmean_gpp        (t,donc)  &
  2417)                                                         ,cpatch%qmsqu_gpp        (t,donc)  &
  2418)                                                         ,dnplant                           &
  2419)                                                         ,corr_cohort,.false.)
  2420)             cpatch%qmsqu_npp        (t,recc) = fuse_msqu(cpatch%qmean_npp        (t,recc)  &
  2421)                                                         ,cpatch%qmsqu_npp        (t,recc)  &
  2422)                                                         ,rnplant                           &
  2423)                                                         ,cpatch%qmean_npp        (t,donc)  &
  2424)                                                         ,cpatch%qmsqu_npp        (t,donc)  &
  2425)                                                         ,dnplant                           &
  2426)                                                         ,corr_cohort,.false.)
  2427)             cpatch%qmsqu_plresp     (t,recc) = fuse_msqu(cpatch%qmean_plresp     (t,recc)  &
  2428)                                                         ,cpatch%qmsqu_plresp     (t,recc)  &
  2429)                                                         ,rnplant                           &
  2430)                                                         ,cpatch%qmean_plresp     (t,donc)  &
  2431)                                                         ,cpatch%qmsqu_plresp     (t,donc)  &
  2432)                                                         ,dnplant                           &
  2433)                                                         ,corr_cohort,.false.)
  2434)             !----- Extensive variables. ---------------------------------------------------!
  2435)             cpatch%qmsqu_sensible_lc(t,recc) = fuse_msqu(cpatch%qmean_sensible_lc(t,recc)  &
  2436)                                                         ,cpatch%qmsqu_sensible_lc(t,recc)  &
  2437)                                                         ,rnplant                           &
  2438)                                                         ,cpatch%qmean_sensible_lc(t,donc)  &
  2439)                                                         ,cpatch%qmsqu_sensible_lc(t,donc)  &
  2440)                                                         ,dnplant                           &
  2441)                                                         ,corr_cohort,.true. )
  2442)             cpatch%qmsqu_vapor_lc   (t,recc) = fuse_msqu(cpatch%qmean_vapor_lc   (t,recc)  &
  2443)                                                         ,cpatch%qmsqu_vapor_lc   (t,recc)  &
  2444)                                                         ,rnplant                           &
  2445)                                                         ,cpatch%qmean_vapor_lc   (t,donc)  &
  2446)                                                         ,cpatch%qmsqu_vapor_lc   (t,donc)  &
  2447)                                                         ,dnplant                           &
  2448)                                                         ,corr_cohort,.true. )
  2449)             cpatch%qmsqu_transp     (t,recc) = fuse_msqu(cpatch%qmean_transp     (t,recc)  &
  2450)                                                         ,cpatch%qmsqu_transp     (t,recc)  &
  2451)                                                         ,rnplant                           &
  2452)                                                         ,cpatch%qmean_transp     (t,donc)  &
  2453)                                                         ,cpatch%qmsqu_transp     (t,donc)  &
  2454)                                                         ,dnplant                           &
  2455)                                                         ,corr_cohort,.true. )
  2456)             cpatch%qmsqu_sensible_wc(t,recc) = fuse_msqu(cpatch%qmean_sensible_wc(t,recc)  &
  2457)                                                         ,cpatch%qmsqu_sensible_wc(t,recc)  &
  2458)                                                         ,rnplant                           &
  2459)                                                         ,cpatch%qmean_sensible_wc(t,donc)  &
  2460)                                                         ,cpatch%qmsqu_sensible_wc(t,donc)  &
  2461)                                                         ,dnplant                           &
  2462)                                                         ,corr_cohort,.true. )
  2463)             cpatch%qmsqu_vapor_wc   (t,recc) = fuse_msqu(cpatch%qmean_vapor_wc   (t,recc)  &
  2464)                                                         ,cpatch%qmsqu_vapor_wc   (t,recc)  &
  2465)                                                         ,rnplant                           &
  2466)                                                         ,cpatch%qmean_vapor_wc   (t,donc)  &
  2467)                                                         ,cpatch%qmsqu_vapor_wc   (t,donc)  &
  2468)                                                         ,dnplant                           &
  2469)                                                         ,corr_cohort,.true. )
  2470)             !------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2471)          end do
  2472)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2473) 
  2474) 
  2475) 
  2476)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2477)          !    Intensive variables, scaled by plant density.                                !
  2478)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2479)          cpatch%qmean_gpp             (:,recc) = cpatch%qmean_gpp             (:,recc)     &
  2480)                                                * rnplant                                   &
  2481)                                                + cpatch%qmean_gpp             (:,donc)     &
  2482)                                                * dnplant
  2483)          cpatch%qmean_npp             (:,recc) = cpatch%qmean_npp             (:,recc)     &
  2484)                                                * rnplant                                   &
  2485)                                                + cpatch%qmean_npp             (:,donc)     &
  2486)                                                * dnplant
  2487)          cpatch%qmean_leaf_resp       (:,recc) = cpatch%qmean_leaf_resp       (:,recc)     &
  2488)                                                * rnplant                                   &
  2489)                                                + cpatch%qmean_leaf_resp       (:,donc)     &
  2490)                                                * dnplant
  2491)          cpatch%qmean_root_resp       (:,recc) = cpatch%qmean_root_resp       (:,recc)     &
  2492)                                                * rnplant                                   &
  2493)                                                + cpatch%qmean_root_resp       (:,donc)     &
  2494)                                                * dnplant
  2495)          cpatch%qmean_leaf_growth_resp(:,recc) = cpatch%qmean_leaf_growth_resp(:,recc)     &
  2496)                                                * rnplant                                   &
  2497)                                                + cpatch%qmean_leaf_growth_resp(:,donc)     &
  2498)                                                * dnplant
  2499)          cpatch%qmean_root_growth_resp(:,recc) = cpatch%qmean_root_growth_resp(:,recc)     &
  2500)                                                * rnplant                                   &
  2501)                                                + cpatch%qmean_root_growth_resp(:,donc)     &
  2502)                                                * dnplant
  2503)          cpatch%qmean_sapa_growth_resp(:,recc) = cpatch%qmean_sapa_growth_resp(:,recc)     &
  2504)                                                * rnplant                                   &
  2505)                                                + cpatch%qmean_sapa_growth_resp(:,donc)     &
  2506)                                                * dnplant
  2507)          cpatch%qmean_sapb_growth_resp(:,recc) = cpatch%qmean_sapb_growth_resp(:,recc)     &
  2508)                                                * rnplant                                   &
  2509)                                                + cpatch%qmean_sapb_growth_resp(:,donc)     &
  2510)                                                * dnplant
  2511)          cpatch%qmean_leaf_storage_resp(:,recc)= cpatch%qmean_leaf_storage_resp(:,recc)    &
  2512)                                                * rnplant                                   &
  2513)                                                + cpatch%qmean_leaf_storage_resp(:,donc)    &
  2514)                                                * dnplant
  2515)          cpatch%qmean_root_storage_resp(:,recc)= cpatch%qmean_root_storage_resp(:,recc)    &
  2516)                                                * rnplant                                   &
  2517)                                                + cpatch%qmean_root_storage_resp(:,donc)    &
  2518)                                                * dnplant
  2519)          cpatch%qmean_sapa_storage_resp(:,recc)= cpatch%qmean_sapa_storage_resp(:,recc)    &
  2520)                                                * rnplant                                   &
  2521)                                                + cpatch%qmean_sapa_storage_resp(:,donc)    &
  2522)                                                * dnplant
  2523)          cpatch%qmean_sapb_storage_resp(:,recc)= cpatch%qmean_sapb_storage_resp(:,recc)    &
  2524)                                                * rnplant                                   &
  2525)                                                + cpatch%qmean_sapb_storage_resp(:,donc)    &
  2526)                                                * dnplant
  2527)          cpatch%qmean_plresp          (:,recc) = cpatch%qmean_plresp          (:,recc)     &
  2528)                                                * rnplant                                   &
  2529)                                                + cpatch%qmean_plresp          (:,donc)     &
  2530)                                                * dnplant
  2531)          cpatch%qmean_light_level     (:,recc) = cpatch%qmean_light_level     (:,recc)     &
  2532)                                                * rnplant                                   &
  2533)                                                + cpatch%qmean_light_level     (:,donc)     &
  2534)                                                * dnplant
  2535)          cpatch%qmean_light_level_beam(:,recc) = cpatch%qmean_light_level_beam(:,recc)     &
  2536)                                                * rnplant                                   &
  2537)                                                + cpatch%qmean_light_level_beam(:,donc)     &
  2538)                                                * dnplant
  2539)          cpatch%qmean_light_level_diff(:,recc) = cpatch%qmean_light_level_diff(:,recc)     &
  2540)                                                * rnplant                                   &
  2541)                                                + cpatch%qmean_light_level_diff(:,donc)     &
  2542)                                                * dnplant
  2543)          cpatch%qmean_par_level_beam  (:,recc) = cpatch%qmean_par_level_beam  (:,recc)     &
  2544)                                                * rnplant                                   &
  2545)                                                + cpatch%qmean_par_level_beam  (:,donc)     &
  2546)                                                * dnplant
  2547)          cpatch%qmean_par_level_diffd (:,recc) = cpatch%qmean_par_level_diffd (:,recc)     &
  2548)                                                * rnplant                                   &
  2549)                                                + cpatch%qmean_par_level_diffd (:,donc)     &
  2550)                                                * dnplant
  2551)          cpatch%qmean_par_level_diffu (:,recc) = cpatch%qmean_par_level_diffu (:,recc)     &
  2552)                                                * rnplant                                   &
  2553)                                                + cpatch%qmean_par_level_diffu (:,donc)     &
  2554)                                                * dnplant
  2555)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2556) 
  2557) 
  2558) 
  2559) 
  2560)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2561)          !    Intensive variables, scaled by LAI.                                          !
  2562)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2563)          cpatch%qmean_leaf_gsw      (:,recc) = cpatch%qmean_leaf_gsw      (:,recc) * rlai  &
  2564)                                              + cpatch%qmean_leaf_gsw      (:,donc) * dlai
  2565)          cpatch%qmean_leaf_gbw      (:,recc) = cpatch%qmean_leaf_gbw      (:,recc) * rlai  &
  2566)                                              + cpatch%qmean_leaf_gbw      (:,donc) * dlai
  2567)          cpatch%qmean_fs_open       (:,recc) = cpatch%qmean_fs_open       (:,recc) * rlai  &
  2568)                                              + cpatch%qmean_fs_open       (:,donc) * dlai
  2569)          cpatch%qmean_fsw           (:,recc) = cpatch%qmean_fsw           (:,recc) * rlai  &
  2570)                                              + cpatch%qmean_fsw           (:,donc) * dlai
  2571)          cpatch%qmean_fsn           (:,recc) = cpatch%qmean_fsn           (:,recc) * rlai  &
  2572)                                              + cpatch%qmean_fsn           (:,donc) * dlai
  2573)          cpatch%qmean_A_open        (:,recc) = cpatch%qmean_A_open        (:,recc) * rlai  &
  2574)                                              + cpatch%qmean_A_open        (:,donc) * dlai
  2575)          cpatch%qmean_A_closed      (:,recc) = cpatch%qmean_A_closed      (:,recc) * rlai  &
  2576)                                              + cpatch%qmean_A_closed      (:,donc) * dlai
  2577)          cpatch%qmean_A_net         (:,recc) = cpatch%qmean_A_net         (:,recc) * rlai  &
  2578)                                              + cpatch%qmean_A_net         (:,donc) * dlai
  2579)          cpatch%qmean_A_light       (:,recc) = cpatch%qmean_A_light       (:,recc) * rlai  &
  2580)                                              + cpatch%qmean_A_light       (:,donc) * dlai
  2581)          cpatch%qmean_A_rubp        (:,recc) = cpatch%qmean_A_rubp        (:,recc) * rlai  &
  2582)                                              + cpatch%qmean_A_rubp        (:,donc) * dlai
  2583)          cpatch%qmean_A_co2         (:,recc) = cpatch%qmean_A_co2         (:,recc) * rlai  &
  2584)                                              + cpatch%qmean_A_co2         (:,donc) * dlai
  2585)          cpatch%qmean_psi_open      (:,recc) = cpatch%qmean_psi_open      (:,recc) * rlai  &
  2586)                                              + cpatch%qmean_psi_open      (:,donc) * dlai
  2587)          cpatch%qmean_psi_closed    (:,recc) = cpatch%qmean_psi_closed    (:,recc) * rlai  &
  2588)                                              + cpatch%qmean_psi_closed    (:,donc) * dlai
  2589)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2590) 
  2591) 
  2592) 
  2593) 
  2594)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2595)          !    Intensive variables, scaled by WAI.                                          !
  2596)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2597)          cpatch%qmean_wood_gbw      (:,recc) = cpatch%qmean_wood_gbw      (:,recc) * rwai  &
  2598)                                              + cpatch%qmean_wood_gbw      (:,donc) * dwai
  2599)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2600) 
  2601) 
  2602) 
  2603) 
  2604)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2605)          !    Extensive variables.                                                         !
  2606)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2607)          cpatch%qmean_leaf_energy   (:,recc) = cpatch%qmean_leaf_energy   (:,recc)         &
  2608)                                              + cpatch%qmean_leaf_energy   (:,donc)
  2609)          cpatch%qmean_leaf_water    (:,recc) = cpatch%qmean_leaf_water    (:,recc)         &
  2610)                                              + cpatch%qmean_leaf_water    (:,donc)
  2611)          cpatch%qmean_leaf_hcap     (:,recc) = cpatch%qmean_leaf_hcap     (:,recc)         &
  2612)                                              + cpatch%qmean_leaf_hcap     (:,donc)
  2613)          cpatch%qmean_wood_energy   (:,recc) = cpatch%qmean_wood_energy   (:,recc)         &
  2614)                                              + cpatch%qmean_wood_energy   (:,donc)
  2615)          cpatch%qmean_wood_water    (:,recc) = cpatch%qmean_wood_water    (:,recc)         &
  2616)                                              + cpatch%qmean_wood_water    (:,donc)
  2617)          cpatch%qmean_wood_hcap     (:,recc) = cpatch%qmean_wood_hcap     (:,recc)         &
  2618)                                              + cpatch%qmean_wood_hcap     (:,donc)
  2619)          cpatch%qmean_water_supply  (:,recc) = cpatch%qmean_water_supply  (:,recc)         &
  2620)                                              + cpatch%qmean_water_supply  (:,donc)
  2621)          cpatch%qmean_par_l         (:,recc) = cpatch%qmean_par_l         (:,recc)         &
  2622)                                              + cpatch%qmean_par_l         (:,donc)
  2623)          cpatch%qmean_par_l_beam    (:,recc) = cpatch%qmean_par_l_beam    (:,recc)         &
  2624)                                              + cpatch%qmean_par_l_beam    (:,donc)
  2625)          cpatch%qmean_par_l_diff    (:,recc) = cpatch%qmean_par_l_diff    (:,recc)         &
  2626)                                              + cpatch%qmean_par_l_diff    (:,donc)
  2627) 
  2628)  
  2629) 
  2630)          cpatch%qmean_rshort_l      (:,recc) = cpatch%qmean_rshort_l      (:,recc)         &
  2631)                                              + cpatch%qmean_rshort_l      (:,donc)
  2632)          cpatch%qmean_rlong_l       (:,recc) = cpatch%qmean_rlong_l       (:,recc)         &
  2633)                                              + cpatch%qmean_rlong_l       (:,donc)
  2634)          cpatch%qmean_sensible_lc   (:,recc) = cpatch%qmean_sensible_lc   (:,recc)         &
  2635)                                              + cpatch%qmean_sensible_lc   (:,donc)
  2636)          cpatch%qmean_vapor_lc      (:,recc) = cpatch%qmean_vapor_lc      (:,recc)         &
  2637)                                              + cpatch%qmean_vapor_lc      (:,donc)
  2638)          cpatch%qmean_transp        (:,recc) = cpatch%qmean_transp        (:,recc)         &
  2639)                                              + cpatch%qmean_transp        (:,donc)
  2640)          cpatch%qmean_intercepted_al(:,recc) = cpatch%qmean_intercepted_al(:,recc)         &
  2641)                                              + cpatch%qmean_intercepted_al(:,donc)
  2642)          cpatch%qmean_wshed_lg      (:,recc) = cpatch%qmean_wshed_lg      (:,recc)         &
  2643)                                              + cpatch%qmean_wshed_lg      (:,donc)
  2644)          cpatch%qmean_rshort_w      (:,recc) = cpatch%qmean_rshort_w      (:,recc)         &
  2645)                                              + cpatch%qmean_rshort_w      (:,donc)
  2646)          cpatch%qmean_rlong_w       (:,recc) = cpatch%qmean_rlong_w       (:,recc)         &
  2647)                                              + cpatch%qmean_rlong_w       (:,donc)
  2648)          cpatch%qmean_rad_profile (:,:,recc) = cpatch%qmean_rad_profile (:,:,recc)         &
  2649)                                              + cpatch%qmean_rad_profile (:,:,donc)
  2650)          cpatch%qmean_sensible_wc   (:,recc) = cpatch%qmean_sensible_wc   (:,recc)         &
  2651)                                              + cpatch%qmean_sensible_wc   (:,donc)
  2652)          cpatch%qmean_vapor_wc      (:,recc) = cpatch%qmean_vapor_wc      (:,recc)         &
  2653)                                              + cpatch%qmean_vapor_wc      (:,donc)
  2654)          cpatch%qmean_intercepted_aw(:,recc) = cpatch%qmean_intercepted_aw(:,recc)         &
  2655)                                              + cpatch%qmean_intercepted_aw(:,donc)
  2656)          cpatch%qmean_wshed_wg      (:,recc) = cpatch%qmean_wshed_wg      (:,recc)         &
  2657)                                              + cpatch%qmean_wshed_wg      (:,donc)
  2658)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2659) 
  2660) 
  2661) 
  2662)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2663)          !      We update temperature and liquid water fraction.  We check whether the     !
  2664)          ! heat capacity is non-zero.  If it is a normal number, use the standard thermo-  !
  2665)          ! dynamic library, otherwise, average temperature, this is probably a blend of    !
  2666)          ! tiny cohorts that couldn't be solved, or the wood is not solved.                !
  2667)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2668)          do t=1,ndcycle
  2669)             !------ Leaf. -----------------------------------------------------------------!
  2670)             if ( cpatch%qmean_leaf_hcap(t,recc) > 0. ) then
  2671)                !----- Update temperature and liquid fraction. -----------------------------!
  2672)                call uextcm2tl(cpatch%qmean_leaf_energy(t,recc)                             &
  2673)                              ,cpatch%qmean_leaf_water (t,recc)                             &
  2674)                              ,cpatch%qmean_leaf_hcap  (t,recc)                             &
  2675)                              ,cpatch%qmean_leaf_temp  (t,recc)                             &
  2676)                              ,cpatch%qmean_leaf_fliq  (t,recc))
  2677)                !---------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2678) 
  2679) 
  2680)                !----- Scale vapour pressure deficit using LAI. ----------------------------!
  2681)                cpatch%qmean_leaf_vpdef (t,recc) = cpatch%qmean_leaf_vpdef  (t,recc) * rlai &
  2682)                                                 + cpatch%qmean_leaf_vpdef  (t,donc) * dlai
  2683)                !---------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2684)             else
  2685)                !----- None of the cohorts has leaf biomass use nplant to scale them. ------!
  2686)                cpatch%qmean_leaf_temp (t,recc) = cpatch%qmean_leaf_temp (t,recc) * rnplant &
  2687)                                                + cpatch%qmean_leaf_temp (t,donc) * dnplant
  2688)                cpatch%qmean_leaf_fliq (t,recc) = 0.0
  2689)                cpatch%qmean_leaf_vpdef(t,recc) = cpatch%qmean_leaf_vpdef(t,recc) * rnplant &
  2690)                                                + cpatch%qmean_leaf_vpdef(t,donc) * dnplant
  2691)                !---------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2692)             end if
  2693)             !------ Wood. -----------------------------------------------------------------!
  2694)             if ( cpatch%qmean_wood_hcap(t,recc) > 0. ) then
  2695)                !----- Update temperature and liquid fraction. -----------------------------!
  2696)                call uextcm2tl(cpatch%qmean_wood_energy(t,recc)                             &
  2697)                              ,cpatch%qmean_wood_water (t,recc)                             &
  2698)                              ,cpatch%qmean_wood_hcap  (t,recc)                             &
  2699)                              ,cpatch%qmean_wood_temp  (t,recc)                             &
  2700)                              ,cpatch%qmean_wood_fliq  (t,recc))
  2701)                !---------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2702)             else
  2703)                !----- None of the cohorts has leaf biomass use nplant to scale them. ------!
  2704)                cpatch%qmean_wood_temp (t,recc) = cpatch%qmean_wood_temp (t,recc) * rnplant &
  2705)                                                + cpatch%qmean_wood_temp (t,donc) * dnplant
  2706)                cpatch%qmean_wood_fliq (t,recc) = 0.0
  2707)                !---------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2708)             end if
  2709)             !------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2710)          end do
  2711)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2712)       end if
  2713)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2714) 
  2715) 
  2716) 
  2717)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2718)       !     Lastly, we update nplant, LAI, WAI, and crown area.  They may be used as       !
  2719)       ! weighting factors so we leave them to the end.                                     !
  2720)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2721)       cpatch%nplant     (recc) = cpatch%nplant(recc) + cpatch%nplant(donc)
  2722)       cpatch%lai        (recc) = cpatch%lai   (recc) + cpatch%lai   (donc)
  2723)       cpatch%wai        (recc) = cpatch%wai   (recc) + cpatch%wai   (donc)
  2724)       !----- Make sure that crown area is bounded. ----------------------------------------!
  2725)       cpatch%crown_area (recc) = min(1.,cpatch%crown_area(recc)  + cpatch%crown_area(donc))
  2726)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2727) 
  2728)       return
  2729)    end subroutine fuse_2_cohorts
  2730)    !=======================================================================================!
  2731)    !=======================================================================================!
  2732) 
  2733) 
  2734) 
  2735) 
  2736) 
  2737) 
  2738)    !=======================================================================================!
  2739)    !=======================================================================================!
  2740)    !   This subroutine will sort the patches by age (1st = oldest, last = youngest.)       !
  2741)    !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2742)    subroutine sort_patches(csite)
  2743) 
  2744)       use ed_state_vars, only  :  sitetype   ! ! Structure
  2745)       implicit none
  2746)       !----- Arguments --------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2747)       type(sitetype), target   :: csite      ! Current site, that will have patches sorted.
  2748)       !----- Local variables --------------------------------------------------------------!
  2749)       type(sitetype), pointer  :: tempsite   ! Structure to temporarily host the sorted site
  2750)       integer                  :: ipa        ! Counters
  2751)       integer                  :: oldpa      ! Index of oldest patch
  2752)       logical                  :: sorted     ! Flag: the site is already sorted
  2753)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2754)       
  2755)       !----- No need to sort a site with a single patch. ----------------------------------!
  2756)       if (csite%npatches < 2) return
  2757) 
  2758)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2759)       !     Check whether this site is already sorted.   We don't want to do the entire    !
  2760)       ! deallocating/copying/allocating thing if it's not needed as this takes up too much !
  2761)       ! time.                                                                              !
  2762)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2763)       sorted = .true.
  2764)       sortcheck: do ipa=1,csite%npatches-1
  2765)          sorted = csite%age(ipa) >= csite%age(ipa+1)
  2766)          if (.not. sorted) exit sortcheck
  2767)       end do sortcheck
  2768)       if (sorted) return
  2769)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2770) 
  2771) 
  2772) 
  2773)       !----- Assign a scratch patch. ------------------------------------------------------!
  2774)       nullify (tempsite)
  2775)       allocate(tempsite)
  2776)       call allocate_sitetype(tempsite,csite%npatches)
  2777)       
  2778)       ipa = 0
  2779)       !---- Loop until all patches were sorted. -------------------------------------------!
  2780)       do while (ipa < csite%npatches)
  2781)          ipa = ipa + 1
  2782)       
  2783)          !----- Find the oldest site. -----------------------------------------------------!
  2784)          oldpa = maxloc(csite%age,dim=1)
  2785)          
  2786)          !----- Copy to patch the scratch structure. --------------------------------------!
  2787)          call copy_sitetype(csite,tempsite,oldpa,oldpa,ipa,ipa)
  2788)          
  2789)          !----- Put a non-sense age so this patch will never "win" again. -----------------!
  2790)          csite%age(oldpa) = -huge(1.)
  2791)       end do
  2792) 
  2793)       !------ Reset the actual patch, and re-allocate it. ---------------------------------!
  2794)       call deallocate_sitetype(csite)
  2795)       call allocate_sitetype  (csite,tempsite%npatches)
  2796) 
  2797)       !------ Copy the scratch patch to the regular one. ----------------------------------!
  2798)       call copy_sitetype(tempsite,csite,1,tempsite%npatches,1,tempsite%npatches)
  2799)       call deallocate_sitetype(tempsite)
  2800)       deallocate(tempsite)
  2801) 
  2802)       return
  2803) 
  2804)    end subroutine sort_patches
  2805)    !=======================================================================================!
  2806)    !=======================================================================================!
  2807) 
  2808) 
  2809) 
  2810) 
  2811) 
  2812) 
  2813)    !=======================================================================================!
  2814)    !=======================================================================================!
  2815)    !   This subroutine will perform patch fusion based on some similarity criteria to      !
  2816)    ! determine whether they can be fused with no significant loss of information. The user !
  2817)    ! is welcome to set up a benchmark, but they should be aware that no miracles will      !
  2818)    ! happen here. If there are more very distinct patches than maxpatch, then the user     !
  2819)    ! will need to live with that and accept life is not always fair with those with        !
  2820)    ! limited computational resources.                                                      !
  2821)    !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2822)    subroutine fuse_patches(cgrid,ifm,fuse_initial)
  2823)       use patch_pft_size_profile_mod
  2824)       use ed_state_vars       , only : edtype              & ! structure
  2825)                                      , polygontype         & ! structure
  2826)                                      , sitetype            & ! structure
  2827)                                      , patchtype           ! ! structure
  2828)       use fusion_fission_coms , only : ff_nhgt             & ! intent(in)
  2829)                                      , niter_patfus        & ! intent(in)
  2830)                                      , dark_cumlai_max     & ! intent(in)
  2831)                                      , dark_cumlai_mult    & ! intent(in)
  2832)                                      , sunny_cumlai_min    & ! intent(in)
  2833)                                      , sunny_cumlai_mult   & ! intent(in)
  2834)                                      , print_fuse_details  & ! intent(in)
  2835)                                      , light_toler_min     & ! intent(in)
  2836)                                      , light_toler_mult    & ! intent(in)
  2837)                                      , min_oldgrowth       & ! intent(in)
  2838)                                      , fuse_prefix         ! ! intent(in)
  2839)       use ed_max_dims         , only : n_pft               & ! intent(in)
  2840)                                      , str_len             ! ! intent(in)
  2841)       use mem_polygons        , only : maxpatch            ! ! intent(in)
  2842)       use ed_node_coms        , only : mynum               ! ! intent(in)
  2843)       use ed_misc_coms        , only : current_time        ! ! intent(in)
  2844)       use grid_coms           , only : nzg                 & ! intent(in)
  2845)                                      , nzs                 ! ! intent(in)
  2846)       implicit none
  2847)       !----- Arguments --------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2848)       type(edtype)          , target      :: cgrid           ! Current grid
  2849)       integer               , intent(in)  :: ifm             ! Current grid index
  2850)       logical               , intent(in)  :: fuse_initial    ! Called from initialisation?
  2851)       !----- Local variables --------------------------------------------------------------!
  2852)       type(polygontype)     , pointer     :: cpoly           ! Current polygon
  2853)       type(polygontype)     , pointer     :: jpoly           ! Current polygon
  2854)       type(sitetype)        , pointer     :: csite           ! Current site
  2855)       type(patchtype)       , pointer     :: cpatch          ! Current patch
  2856)       type(patchtype)       , pointer     :: donpatch        ! Donor patch
  2857)       type(patchtype)       , pointer     :: recpatch        ! Receptor patch
  2858)       type(sitetype)        , pointer     :: tempsite        ! Temporary site
  2859)       logical, dimension(:) , allocatable :: fuse_table      ! Flag: this will remain.
  2860)       character(len=str_len)              :: fuse_fout       ! Filename for detailed output
  2861)       integer                             :: ipy             ! Counters
  2862)       integer                             :: isi             ! Counters
  2863)       integer                             :: jpy             ! Counters
  2864)       integer                             :: jsi             ! Counters
  2865)       integer                             :: ipa             ! Counters
  2866)       integer                             :: ico             ! Counters
  2867)       integer                             :: donp            ! Counters
  2868)       integer                             :: recp            ! Counters
  2869)       integer                             :: rec_lu          ! Land use of receptor patch
  2870)       integer                             :: don_lu          ! Land use of donor patch
  2871)       integer                             :: ihgt            ! Counters
  2872)       integer                             :: ifus            ! Counters
  2873)       integer                             :: npatches_new    ! New # of patches
  2874)       integer                             :: npatches_old    ! Old # of patches
  2875)       integer                             :: npatches_orig   ! Original # of patches
  2876)       logical                             :: fuse_flag       ! Flag: fusion will happen
  2877)       logical                             :: recp_found      ! Found a receptor candidate
  2878)       logical                             :: sunny_donp      ! Donor patch bin too sunny
  2879)       logical                             :: sunny_recp      ! Receptor patch bin too sunny
  2880)       logical                             :: dark_donp       ! Donor patch bin too small
  2881)       logical                             :: dark_recp       ! Receptor patch bin too small
  2882)       logical                             :: same_age        ! Patches with same age
  2883)       logical                             :: old_or_same_lu  ! Old patches or the same LU.
  2884)       real                                :: diff            ! Absolute difference in prof.
  2885)       real                                :: refv            ! Reference value of bin
  2886)       real                                :: norm            ! Normalised difference
  2887)       real                                :: llevel_donp     ! Light level of donor patch
  2888)       real                                :: llevel_recp     ! Light level of rec.  patch
  2889)       real                                :: sunny_toler     ! Light layer tolerance.
  2890)       real                                :: dark_lai80      ! Minimum dark layer.
  2891)       real                                :: dark_toler      ! Dark layer tolerance.
  2892)       real                                :: light_toler     ! Light level Relative toler.
  2893)       real                                :: old_area        ! For area conservation check
  2894)       real                                :: new_area        ! For area conservation check
  2895)       real                                :: now_area        ! Area for LAI80
  2896)       real                                :: old_lai_tot     ! Old total LAI
  2897)       real                                :: old_nplant_tot  ! Old total nplant
  2898)       real                                :: new_lai_tot     ! New total LAI
  2899)       real                                :: new_nplant_tot  ! New total nplant
  2900)       real                                :: elim_nplant     ! Elim. nplant during 1 fusion
  2901)       real                                :: elim_lai        ! Elim. LAI during 1 fusion
  2902)       real                                :: elim_nplant_tot ! Total eliminated nplant
  2903)       real                                :: elim_lai_tot    ! Elim. eliminated LAI
  2904)       real                                :: cumlai_recp     ! Cumulative LAI (receptor)
  2905)       real                                :: cumlai_donp     ! Cumulative LAI (donor)
  2906)       integer                             :: tot_npolygons   ! Total # of polygons
  2907)       integer                             :: tot_nsites      ! Total # of sites
  2908)       integer                             :: tot_npatches    ! Total # of patches
  2909)       integer                             :: tot_ncohorts    ! Total # of cohorts
  2910)       !----- Locally saved variables. --------------------------------------------------------!
  2911)       logical                   , save    :: first_time = .true.
  2912)       logical                   , save    :: dont_force_fuse
  2913)       logical                   , save    :: force_fuse
  2914)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2915) 
  2916) 
  2917)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2918)       !     First time here.  Delete all files.                                            !
  2919)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2920)       if (first_time) then
  2921)          force_fuse      = abs(maxpatch) == 1
  2922)          dont_force_fuse = .not. force_fuse
  2923)          if (print_fuse_details) then
  2924)             do jpy = 1, cgrid%npolygons
  2925)                jpoly => cgrid%polygon(jpy)
  2926)                do jsi = 1, jpoly%nsites
  2927)                   write (fuse_fout,fmt='(a,2(a,i4.4),a)')                                  &
  2928)                         trim(fuse_prefix),'polygon_',jpy,'_site_',jsi,'.txt'
  2929)                   open (unit=72,file=trim(fuse_fout),status='replace',action='write')
  2930)                   write(unit=72,fmt='(a)')       '----------------------------------------'
  2931)                   write(unit=72,fmt='(a)')       ' Patch Fusion log for: '
  2932)                   write(unit=72,fmt='(a,1x,i5)') ' POLYGON: ',jpy 
  2933)                   write(unit=72,fmt='(a,1x,i5)') ' SITE:    ',jsi 
  2934)                   write(unit=72,fmt='(a)')       '----------------------------------------'
  2935)                   write(unit=72,fmt='(a)')       ' '
  2936)                   close(unit=72,status='keep')
  2937)                end do
  2938)                !---------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2939)             end do
  2940)             !------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2941)          end if
  2942)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2943)          first_time = .false.
  2944)       end if
  2945)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2946) 
  2947) 
  2948) 
  2949)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2950)       !     Return if maxpatch is 0, this is a flag for no patch fusion.                   !
  2951)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2952)       if (maxpatch == 0) return
  2953)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2954) 
  2955) 
  2956) 
  2957) 
  2958)       polyloop: do ipy = 1,cgrid%npolygons
  2959)          cpoly => cgrid%polygon(ipy)
  2960)          
  2961)          siteloop: do isi = 1,cpoly%nsites
  2962)             csite => cpoly%site(isi)
  2963) 
  2964)             write(fuse_fout,fmt='(a,2(a,i4.4),a)')                                         &
  2965)                      trim(fuse_prefix),'polygon_',ipy,'_site_',isi,'.txt'
  2966) 
  2967)             if (print_fuse_details) then
  2968)                open (unit=72,file=trim(fuse_fout),status='old',action='write'              &
  2969)                                                  ,position='append')
  2970) 
  2971)                write(unit=72,fmt='(2(a,i2.2),a,i4.4)')    ' - Date: ',current_time%month   &
  2972)                                                                  ,'/',current_time%date    &
  2973)                                                                  ,'/',current_time%year
  2974)                write(unit=72,fmt='(a,1x,i6)') '   + Initial number of patches: '           &
  2975)                                              ,csite%npatches
  2976)                write(unit=72,fmt='(a)')       '   + Looking for empty patches: '
  2977)                close(unit=72,status='keep')
  2978)             end if
  2979) 
  2980)             !----- Skip this site if it contains only one patch... ------------------------!
  2981)             if (csite%npatches < 2) cycle siteloop
  2982) 
  2983)             !----- Save original number of patches. ---------------------------------------!
  2984)             npatches_orig = csite%npatches
  2985) 
  2986)             !----- Allocate the swapper patches in the site type. -------------------------!
  2987)             nullify(tempsite)
  2988)             allocate(tempsite)
  2989)             call allocate_sitetype(tempsite, csite%npatches)
  2990)             allocate(fuse_table(csite%npatches))
  2991) 
  2992)             !------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2993)             !     Allocate the fusion flag vector, and set all elements to .true., which   !
  2994)             ! means that every patch can be fused.  As soon as the patch is fused, we will !
  2995)             ! switch the flag to false.                                                    !
  2996)             !------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2997)             fuse_table(:) = .true.
  2998)             !------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  2999) 
  3000) 
  3001)             !------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3002)             !     Find the original number of plants, LAI, and area, which will be used    !
  3003)             ! for sanity check.  We also compute the pft and size profile for all patches, !
  3004)             ! which will be used for the fusion criterion.                                 !
  3005)             !------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3006)             old_nplant_tot = 0.
  3007)             old_lai_tot    = 0.
  3008)             old_area       = 0.
  3009)             do ipa = 1,csite%npatches
  3010)                call patch_pft_size_profile(csite,ipa)
  3011) 
  3012)                old_area  = old_area + csite%area(ipa)
  3013)                cpatch => csite%patch(ipa)
  3014)                do ico = 1, cpatch%ncohorts
  3015)                   old_nplant_tot = old_nplant_tot + cpatch%nplant(ico) * csite%area(ipa)
  3016)                   old_lai_tot    = old_lai_tot    + cpatch%lai(ico)    * csite%area(ipa)
  3017)                end do
  3018)             end do
  3019)             !------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3020) 
  3021) 
  3022) 
  3023)             !----- Initialise the total eliminated nplant and LAI to zero. ----------------!
  3024)             elim_nplant_tot = 0.
  3025)             elim_lai_tot    = 0.
  3026)             !------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3027) 
  3028) 
  3029) 
  3030)             !------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3031)             !     This loop will check whether there is at least two patches with exact    !
  3032)             ! same age.  This is common in initialisation with site-level measurements.    !
  3033)             ! In this case we want to merge any patch, regardless on their "age position", !
  3034)             ! which doesn't mean anything in this case.                                    !
  3035)             !------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3036)             same_age=.false.
  3037)             donloop_check: do donp=csite%npatches,2,-1
  3038)                recloop_check: do recp=donp-1,1,-1
  3039)                   same_age = csite%age(recp)       == csite%age(donp) .and.                &
  3040)                              csite%dist_type(recp) == csite%dist_type(donp)
  3041)                   if (print_fuse_details) then
  3042)                         open (unit=72,file=trim(fuse_fout),status='old',action='write'     &
  3043)                                               ,position='append')
  3044)                         write(unit=72,fmt='(a,1x,l1)') '     * same_age is ',same_age
  3045)                         close(unit=72,status='keep')
  3046)                   end if
  3047)                   !----- At least two patches have the same age. --------------------------!
  3048)                   if (same_age) exit donloop_check
  3049)               end do recloop_check
  3050)             end do donloop_check
  3051)             !------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3052) 
  3053)             !------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3054)             donloope: do donp=csite%npatches,2,-1
  3055)                donpatch => csite%patch(donp)
  3056)                don_lu = csite%dist_type(donp)
  3057)                
  3058)                !----- If patch is not empty, or has already been fused, move on. ----------!
  3059)                if ( (.not. fuse_table(donp)) .or.                                          &
  3060)                     ( dont_force_fuse .and.  donpatch%ncohorts > 0) ) then
  3061)                   cycle donloope
  3062)                end if
  3063)                !---------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3064) 
  3065)                !---------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3066)                !     If we reach this point, it means that the donor patch is empty and    !
  3067)                ! hasn't been fused yet: look for an older empty patch and merge them.      !
  3068)                !---------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3069)                if (print_fuse_details) then
  3070)                   open (unit=72,file=trim(fuse_fout),status='old',action='write'           &
  3071)                                                     ,position='append')
  3072)                   write(unit=72,fmt='(a,i6,a)') '     * Patch ',donp,' is empty.'
  3073)                   close(unit=72,status='keep')
  3074)                end if
  3075)                recloope: do recp=donp-1,1,-1
  3076)                   recpatch => csite%patch(recp)
  3077)                   rec_lu = csite%dist_type(recp)
  3078) 
  3079)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3080)                   !     Set this flag that checks whether the patches have the same        !
  3081)                   ! disturbance type or are too old so we don't need to distinguish them.  !
  3082)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3083)                   old_or_same_lu =   don_lu == rec_lu                         .or.         &
  3084)                                    ( csite%age(donp) >= min_oldgrowth(don_lu) .and.        &
  3085)                                      csite%age(recp) >= min_oldgrowth(rec_lu) )
  3086)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3087) 
  3088)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3089)                   !     Skip the patch if it isn't empty, or it has already been fused, or !
  3090)                   ! if the donor and receptor have different disturbance types.            !
  3091)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3092)                   if ( (.not. fuse_table(recp))                       .or.                 &
  3093)                        ( dont_force_fuse                              .and.                &
  3094)                          ( recpatch%ncohorts > 0 .or. (.not. old_or_same_lu) ) ) ) then
  3095)                      cycle recloope
  3096)                   end if
  3097)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3098) 
  3099)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3100)                   !     Skip the patch if they don't have the same disturbance type and    !
  3101)                   ! are not too old.                                                       !
  3102)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3103)                   if (.not. old_or_same_lu) cycle recloope
  3104)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3105) 
  3106)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3107)                   !     Take an average of the patch properties of donpatch and recpatch,  !
  3108)                   ! and assign the average recpatch.                                       !
  3109)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3110)                   call fuse_2_patches(csite,donp,recp,nzg,nzs                              &
  3111)                                      ,cpoly%lsl(isi),cpoly%ntext_soil(:,isi)               &
  3112)                                      ,cpoly%green_leaf_factor(:,isi),fuse_initial          &
  3113)                                      ,elim_nplant,elim_lai)
  3114)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3115) 
  3116) 
  3117)                   !----- Record the fusion if requested by the user. ----------------------!
  3118)                   if (print_fuse_details) then
  3119)                      open (unit=72,file=trim(fuse_fout),status='old',action='write'        &
  3120)                                                         ,position='append')
  3121)                      write(unit=72,fmt='(2(a,i6),a)') '     * Patches ',donp,' and ',recp  &
  3122)                                                      ,' were fused.'
  3123)                      close(unit=72,status='keep')
  3124)                   end if
  3125)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3126) 
  3127) 
  3128)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3129)                   !    Update total eliminated nplant and LAI.  This is actually not       !
  3130)                   ! necessary in this loop as both patches are empty, but we do it anyway  !
  3131)                   ! just to be consistent.                                                 !
  3132)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3133)                   elim_nplant_tot = elim_nplant_tot + elim_nplant
  3134)                   elim_lai_tot    = elim_lai_tot    + elim_lai
  3135)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3136) 
  3137) 
  3138) 
  3139)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3140)                   !     Recalculate the pft size profile for the averaged patch at recp.   !
  3141)                   ! Again, this is not really necessary as the receptor patch is empty,    !
  3142)                   ! but just to be consistent...                                           !
  3143)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3144)                   call patch_pft_size_profile(csite,recp)
  3145)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3146) 
  3147) 
  3148) 
  3149)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3150)                   !     The patch at index donp will be eliminated and should not be       !
  3151)                   ! checked for fusion again; we switch the fuse_table flag to .false. so  !
  3152)                   ! next time we reach this patch we will skip it.                         !
  3153)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3154)                   fuse_table(donp) = .false.
  3155)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3156) 
  3157)                   !------ We are done with donp, so we quit the recp loop. ----------------!
  3158)                   exit recloope
  3159) 
  3160)                end do recloope
  3161)             end do donloope
  3162)             !------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3163) 
  3164) 
  3165)             !------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3166)             !     Second loop.  Here we will fuse all patches with the same age and        !
  3167)             ! disturbance type.                                                            !
  3168)             !------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3169) 
  3170)             if (same_age) then
  3171)                !----- Start with no multiplication factor. --------------------------------!
  3172)                dark_toler   = dark_cumlai_max
  3173)                sunny_toler  = sunny_cumlai_min
  3174)                light_toler  = light_toler_min
  3175) 
  3176)                mainfuseloopa: do ifus=0,niter_patfus
  3177) 
  3178)                   npatches_old = count(fuse_table)
  3179)                   npatches_new = npatches_old
  3180) 
  3181)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3182)                   !    Inform that the upcoming fusions are going to be with populated     !
  3183)                   ! patches, and record the tolerance used.                                !
  3184)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3185)                   if (print_fuse_details) then
  3186)                      open (unit=72,file=trim(fuse_fout),status='old',action='write'        &
  3187)                                                         ,position='append')
  3188)                      write(unit=72,fmt='(a,1x,3(a,1x,es9.2,1x))')                          &
  3189)                                   '   + Looking for similar populated patches of same age' &
  3190)                                  ,' - Sunny Tolerance =',sunny_toler                       &
  3191)                                  ,' - Dark Tolerance  =',dark_toler                        &
  3192)                                  ,' - Rel. Tolerance  =',light_toler
  3193)                      close(unit=72,status='keep')
  3194)                   end if
  3195)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3196) 
  3197)                   donloopa: do donp=csite%npatches,2,-1
  3198)                      donpatch => csite%patch(donp)
  3199)                      don_lu = csite%dist_type(donp)
  3200)                      
  3201)                      !----- If patch is not empty, or has already been fused, move on. ----!
  3202)                      if ( (.not. fuse_table(donp)) .or.                                    &
  3203)                           ( dont_force_fuse .and. donpatch%ncohorts == 0 ) ) then
  3204)                         cycle donloopa
  3205)                      end if
  3206)                      !---------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3207) 
  3208) 
  3209)                      !---------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3210)                      !     If we reach this point, it means that the donor patch is        !
  3211)                      ! populated and hasn't been fused yet: look for other patches with    !
  3212)                      ! the same age and merge them.                                        !
  3213)                      !---------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3214)                      if (print_fuse_details) then
  3215)                         open (unit=72,file=trim(fuse_fout),status='old',action='write'     &
  3216)                                                           ,position='append')
  3217)                         write(unit=72,fmt='(a,i6,a)') '     * Patch ',donp,' is populated.'
  3218)                         close(unit=72,status='keep')
  3219)                      end if
  3220)                      recloopa: do recp=donp-1,1,-1
  3221)                         recpatch => csite%patch(recp)
  3222)                         rec_lu = csite%dist_type(recp)
  3223) 
  3224)                         !------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3225)                         !     Skip the patch if it isn't empty, or it has already been     !
  3226)                         ! fused, or if the donor and receptor have different disturbance   !
  3227)                         ! types.                                                           !
  3228)                         !------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3229)                         if ( (.not. fuse_table(recp))                           .or.       &
  3230)                              ( dont_force_fuse                                 .and.       &
  3231)                                ( recpatch%ncohorts == 0                         .or.       &
  3232)                                  csite%dist_type(donp) /= csite%dist_type(recp) .or.       &
  3233)                                  csite%age(donp)       /=  csite%age(recp)           ) ) ) &
  3234)                         then
  3235)                            cycle recloopa
  3236)                         end if
  3237)                         !------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3238) 
  3239)                         !------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3240)                         !     Find the LAI that corresponds to 80% of the maximum LAI, to  !
  3241)                         ! avoid relaxing too much for forests.                             !
  3242)                         !------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3243)                         dark_lai80 = 0.40 * ( sum(csite%cumlai_profile(:,1,recp))          &
  3244)                                             + sum(csite%cumlai_profile(:,1,donp)) )
  3245) 
  3246) 
  3247)                         !------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3248)                         !     Compare the size profile for each PFT.  Here we compare the  !
  3249)                         ! maximum LAI for each PFT and height bin.  We switched the        !
  3250)                         ! classes from DBH to height because different PFTs may have       !
  3251)                         ! different heights for a given DBH, so we want to make sure the   !
  3252)                         ! light profile is right.                                          !
  3253)                         !------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3254)                         hgtloopa: do ihgt=1,ff_nhgt
  3255)                            cumlai_recp = sum(csite%cumlai_profile(:,ihgt,recp))
  3256)                            cumlai_donp = sum(csite%cumlai_profile(:,ihgt,donp))
  3257) 
  3258)                            !---------------------------------------------------------------!
  3259)                            !    Check whether these bins contain some LAI.  We don't need  !
  3260)                            ! to check the cohorts if the understorey is too dark, so once  !
  3261)                            ! both patches becomes very dark (very high LAI), we stop       !
  3262)                            ! checking the profiles.                                        !
  3263)                            !---------------------------------------------------------------!
  3264)                            dark_donp = cumlai_donp > dark_toler
  3265)                            dark_recp = cumlai_recp > dark_toler
  3266)                            !---------------------------------------------------------------!
  3267) 
  3268) 
  3269) 
  3270)                            !---------------------------------------------------------------!
  3271)                            if (dark_recp .and. dark_donp) then
  3272) 
  3273)                               if (print_fuse_details) then
  3274)                                  open  (unit=72,file=trim(fuse_fout),status='old'          &
  3275)                                                ,action='write',position='append')
  3276)                                  write (unit=72,fmt='(1(a,1x,i6,1x),4(a,1x,es9.2,1x)'//    &
