  3277)                                                     ',2(a,1x,l1,1x))')                     &
  3278)                                     '       * IHGT =',ihgt                                 &
  3279)                                             ,'CUMLAI_RECP =',cumlai_recp                   &
  3280)                                             ,'CUMLAI_DONP =',cumlai_donp                   &
  3281)                                             ,'DARK_TOLER =',dark_toler                     &
  3282)                                             ,'DARK_LAI80 =',dark_lai80                     &
  3283)                                             ,'DARK_RECP =',dark_recp                       &
  3284)                                             ,'DARK_DONP =',dark_donp
  3285)                                  close (unit=72,status='keep')
  3286)                               end if
  3287)                               cycle hgtloopa
  3288)                            end if
  3289)                            !---------------------------------------------------------------!
  3290) 
  3291) 
  3292) 
  3293)                            
  3294)                            !---------------------------------------------------------------!
  3295)                            !    Check whether these bins contain some LAI.  Bins that have !
  3296)                            ! tiny cumulative LAI may differ by a lot in the relative       !
  3297)                            ! scale, but the actual value is so small that we don't really  !
  3298)                            ! care whether they are relatively different.                   !
  3299)                            !---------------------------------------------------------------!
  3300)                            sunny_donp = cumlai_donp <= sunny_toler
  3301)                            sunny_recp = cumlai_recp <= sunny_toler
  3302)                            !---------------------------------------------------------------!
  3303) 
  3304) 
  3305) 
  3306) 
  3307) 
  3308)                            !---------------------------------------------------------------!
  3309)                            !    If both patches have little or no biomass in this bin,     !
  3310)                            ! don't even bother checking the difference.                    !
  3311)                            !---------------------------------------------------------------!
  3312)                            if (sunny_donp .and. sunny_recp) then
  3313)                               if (print_fuse_details) then
  3314)                                  open  (unit=72,file=trim(fuse_fout),status='old'          &
  3315)                                                ,action='write',position='append')
  3316)                                  write (unit=72,fmt='(1(a,1x,i6,1x),3(a,1x,es9.2,1x)'//    &
  3317)                                                     ',2(a,1x,l1,1x))')                     &
  3318)                                     '       * IHGT=',ihgt                                  &
  3319)                                             ,'CUMLAI_RECP =',cumlai_recp                   &
  3320)                                             ,'CUMLAI_DONP =',cumlai_donp                   &
  3321)                                             ,'SUNNY_TOLER =',sunny_toler                   &
  3322)                                             ,'SUNNY_RECP =',sunny_recp                     &
  3323)                                             ,'SUNNY_RECP =',sunny_donp
  3324)                                  close (unit=72,status='keep')
  3325)                               end if
  3326)                               cycle hgtloopa
  3327)                            end if
  3328)                            !---------------------------------------------------------------!
  3329) 
  3330) 
  3331)                            !---------------------------------------------------------------!
  3332)                            !    Find the normalised difference in the density of this PFT  !
  3333)                            ! and size.  If one of the patches is missing any member of the !
  3334)                            ! profile the norm will be set to 2.0, which is the highest     !
  3335)                            ! value that the norm can be.                                   !
  3336)                            !---------------------------------------------------------------!
  3337)                            llevel_donp = exp(- 0.5 * cumlai_donp)
  3338)                            llevel_recp = exp(- 0.5 * cumlai_recp)
  3339)                            
  3340)                            diff = abs(llevel_donp - llevel_recp )
  3341)                            refv =    (llevel_donp + llevel_recp ) * 0.5
  3342)                            norm = diff / refv
  3343)                            fuse_flag = norm <= light_toler
  3344)                            !---------------------------------------------------------------!
  3345) 
  3346) 
  3347) 
  3348)                            !---------------------------------------------------------------!
  3349)                            if (print_fuse_details) then
  3350)                               open  (unit=72,file=trim(fuse_fout),status='old'             &
  3351)                                             ,action='write',position='append')
  3352)                               write (unit=72,fmt='(1(a,1x,i6,1x),7(a,1x,es9.2,1x)'//       &
  3353)                                                  ',1(a,1x,l1,1x))')                        &
  3354)                                  '       * IHGT=',ihgt                                     &
  3355)                                 ,'CLAI_RECP =',cumlai_recp,'CLAI_DONP =',cumlai_donp       &
  3356)                                 ,'LL_RECP =',llevel_recp,'LL_DONP =',llevel_donp           &
  3357)                                 ,'DIFF =',diff,'REFV =',refv,'NORM =',norm                 &
  3358)                                 ,'FUSE_FLAG =',fuse_flag
  3359)                               close (unit=72,status='keep')
  3360)                            end if
  3361)                            !---------------------------------------------------------------!
  3362) 
  3363) 
  3364) 
  3365)                            !---------------------------------------------------------------!
  3366)                            !     If fuse_flag is false, the patches aren't similar, move   !
  3367)                            ! to the next donor patch.                                      !
  3368)                            !---------------------------------------------------------------!
  3369)                            if (dont_force_fuse .and. (.not. fuse_flag)) cycle recloopa
  3370)                            !---------------------------------------------------------------!
  3371)                         end do hgtloopa
  3372)                         !------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3373) 
  3374) 
  3375) 
  3376)                         !------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3377)                         !     Take an average of the patch properties of donpatch and      !
  3378)                         ! recpatch, and assign the average recpatch.                       !
  3379)                         !------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3380)                         call fuse_2_patches(csite,donp,recp,nzg,nzs                        &
  3381)                                            ,cpoly%lsl(isi),cpoly%ntext_soil(:,isi)         &
  3382)                                            ,cpoly%green_leaf_factor(:,isi),fuse_initial    &
  3383)                                            ,elim_nplant,elim_lai)
  3384)                         !------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3385) 
  3386) 
  3387)                         !----- Record the fusion if requested by the user. ----------------!
  3388)                         if (print_fuse_details) then
  3389)                            open (unit=72,file=trim(fuse_fout),status='old',action='write'  &
  3390)                                                               ,position='append')
  3391)                            write(unit=72,fmt='(2(a,i6),a)') '     * Patches ',donp,' and ' &
  3392)                                                                    ,recp,' were fused.'
  3393)                            close(unit=72,status='keep')
  3394)                         end if
  3395)                         !------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3396) 
  3397) 
  3398)                         !------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3399)                         !    Update total eliminated nplant and LAI.  This is actually not !
  3400)                         ! necessary in this loop as both patches are empty, but we do it   !
  3401)                         ! anyway just to be consistent.                                    !
  3402)                         !------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3403)                         elim_nplant_tot = elim_nplant_tot + elim_nplant
  3404)                         elim_lai_tot    = elim_lai_tot    + elim_lai
  3405)                         !------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3406) 
  3407) 
  3408) 
  3409)                         !------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3410)                         !     Recalculate the pft size profile for the averaged patch at   !
  3411)                         ! recp.  Again, this is not really necessary as the receptor patch !
  3412)                         ! is empty, but just to be consistent...                           !
  3413)                         !------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3414)                         call patch_pft_size_profile(csite,recp)
  3415)                         !------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3416) 
  3417) 
  3418) 
  3419)                         !------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3420)                         !     The patch at index donp will be eliminated and should not be !
  3421)                         ! checked for fusion again; we switch the fuse_table flag to       !
  3422)                         ! .false. so next time we reach this patch we will skip it.        !
  3423)                         !------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3424)                         fuse_table(donp) = .false.
  3425)                         !------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3426)                         !------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3427)                         !     Update the number of valid patches.                          !
  3428)                         !------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3429)                         npatches_new = npatches_new - 1
  3430)                         !------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3431) 
  3432)                         !------ We are done with donp, so we quit the recp loop. ----------!
  3433)                         exit recloopa
  3434)                      end do recloopa
  3435)                   end do donloopa
  3436) 
  3437)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3438)                   !      Check how many patches are valid.  If the total number of patches !
  3439)                   ! is less than the target, or if we have reached the maximum tolerance   !
  3440)                   ! and the patch fusion still can't find similar patches, we quit the     !
  3441)                   ! fusion loop.                                                           !
  3442)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3443)                   if (npatches_new <= abs(maxpatch)) exit mainfuseloopa
  3444)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3445) 
  3446) 
  3447) 
  3448)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3449)                   !     Find the LAI that corresponds to 80% of the maximum LAI, to        !
  3450)                   ! avoid relaxing too much for forests.                                   !
  3451)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3452)                   dark_lai80 = 0.
  3453)                   now_area   = 0.
  3454)                   do ipa=1,csite%npatches
  3455)                      if (fuse_table(ipa)) then
  3456)                         now_area   = now_area + csite%area(ipa)
  3457)                         dark_lai80 = dark_lai80                                            &
  3458)                                    + 0.80 * sum(csite%cumlai_profile(:,1,ipa))             &
  3459)                                    * csite%area(ipa)
  3460)                      end if
  3461)                   end do
  3462)                   if (now_area > 0.) dark_lai80 = dark_lai80 / now_area
  3463)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3464) 
  3465) 
  3466) 
  3467)                   !----- Increment tolerance ----------------------------------------------!
  3468)                   sunny_toler =     sunny_toler * sunny_cumlai_mult
  3469)                   dark_toler  = max( dark_toler * dark_cumlai_mult , dark_lai80 )
  3470)                   light_toler =     light_toler * light_toler_mult
  3471)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3472)                end do mainfuseloopa
  3473)             end if
  3474)             !------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3475) 
  3476) 
  3477)             !------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3478)             !     Third patch loop. Now that all empty patches have been fused, we will    !
  3479)             ! look for populated patches that have similar size and PFT structure, using   !
  3480)             ! the following algorithm:                                                     !
  3481)             !                                                                              !
  3482)             ! 1. Loop from the youngest to oldest patch;                                   !
  3483)             ! 2. Find next older patch with same dist_type;                                !
  3484)             ! 3. Check whether fusion criterion is met, and If so, fuse them.              !
  3485)             ! 4. After all the fusion, check how many patches we still have:               !
  3486)             !    If it is less than maxpatch, we quit, otherwise, we relax the tolerance a !
  3487)             !    little and try fusing more.  Notice that we will always try fusing        !
  3488)             !    patches at least once, even when the original number is less than         !
  3489)             !    maxpatch.                                                                 !
  3490)             !------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3491)             !----- Start with no multiplication factor. -----------------------------------!
  3492)             dark_toler   = dark_cumlai_max
  3493)             sunny_toler  = sunny_cumlai_min
  3494)             light_toler  = light_toler_min
  3495) 
  3496)             mainfuseloop: do ifus=0,niter_patfus
  3497) 
  3498)                npatches_old = count(fuse_table)
  3499)                npatches_new = npatches_old
  3500) 
  3501)                !---------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3502)                !    Inform that the upcoming fusions are going to be with populated        !
  3503)                ! patches, and record the tolerance used.                                   !
  3504)                !---------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3505)                if (print_fuse_details) then
  3506)                   open (unit=72,file=trim(fuse_fout),status='old',action='write'           &
  3507)                                                      ,position='append')
  3508)                   write(unit=72,fmt='(a,1x,3(a,1x,es9.2,1x))')                             &
  3509)                                               '   + Looking for similar populated patches' &
  3510)                                              ,' - Sunny Tolerance =',sunny_toler           &
  3511)                                              ,' - Dark Tolerance  =',dark_toler            &
  3512)                                              ,' - Rel. Tolerance  =',light_toler
  3513)                   close(unit=72,status='keep')
  3514)                end if
  3515)                !---------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3516) 
  3517)                !---------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3518)                !     Loop from youngest to the second oldest patch.                        !
  3519)                !---------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3520)                donloopp: do donp = csite%npatches,2,-1
  3521)                   donpatch => csite%patch(donp)
  3522)                   don_lu = csite%dist_type(donp)
  3523) 
  3524)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3525)                   !     If this is an empty patch, or has already been merged, we skip it. !
  3526)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3527)                   if ((.not. fuse_table(donp))) then
  3528)                      if (print_fuse_details) then
  3529)                         open  (unit=72,file=trim(fuse_fout),status='old',action='write'    &
  3530)                                                            ,position='append')
  3531)                         write (unit=72,fmt='(a,1x,i6,1x,a)') '     - DONP:',donp           &
  3532)                                                             ,'has been already fused...'
  3533)                         close (unit=72,status='keep')
  3534)                      end if
  3535)                      cycle donloopp
  3536)                   end if
  3537)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3538) 
  3539)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3540)                   !      If we have reached this place, the donor patch can be fused.  Now !
  3541)                   ! look for the next oldest patch that has the same disturbance type.  In !
  3542)                   ! case we can't find such patch, we will move to the next donor          !
  3543)                   ! candidate.                                                             !
  3544)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3545)                   recp_found = .false.
  3546)                   recloopp: do recp=donp-1,1,-1
  3547) 
  3548)                      rec_lu = csite%dist_type(recp)
  3549) 
  3550)                      old_or_same_lu =   don_lu == rec_lu                         .or.      &
  3551)                                       ( csite%age(donp) >= min_oldgrowth(don_lu) .and.     &
  3552)                                         csite%age(recp) >= min_oldgrowth(rec_lu) )
  3553) 
  3554)                      recp_found = old_or_same_lu .and. fuse_table(recp) .and.              &
  3555)                                   (csite%dist_type(recp) == 1 .or. csite%age(recp) > 3.)
  3556) 
  3557)                      if (recp_found) then
  3558)                         recpatch => csite%patch(recp)
  3559)                         exit recloopp
  3560)                      end if
  3561)                   end do recloopp
  3562)                  
  3563)                   if (.not. recp_found) then
  3564)                      if (print_fuse_details) then
  3565)                         open  (unit=72,file=trim(fuse_fout),status='old',action='write'    &
  3566)                                                            ,position='append')
  3567)                         write (unit=72,fmt='(a)') '     - No receptor patch found. '
  3568)                         close (unit=72,status='keep')
  3569)                      end if
  3570)                      cycle donloopp
  3571)                   end if
  3572)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3573) 
  3574)                   if (print_fuse_details) then
  3575)                      open  (unit=72,file=trim(fuse_fout),status='old',action='write'       &
  3576)                                                         ,position='append')
  3577)                      write (unit=72,fmt='(2(a,1x,i6,1x))') '     - DONP =',donp            &
  3578)                                                                  ,'RECP =',recp
  3579)                      close (unit=72,status='keep')
  3580)                   end if
  3581) 
  3582)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3583)                   !     This should never happen because we have already fused all empty   !
  3584)                   ! patches, but, just in case... If both patches are empty they cannot be !
  3585)                   ! fused in this loop.                                                    !
  3586)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3587)                   if ( dont_force_fuse        .and.                                        &
  3588)                        donpatch%ncohorts == 0 .and. recpatch%ncohorts == 0) then
  3589)                      cycle donloopp
  3590)                   end if
  3591)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3592) 
  3593) 
  3594)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3595)                   !     Find the LAI that corresponds to 80% of the maximum LAI, to avoid  !
  3596)                   ! relaxing too much for forests.                                         !
  3597)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3598)                   dark_lai80 = 0.40 * ( sum(csite%cumlai_profile(:,1,recp))                &
  3599)                                       + sum(csite%cumlai_profile(:,1,donp)) )
  3600) 
  3601)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3602)                   !     Compare the size profile for each PFT.  Here we compare the        !
  3603)                   ! maximum LAI for each PFT and height bin.  We switched the classes from !
  3604)                   ! DBH to height because different PFTs may have different heights for a  !
  3605)                   ! given DBH, so we want to make sure the light profile is right.         !
  3606)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3607)                   hgtloop: do ihgt=1,ff_nhgt
  3608) 
  3609)                      cumlai_recp = sum(csite%cumlai_profile(:,ihgt,recp))
  3610)                      cumlai_donp = sum(csite%cumlai_profile(:,ihgt,donp))
  3611) 
  3612)                      !---------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3613)                      !    Check whether these bins contain some LAI.  We don't need to     !
  3614)                      ! check the cohorts if the understorey is too dark, so once both      !
  3615)                      ! patches becomes very dark (very high LAI), we stop checking the     !
  3616)                      ! profiles.                                                           !
  3617)                      !---------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3618)                      dark_donp = cumlai_donp > dark_toler
  3619)                      dark_recp = cumlai_recp > dark_toler
  3620)                      !---------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3621) 
  3622)                      !---------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3623)                      if (dark_recp .and. dark_donp) then
  3624) 
  3625)                         if (print_fuse_details) then
  3626)                            open  (unit=72,file=trim(fuse_fout),status='old',action='write' &
  3627)                                                               ,position='append')
  3628)                            write (unit=72,fmt='(1(a,1x,i6,1x),4(a,1x,es9.2,1x)'//          &
  3629)                                               ',2(a,1x,l1,1x))')                           &
  3630)                               '       * IHGT=',ihgt                                        &
  3631)                              ,'CUMLAI_RECP =',cumlai_recp,'CUMLAI_DONP =',cumlai_donp      &
  3632)                              ,'DARK_TOLER =',dark_toler,'DARK_LAI80 =',dark_lai80          &
  3633)                              ,'DARK_RECP =',dark_recp,'DARK_DONP =',dark_donp
  3634)                            close (unit=72,status='keep')
  3635)                         end if
  3636)                         cycle hgtloop
  3637)                      end if
  3638)                      !---------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3639) 
  3640)                      
  3641)                      !---------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3642)                      !    Check whether these bins contain some LAI.  Bins that have       !
  3643)                      ! tiny cumulative LAI may differ by a lot in the relative scale,      !
  3644)                      ! but the actual value is so small that we don't really care          !
  3645)                      ! whether they are relatively different.                              !
  3646)                      !---------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3647)                      sunny_donp = cumlai_donp <= sunny_toler
  3648)                      sunny_recp = cumlai_recp <= sunny_toler
  3649)                      !---------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3650) 
  3651) 
  3652)                      !---------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3653)                      !    If both patches have little or no biomass in this bin, don't     !
  3654)                      ! even bother checking the difference.                                !
  3655)                      !---------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3656)                      if (sunny_donp .and. sunny_recp) then
  3657) 
  3658)                         if (print_fuse_details) then
  3659)                            open  (unit=72,file=trim(fuse_fout),status='old',action='write' &
  3660)                                                               ,position='append')
  3661)                            write (unit=72,fmt='(1(a,1x,i6,1x),3(a,1x,es9.2,1x)'//          &
  3662)                                               ',2(a,1x,l1,1x))')                           &
  3663)                               '       * IHGT=',ihgt                                        &
  3664)                              ,'CUMLAI_RECP =',cumlai_recp,'CUMLAI_DONP =',cumlai_donp      &
  3665)                              ,'SUNNY_TOLER =',sunny_toler,'SUNNY_RECP =',sunny_recp        &
  3666)                              ,'SUNNY_RECP =',sunny_donp
  3667)                            close (unit=72,status='keep')
  3668)                         end if
  3669) 
  3670)                         cycle hgtloop
  3671)                      end if
  3672)                      !---------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3673) 
  3674) 
  3675)                      !---------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3676)                      !    Find the normalised difference in the density of this PFT and    !
  3677)                      ! size.  If one of the patches is missing any member of the           !
  3678)                      ! profile the norm will be set to 2.0, which is the highest value     !
  3679)                      ! that the norm can be.                                               !
  3680)                      !---------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3681)                      llevel_donp = exp(- 0.5 * cumlai_donp)
  3682)                      llevel_recp = exp(- 0.5 * cumlai_recp)
  3683)                      
  3684)                      diff = abs(llevel_donp - llevel_recp )
  3685)                      refv =    (llevel_donp + llevel_recp ) * 0.5
  3686)                      norm = diff / refv
  3687)                      fuse_flag = norm <= light_toler
  3688)                      !---------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3689) 
  3690) 
  3691) 
  3692)                      !---------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3693)                      if (print_fuse_details) then
  3694)                         open  (unit=72,file=trim(fuse_fout),status='old',action='write'    &
  3695)                                                            ,position='append')
  3696)                         write (unit=72,fmt='(1(a,1x,i6,1x),7(a,1x,es9.2,1x)'//             &
  3697)                                            ',1(a,1x,l1,1x))')                              &
  3698)                            '       * IHGT=',ihgt                                           &
  3699)                           ,'CLAI_RECP =',cumlai_recp,'CLAI_DONP =',cumlai_donp             &
  3700)                           ,'LL_RECP =',llevel_recp,'LL_DONP =',llevel_donp                 &
  3701)                           ,'DIFF =',diff,'REFV =',refv,'NORM =',norm                       &
  3702)                           ,'FUSE_FLAG =',fuse_flag
  3703)                         close (unit=72,status='keep')
  3704)                      end if
  3705)                      !---------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3706) 
  3707) 
  3708) 
  3709)                      !---------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3710)                      !     If fuse_flag is false, the patches aren't similar, move to      !
  3711)                      ! the next donor patch.                                               !
  3712)                      !---------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3713)                      if (dont_force_fuse .and. (.not. fuse_flag)) cycle donloopp
  3714)                      !---------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3715)                   end do hgtloop
  3716)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3717) 
  3718)                  
  3719) 
  3720)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3721)                   !      Reaching this point means that the patches are sufficiently       !
  3722)                   ! similar so they will be fused.   We take the average of the patch      !
  3723)                   ! properties of donpatch and recpatch, and leave the averaged values at  !
  3724)                   ! recpatch.                                                              !
  3725)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3726)                   call fuse_2_patches(csite,donp,recp,nzg,nzs                              &
  3727)                                      ,cpoly%lsl(isi),cpoly%ntext_soil(:,isi)               &
  3728)                                      ,cpoly%green_leaf_factor(:,isi),fuse_initial          &
  3729)                                      ,elim_nplant,elim_lai)
  3730)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3731) 
  3732)                   
  3733) 
  3734)                   !----- Record the fusion if requested by the user. ----------------------!
  3735)                   if (print_fuse_details) then
  3736)                      open (unit=72,file=trim(fuse_fout),status='old',action='write'        &
  3737)                                                         ,position='append')
  3738)                      write(unit=72,fmt='(2(a,i6),a)') '     * Patches ',donp,' and ',recp  &
  3739)                                                      ,' were fused.'
  3740)                      close(unit=72,status='keep')
  3741)                   end if
  3742)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3743) 
  3744)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3745)                   !    Some cohorts may have been eliminated during the fusion process,    !
  3746)                   ! because they were way too small.  Add the eliminated plant density and !
  3747)                   ! LAI because we want to make sure that the fusion routine conserves the !
  3748)                   ! total plant density and LAI that remained in the polygon.              !
  3749)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3750)                   elim_nplant_tot = elim_nplant_tot + elim_nplant
  3751)                   elim_lai_tot    = elim_lai_tot    + elim_lai
  3752)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3753) 
  3754) 
  3755)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3756)                   !     Recalculate the pft size profile for the updated receptor patch.   !
  3757)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3758)                   call patch_pft_size_profile(csite,recp)
  3759)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3760) 
  3761) 
  3762)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3763)                   !     From now on donpatch should not be used: set fuse_table flag as    !
  3764)                   ! .false. so we won't check it again.                                    !
  3765)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3766)                   fuse_table(donp) = .false.
  3767)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3768) 
  3769) 
  3770)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3771)                   !     Update the number of valid patches.                                !
  3772)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3773)                   npatches_new = npatches_new - 1
  3774)                   !------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3775)                end do donloopp         ! do donp = csite%npatches,2,-1
  3776)                !---------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3777) 
  3778)                !---------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3779)                !      Check how many patches are valid.  If the total number of patches is !
  3780)                ! less than the target, or if we have reached the maximum tolerance and the !
  3781)                ! patch fusion still can't find similar patches, we quit the fusion loop.   !
  3782)                !---------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3783)                if (npatches_new <= abs(maxpatch))  exit mainfuseloop
  3784)                !---------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3785) 
  3786) 
  3787) 
  3788)                !---------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3789)                !     Find the LAI that corresponds to 80% of the maximum LAI, to           !
  3790)                ! avoid relaxing too much for forests.                                      !
  3791)                !---------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3792)                dark_lai80 = 0.
  3793)                now_area   = 0.
  3794)                do ipa=1,csite%npatches
  3795)                   if (fuse_table(ipa)) then
  3796)                      now_area   = now_area + csite%area(ipa)
  3797)                      dark_lai80 = dark_lai80                                               &
  3798)                                 + 0.80 * sum(csite%cumlai_profile(:,1,ipa))                &
  3799)                                 * csite%area(ipa)
  3800)                   end if
  3801)                end do
  3802)                if (now_area > 0.) dark_lai80 = dark_lai80 / now_area
  3803)                !---------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3804) 
  3805)                !----- Increment tolerance -------------------------------------------------!
  3806)                sunny_toler =     sunny_toler * sunny_cumlai_mult
  3807)                dark_toler  = max( dark_toler * dark_cumlai_mult , dark_lai80 )
  3808)                light_toler =     light_toler * light_toler_mult
  3809)                !---------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3810)             end do mainfuseloop
  3811)             !------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3812) 
  3813)             !----- Set the number of patches in the site to "npatches_new" ----------------!
  3814)             tempsite%npatches = npatches_new
  3815)             !------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3816) 
  3817) 
  3818) 
  3819)             !----- If there was any patch fusion, need to shrink csite --------------------!
  3820)             if (npatches_new < csite%npatches) then
  3821)                !---------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3822)                !    Copy the selected data into the temporary space, args 1 and 3 must be  !
  3823)                ! dimension of arg 4. Argument 2 must be the dimension of the sum of the    !
  3824)                ! 3rd argument.                                                             !
  3825)                !---------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3826)                call copy_sitetype_mask(csite,tempsite,fuse_table,size(fuse_table)          &
  3827)                                       ,npatches_new)
  3828)                call deallocate_sitetype(csite)
  3829) 
  3830)                !----- Reallocate the current site. ----------------------------------------!
  3831)                call allocate_sitetype(csite,npatches_new)
  3832) 
  3833)                !----- Copy the selected temporary data into the orignal site vectors. -----!
  3834)                call copy_sitetype(tempsite,csite,1,npatches_new,1,npatches_new)
  3835) 
  3836)                !---------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3837)                !     The new and fused csite is now complete, clean up the temporary       !
  3838)                ! data. Deallocate it afterwards.                                           !
  3839)                !---------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3840)                call deallocate_sitetype(tempsite)
  3841)             end if
  3842)             !------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3843) 
  3844) 
  3845) 
  3846)             !----- Deallocation should happen outside the "if" statement ------------------!
  3847)             deallocate(tempsite)
  3848)             deallocate(fuse_table)
  3849)             !------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3850) 
  3851) 
  3852)             !----- Make sure that patches are sorted from oldest to youngest. -------------!
  3853)             call sort_patches(csite)
  3854) 
  3855)             if (print_fuse_details) then
  3856)                open (unit=72,file=trim(fuse_fout),status='old',action='write'              &
  3857)                                                   ,position='append')
  3858)                write(unit=72,fmt='(a)')             '   + Patches were sorted. '
  3859)                write(unit=72,fmt='(2(a,1x,i6,1x))')                                        &
  3860)                                        '   + Number of patches.  Original =',npatches_orig &
  3861)                                                                 ,'Current =',csite%npatches
  3862)                write(unit=72,fmt='(a)')       ' '
  3863)                close(unit=72,status='keep')
  3864)             end if
  3865) 
  3866) 
  3867)             !----- This is for mass conservation check ------------------------------------!
  3868)             new_nplant_tot = 0.
  3869)             new_lai_tot    = 0.
  3870)             new_area       = 0.
  3871)             do ipa = 1,csite%npatches
  3872)                new_area = new_area + csite%area(ipa)
  3873)                cpatch => csite%patch(ipa)
  3874)                do ico = 1, cpatch%ncohorts
  3875)                   new_nplant_tot = new_nplant_tot + cpatch%nplant(ico)*csite%area(ipa)
  3876)                   new_lai_tot    = new_lai_tot    + cpatch%lai(ico)*csite%area(ipa)
  3877)                end do
  3878)             end do
  3879)             !------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3880) 
  3881) 
  3882)             !------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3883)             !     Sanity check.  Except for the cohorts that were eliminated because they  !
  3884)             ! have become too small after fusion, the total plant count and LAI should be  !
  3885)             ! preserved.  In case something went wrong, we stop the run, it is likely to   !
  3886)             ! be a bug.                                                                    !
  3887)             !------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3888)             if (new_area       < 0.99 * old_area       .or.                                &
  3889)                 new_area       > 1.01 * old_area            ) then
  3890)                write (unit=*,fmt='(a,1x,es12.5)') 'OLD_AREA:       ',old_area
  3891)                write (unit=*,fmt='(a,1x,es12.5)') 'NEW_AREA:       ',new_area
  3892)                write (unit=*,fmt='(a,1x,es12.5)') 'NEW_LAI_TOT:    ',new_lai_tot
  3893)                write (unit=*,fmt='(a,1x,es12.5)') 'OLD_LAI_TOT:    ',old_lai_tot
  3894)                write (unit=*,fmt='(a,1x,es12.5)') 'ELIM_LAI_TOT:   ',elim_lai_tot
  3895)                write (unit=*,fmt='(a,1x,es12.5)') 'NEW_NPLANT_TOT: ',new_nplant_tot
  3896)                write (unit=*,fmt='(a,1x,es12.5)') 'OLD_NPLANT_TOT: ',old_nplant_tot
  3897)                write (unit=*,fmt='(a,1x,es12.5)') 'ELIM_NPLANT_TOT:',elim_nplant_tot
  3898)                call fatal_error('Conservation failed while fusing patches'                 &
  3899)                               &,'fuse_patches','fuse_fiss_utils.f90')
  3900)             end if
  3901)             !------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3902)             
  3903)          end do siteloop
  3904)       end do polyloop
  3905) 
  3906)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3907)       !     Print a banner to inform the user how many patches and cohorts exist.          !
  3908)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3909)       tot_npolygons = cgrid%npolygons
  3910)       tot_ncohorts  = 0
  3911)       tot_npatches  = 0
  3912)       tot_nsites    = 0
  3913)       do ipy=1,cgrid%npolygons
  3914)          cpoly => cgrid%polygon(ipy)
  3915)          tot_nsites = tot_nsites + cpoly%nsites 
  3916)          do isi=1,cpoly%nsites
  3917)             csite => cpoly%site(isi)
  3918)             tot_npatches = tot_npatches + csite%npatches
  3919)             do ipa=1,csite%npatches
  3920)                cpatch => csite%patch(ipa)
  3921)                tot_ncohorts = tot_ncohorts + cpatch%ncohorts
  3922)             end do
  3923)          end do
  3924)       end do
  3925)       write (unit=*,fmt='(6(a,1x,i8,1x))')                                                 &
  3926)         'Total count in node',mynum,'for grid',ifm,': POLYGONS=',tot_npolygons             &
  3927)        ,'SITES=',tot_nsites,'PATCHES=',tot_npatches,'COHORTS=',tot_ncohorts
  3928)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3929) 
  3930)       return
  3931)    end subroutine fuse_patches
  3932)    !=======================================================================================!
  3933)    !=======================================================================================!
  3934) 
  3935) 
  3936) 
  3937) 
  3938) 
  3939) 
  3940)    !=======================================================================================!
  3941)    !=======================================================================================!
  3942)    !   This subroutine will merge two patches into 1.                                      !
  3943)    !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3944)    subroutine fuse_2_patches(csite,donp,recp,mzg,mzs,lsl,ntext_soil,green_leaf_factor &
  3945)                             ,fuse_initial,elim_nplant,elim_lai)
  3946)       use update_derived_props_module
  3947)       use patch_pft_size_profile_mod
  3948)       use ed_state_vars      , only : sitetype              & ! Structure 
  3949)                                     , patchtype             ! ! Structure
  3950)       use soil_coms          , only : soil                  & ! intent(in), lookup table
  3951)                                     , tiny_sfcwater_mass    & ! intent(in)
  3952)                                     , matric_potential      ! ! intent(in)
  3953)       use ed_max_dims        , only : n_pft                 & ! intent(in)
  3954)                                     , n_dbh                 ! ! intent(in)
  3955)       use mem_polygons       , only : maxcohort             ! ! intent(in)
  3956)       use therm_lib          , only : uextcm2tl             & ! subroutine
  3957)                                     , uint2tl               & ! subroutine
  3958)                                     , idealdenssh           & ! function
  3959)                                     , press2exner           & ! function
  3960)                                     , extheta2temp          ! ! function
  3961)       use ed_misc_coms       , only : writing_long          & ! intent(in)
  3962)                                     , writing_eorq          & ! intent(in)
  3963)                                     , writing_dcyc          & ! intent(in)
  3964)                                     , ndcycle               ! ! intent(in)
  3965)       use budget_utils       , only : update_budget         ! ! intent(in)
  3966)       use consts_coms        , only : wdns                  ! ! intent(in)
  3967)       use fusion_fission_coms, only : corr_patch            ! ! intent(in)
  3968)       implicit none
  3969)       !----- Arguments --------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3970)       type(sitetype)         , target      :: csite             ! Current site
  3971)       integer                , intent(in)  :: donp              ! Donating patch
  3972)       integer                , intent(in)  :: recp              ! Receptor patch
  3973)       integer                , intent(in)  :: lsl               ! Lowest soil level
  3974)       integer                , intent(in)  :: mzg               ! # of soil layers
  3975)       integer                , intent(in)  :: mzs               ! # of sfc. water layers
  3976)       integer, dimension(mzg), intent(in)  :: ntext_soil        ! Soil type
  3977)       real, dimension(n_pft) , intent(in)  :: green_leaf_factor ! Green leaf factor...
  3978)       logical                , intent(in)  :: fuse_initial      ! Initialisation?
  3979)       real                   , intent(out) :: elim_nplant       ! Eliminated nplant 
  3980)       real                   , intent(out) :: elim_lai          ! Eliminated lai
  3981)       !----- Local variables --------------------------------------------------------------!
  3982)       type(patchtype)        , pointer     :: cpatch            ! Current patch
  3983)       type(patchtype)        , pointer     :: temppatch         ! Temporary patch
  3984)       integer                              :: iii               ! Counters
  3985)       integer                              :: nsoil             ! Alias for soil texture
  3986)       integer                              :: t                 ! Counter for time of day
  3987)       integer                              :: ndc               ! # of cohorts - donp patch
  3988)       integer                              :: nrc               ! # of cohorts - recp patch
  3989)       real                                 :: can_exner         ! Exner function - CAS
  3990)       real                                 :: newarea           ! new patch area
  3991)       real                                 :: newareai          ! 1./(new patch area)
  3992)       real                                 :: area_scale        ! Cohort rescaling factor.
  3993)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3994)      
  3995)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3996)       !     This function fuses the two patches specified in the argument. It fuses the    !
  3997)       ! first patch in the argument (the "donor" = donp ) into the second patch in the     !
  3998)       ! argument (the "recipient" = recp ), and frees the memory associated with the donor !
  3999)       ! patch.                                                                             !
  4000)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  4001)     
  4002)       !----- The new area is simply the sum of each patch area. ---------------------------!
  4003)       newarea  = csite%area(donp) + csite%area(recp)
  4004)       newareai = 1.0/newarea
  4005)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  4006) 
  4007)       !----- Assign eliminated LAI and nplant to zero (everything stays) ------------------!
  4008)       elim_nplant = 0.
  4009)       elim_lai    = 0.
  4010)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  4011) 
  4012) 
  4013)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  4014)       !     In case of old-growth stands, the disturbance type flag may be different.  In  !
  4015)       ! this case, we keep the type for the largest patch.                                 !
  4016)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  4017)       if (csite%area(donp) > csite%area(recp)) then
  4018)          csite%dist_type(recp) = csite%dist_type(donp)
  4019)       end if
  4020)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  4021) 
  4022) 
  4023) 
  4024)       !----- We now take the weighted average, scale by the individual patch area. --------!
  4025)       csite%age(recp)                = newareai *                                          &
  4026)                                      ( csite%age(donp)                * csite%area(donp)   &
  4027)                                      + csite%age(recp)                * csite%area(recp) )
  4028) 
  4029)       csite%fast_soil_C(recp)        = newareai *                                          &
  4030)                                      ( csite%fast_soil_C(donp)        * csite%area(donp)   &
  4031)                                      + csite%fast_soil_C(recp)        * csite%area(recp) )
  4032) 
  4033)       csite%slow_soil_C(recp)        = newareai *                                          &
  4034)                                      ( csite%slow_soil_C(donp)        * csite%area(donp)   &
  4035)                                      + csite%slow_soil_C(recp)        * csite%area(recp) )
  4036) 
  4037)       csite%structural_soil_C(recp)  = newareai *                                          &
  4038)                                      ( csite%structural_soil_C(donp)  * csite%area(donp)   &
  4039)                                      + csite%structural_soil_C(recp)  * csite%area(recp) )
  4040)                                      
  4041) 
  4042)       csite%structural_soil_L(recp)  = newareai *                                          &
  4043)                                      ( csite%structural_soil_L(donp)  * csite%area(donp)   &
  4044)                                      + csite%structural_soil_L(recp)  * csite%area(recp) )
  4045)                                      
  4046) 
  4047)       csite%mineralized_soil_N(recp) = newareai *                                          &
  4048)                                      ( csite%mineralized_soil_N(donp) * csite%area(donp)   &
  4049)                                      + csite%mineralized_soil_N(recp) * csite%area(recp) )
  4050) 
  4051)       csite%fast_soil_N(recp)        = newareai *                                          &
  4052)                                      ( csite%fast_soil_N(donp)        * csite%area(donp)   &
  4053)                                      + csite%fast_soil_N(recp)        * csite%area(recp) )
  4054) 
  4055)       csite%sum_dgd(recp)            = newareai *                                          &
  4056)                                      ( csite%sum_dgd(donp)            * csite%area(donp)   &
  4057)                                      + csite%sum_dgd(recp)            * csite%area(recp) )
  4058) 
  4059)       csite%sum_chd(recp)            = newareai *                                          &
  4060)                                      ( csite%sum_chd(donp)            * csite%area(donp)   &
  4061)                                      + csite%sum_chd(recp)            * csite%area(recp) )
  4062) 
  4063)       csite%can_co2(recp)            = newareai *                                          &
  4064)                                      ( csite%can_co2(donp)            * csite%area(donp)   &
  4065)                                      + csite%can_co2(recp)            * csite%area(recp) )
  4066) 
  4067)       csite%can_theta(recp)          = newareai *                                          &
  4068)                                      ( csite%can_theta(donp)          * csite%area(donp)   &
  4069)                                      + csite%can_theta(recp)          * csite%area(recp) )
  4070) 
  4071)       csite%can_temp_pv(recp)        = newareai *                                          &
  4072)                                      ( csite%can_temp_pv(donp)        * csite%area(donp)   &
  4073)                                      + csite%can_temp_pv(recp)        * csite%area(recp) )
  4074) 
  4075)       csite%can_theiv(recp)          = newareai *                                          &
  4076)                                      ( csite%can_theiv(donp)          * csite%area(donp)   &
  4077)                                      + csite%can_theiv(recp)          * csite%area(recp) )
  4078) 
  4079)       csite%can_vpdef(recp)          = newareai *                                          &
  4080)                                      ( csite%can_vpdef(donp)          * csite%area(donp)   &
  4081)                                      + csite%can_vpdef(recp)          * csite%area(recp) )
  4082) 
  4083)       csite%can_prss(recp)           = newareai *                                          &
  4084)                                      ( csite%can_prss(donp)           * csite%area(donp)   &
  4085)                                      + csite%can_prss(recp)           * csite%area(recp) )
  4086) 
  4087)       csite%can_shv(recp)            = newareai *                                          &
  4088)                                      ( csite%can_shv(donp)            * csite%area(donp)   &
  4089)                                      + csite%can_shv(recp)            * csite%area(recp) )
  4090) 
  4091)       csite%can_depth(recp)          = newareai *                                          &
  4092)                                      ( csite%can_depth(donp)          * csite%area(donp)   &
  4093)                                      + csite%can_depth(recp)          * csite%area(recp) )
  4094) 
  4095)       csite%ggbare(recp)             = newareai *                                          &
  4096)                                      ( csite%ggbare(donp)             * csite%area(donp)   &
  4097)                                      + csite%ggbare(recp)             * csite%area(recp) )
  4098) 
  4099)       csite%ggnet(recp)              = newareai *                                          &
  4100)                                      ( csite%ggnet(donp)              * csite%area(donp)   &
  4101)                                      + csite%ggnet(recp)              * csite%area(recp) )
  4102) 
  4103)       csite%ggsoil(recp)             = newareai *                                          &
  4104)                                      ( csite%ggsoil(donp)             * csite%area(donp)   &
  4105)                                      + csite%ggsoil(recp)             * csite%area(recp) )
  4106) 
  4107)       
  4108)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  4109)       !    There is no guarantee that there will be a minimum amount of mass in the tempo- !
  4110)       ! rary layer, nor is there any reason for both patches to have the same number of    !
  4111)       ! layers. In order to be safe, the fusion must happen in 5 stages.                   !
  4112)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  4113)       !----- 1. Find the "extensive" sfcwater_energy (convert from J/kg to J/m2); ---------!
  4114)       do iii=1,csite%nlev_sfcwater(recp)
  4115)          csite%sfcwater_energy(iii,recp) = csite%sfcwater_energy(iii,recp)                 &
  4116)                                          * csite%sfcwater_mass  (iii,recp)
  4117)       end do
  4118)       do iii=1,csite%nlev_sfcwater(donp)
  4119)          csite%sfcwater_energy(iii,donp) = csite%sfcwater_energy(iii,donp)                 &
  4120)                                          * csite%sfcwater_mass  (iii,donp)
  4121)       end do
  4122)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  4123)       ! 2. Squeeze all layers into one.  If needed, the layer will be split again next     !
  4124)       !    time the Runge-Kutta integrator is called.  After adding the value to the first !
  4125)       !    layer, discard the value.                                                       !
  4126)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  4127)       do iii=2,csite%nlev_sfcwater(recp)
  4128)          csite%sfcwater_energy(1,recp) = csite%sfcwater_energy(1,recp)                     &
  4129)                                        + csite%sfcwater_energy(iii,recp)
  4130)          csite%sfcwater_depth(1,recp)  = csite%sfcwater_depth(1,recp)                      &
  4131)                                        + csite%sfcwater_depth(iii,recp)
  4132)          csite%sfcwater_mass(1,recp)   = csite%sfcwater_mass(1,recp)                       &
  4133)                                        + csite%sfcwater_mass(iii,recp)
  4134)          csite%sfcwater_energy(iii,recp) = 0.
  4135)          csite%sfcwater_depth(iii,recp)  = 0.
  4136)          csite%sfcwater_mass(iii,recp)   = 0.
  4137)       end do
  4138)       do iii=2,csite%nlev_sfcwater(donp)
  4139)          csite%sfcwater_energy(1,donp) = csite%sfcwater_energy(1,donp)                     &
  4140)                                        + csite%sfcwater_energy(iii,donp)
  4141)          csite%sfcwater_depth(1,donp)  = csite%sfcwater_depth(1,donp)                      &
  4142)                                        + csite%sfcwater_depth(iii,donp)
  4143)          csite%sfcwater_mass(1,donp)   = csite%sfcwater_mass(1,donp)                       &
  4144)                                        + csite%sfcwater_mass(iii,donp)
  4145)          csite%sfcwater_energy(iii,donp) = 0.
  4146)          csite%sfcwater_depth(iii,donp)  = 0.
  4147)          csite%sfcwater_mass(iii,donp)   = 0.
  4148)       end do
  4149)       !----- 3. Merge the patches; --------------------------------------------------------!
  4150)       if (csite%nlev_sfcwater(recp) > 0 .or. csite%nlev_sfcwater(donp) > 0) then
  4151)          csite%sfcwater_mass(1,recp)   = newareai *                                        &
  4152)                                          (csite%sfcwater_mass(1,recp)  * csite%area(recp)  &
  4153)                                          +csite%sfcwater_mass(1,donp)  * csite%area(donp)  )
  4154)          csite%sfcwater_depth(1,recp)  = newareai *                                        &
  4155)                                          (csite%sfcwater_depth(1,recp) * csite%area(recp)  &
  4156)                                          +csite%sfcwater_depth(1,donp) * csite%area(donp)  )
  4157)          csite%sfcwater_energy(1,recp) = newareai *                                        &
  4158)                                          (csite%sfcwater_energy(1,recp) * csite%area(recp) &
  4159)                                          +csite%sfcwater_energy(1,donp) * csite%area(donp) )
  4160)       else
  4161)          csite%sfcwater_mass(1,recp)   = 0.
  4162)          csite%sfcwater_depth(1,recp)  = 0.
  4163)          csite%sfcwater_energy(1,recp) = 0.
  4164)       end if
  4165)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  4166)       ! 4. Converting energy back to J/kg;                                                 !
  4167)       ! 5. Finding temperature and liquid water fraction;                                  !
  4168)       !    (Both are done in new_patch_sfc_props).                                         !
  4169)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  4170)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  4171)      
  4172) 
  4173)       !----- Merge soil energy and water. -------------------------------------------------!
  4174)       do iii=1,mzg
  4175)          csite%soil_energy(iii,recp)     = newareai *                                      &
  4176)                                          ( csite%soil_energy(iii,donp) * csite%area(donp)  &
  4177)                                          + csite%soil_energy(iii,recp) * csite%area(recp))
  4178) 
  4179)          csite%soil_water(iii,recp)      = newareai *                                      &
  4180)                                          ( csite%soil_water(iii,recp)  * csite%area(recp)  &
  4181)                                          + csite%soil_water(iii,donp)  * csite%area(donp))
  4182)       end do
  4183) 
  4184)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  4185)       !     These variables shouldn't matter because they are reset every day/every month, !
  4186)       ! but just in case...                                                                !
  4187)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  4188)       csite%avg_daily_temp       (recp) = newareai                                         &
  4189)                                         * ( csite%avg_daily_temp       (donp)              &
  4190)                                           * csite%area                 (donp)              &
  4191)                                           + csite%avg_daily_temp       (recp)              &
  4192)                                           * csite%area                 (recp) )
  4193) 
  4194)       csite%avg_monthly_gndwater (recp) = newareai                                         &
  4195)                                         * ( csite%avg_monthly_gndwater (donp)              &
  4196)                                           * csite%area                 (donp)              &
  4197)                                           + csite%avg_monthly_gndwater (recp)              &
  4198)                                           * csite%area                 (recp) )
  4199) 
  4200)       csite%avg_monthly_waterdef (recp) = newareai                                         &
  4201)                                         * ( csite%avg_monthly_waterdef (donp)              &
  4202)                                           * csite%area                 (donp)              &
  4203)                                           + csite%avg_monthly_waterdef (recp)              &
  4204)                                           * csite%area                 (recp) )
  4205)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  4206) 
  4207) 
  4208)       
  4209) 
  4210)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  4211)       !    This subroutine takes care of filling:                                          !
  4212)       !                                                                                    !
  4213)       ! + csite%ground_shv(recp)                                                           !
  4214)       ! + csite%ground_ssh(recp)                                                           !
  4215)       ! + csite%ground_temp(recp)                                                          !
  4216)       ! + csite%ground_fliq(recp)                                                          !
  4217)       ! + csite%soil_tempk(k,recp)                                                         !
  4218)       ! + csite%soil_fracliq(k,recp)                                                       !
  4219)       ! + csite%nlev_sfcwater(recp)                                                        !
  4220)       ! + csite%sfcwater_energy(k,recp) (Just converting back to J/kg)                     !
  4221)       ! + csite%csite%sfcwater_tempk(k,recp)                                               !
  4222)       ! + csite%sfcwater_fracliq(k,recp)                                                   !
  4223)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  4224)       call new_patch_sfc_props(csite,recp,mzg,mzs,ntext_soil)
  4225)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  4226) 
  4227)       csite%today_A_decomp(recp)         = newareai *                                      &
  4228)                                          ( csite%today_A_decomp(donp) * csite%area(donp)   &
  4229)                                          + csite%today_A_decomp(recp) * csite%area(recp) )
  4230) 
  4231)       csite%today_Af_decomp(recp)        = newareai *                                      &
  4232)                                          ( csite%today_Af_decomp(donp)* csite%area(donp)   &
  4233)                                          + csite%today_Af_decomp(recp)* csite%area(recp) )
  4234) 
  4235)       do iii = 1,n_pft
  4236)          csite%repro(iii,recp)           = newareai *                                      &
  4237)                                          ( csite%repro(iii,donp)      * csite%area(donp)   &
  4238)                                          + csite%repro(iii,recp)      * csite%area(recp) )
  4239)       end do
  4240)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  4241) 
  4242) 
  4243)  
  4244) 
  4245) 
  4246)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  4247)       !     Budget variables.                                                              !
  4248)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  4249)       csite%co2budget_residual    (recp) = ( csite%co2budget_residual    (recp)            &
  4250)                                            * csite%area                  (recp)            &
  4251)                                            + csite%co2budget_residual    (donp)            &
  4252)                                            * csite%area                  (donp) )          &
  4253)                                          * newareai

  4257)                                            * csite%area                  (donp) )          &
  4258)                                          * newareai

  4593)                                                  *   newareai
  4594)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  4595) 
  4596)         
  4597)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  4598)          !      Now we find the derived properties for the canopy air space.               !
  4599)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  4600) 
  4601)          can_exner                   = press2exner (csite%fmean_can_prss(recp))
  4602)          csite%fmean_can_temp (recp) = extheta2temp(can_exner,csite%fmean_can_theta (recp))
  4603)          csite%fmean_can_rhos (recp) = idealdenssh ( csite%fmean_can_prss  (recp)          &
  4604)                                                    , csite%fmean_can_temp  (recp)          &
  4605)                                                    , csite%fmean_can_shv   (recp)          )
  4606)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  4607) 
  4608) 
  4609) 
  4610)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  4611)          !      Find the soil mean temperature, liquid water fraction, and matric          !
  4612)          ! potential.                                                                      !
  4613)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  4614)          do iii=lsl,mzg
  4615)             nsoil = ntext_soil(iii)
  4616)             call uextcm2tl( csite%fmean_soil_energy(iii,recp)                              &
  4617)                           , csite%fmean_soil_water (iii,recp) * wdns                       &
  4618)                           , soil(nsoil)%slcpd                                              &
  4619)                           , csite%fmean_soil_temp  (iii,recp)                              &
  4620)                           , csite%fmean_soil_fliq  (iii,recp))
  4621) 
  4622)             csite%fmean_soil_mstpot(iii,recp)  =                                           &
  4623)                                   matric_potential(nsoil,csite%fmean_soil_water (iii,recp))
  4624)          end do
  4625)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  4626) 
  4627)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  4628)          !     Find the temporary surface water properties.  They may not be available at  !
  4629)          ! all times, so we must check.                                                    !
  4630)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  4631)          !----- Temporarily make energy extensive [J/m2]. ---------------------------------!
  4632)          csite%fmean_sfcw_depth           (recp) = ( csite%fmean_sfcw_depth        (recp)  &
  4633)                                                    * csite%area                    (recp)  &
  4634)                                                    + csite%fmean_sfcw_depth        (donp)  &
  4635)                                                    * csite%area                    (donp)) &
  4636)                                                  *   newareai
  4637)          csite%fmean_sfcw_energy          (recp) = ( csite%fmean_sfcw_energy       (recp)  &
  4638)                                                    * csite%fmean_sfcw_mass         (recp)  &
  4639)                                                    * csite%area                    (recp)  &
  4640)                                                    + csite%fmean_sfcw_energy       (donp)  &
  4641)                                                    * csite%fmean_sfcw_mass         (donp)  &
  4642)                                                    * csite%area                    (donp)) &
  4643)                                                  *   newareai
  4644)          csite%fmean_sfcw_mass            (recp) = ( csite%fmean_sfcw_mass         (recp)  &
  4645)                                                    * csite%area                    (recp)  &
  4646)                                                    + csite%fmean_sfcw_mass         (donp)  &
  4647)                                                    * csite%area                    (donp)) &
  4648)                                                  *   newareai
  4649)          !----- Check whether there is enough surface water. ------------------------------!
  4650)          if (csite%fmean_sfcw_mass(recp) > tiny_sfcwater_mass) then
  4651)             csite%fmean_sfcw_energy       (recp) =   csite%fmean_sfcw_energy       (recp)  &
  4652)                                                  /   csite%fmean_sfcw_mass         (recp)
  4653)             call uint2tl( csite%fmean_sfcw_energy(recp)                                    &
  4654)                         , csite%fmean_sfcw_temp  (recp)                                    &
  4655)                         , csite%fmean_sfcw_fliq  (recp) )
  4656)          else
  4657)             csite%fmean_sfcw_mass  (recp)  = 0.
  4658)             csite%fmean_sfcw_depth (recp)  = 0.
  4659)             csite%fmean_sfcw_energy(recp)  = 0.
  4660)             csite%fmean_sfcw_temp  (recp)  = csite%fmean_soil_temp(mzg,recp)
  4661)             csite%fmean_sfcw_fliq  (recp)  = csite%fmean_soil_fliq(mzg,recp)
  4662)          end if
  4663)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  4664) 
  4665)       end if
  4666)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  4667) 
  4668) 
  4669) 
  4670)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------! 
  4671)       !    Daily means.                                                                    !
  4672)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
