  4820)          csite%dmean_albedo_nir         (recp) = ( csite%dmean_albedo_nir         (recp)   &
  4821)                                                  * csite%area                     (recp)   &
  4822)                                                  + csite%dmean_albedo_nir         (donp)   &
  4823)                                                  * csite%area                     (donp) ) &
  4824)                                                *   newareai
  4825)          csite%dmean_rlong_albedo       (recp) = ( csite%dmean_rlong_albedo       (recp)   &
  4826)                                                  * csite%area                     (recp)   &
  4827)                                                  + csite%dmean_rlong_albedo       (donp)   &
  4828)                                                  * csite%area                     (donp) ) &
  4829)                                                *   newareai
  4830)          csite%dmean_ustar              (recp) = ( csite%dmean_ustar              (recp)   &
  4831)                                                  * csite%area                     (recp)   &
  4832)                                                  + csite%dmean_ustar              (donp)   &
  4833)                                                  * csite%area                     (donp) ) &
  4834)                                                *   newareai
  4835)          csite%dmean_tstar              (recp) = ( csite%dmean_tstar              (recp)   &
  4836)                                                  * csite%area                     (recp)   &
  4837)                                                  + csite%dmean_tstar              (donp)   &
  4838)                                                  * csite%area                     (donp) ) &
  4839)                                                *   newareai
  4840)          csite%dmean_qstar              (recp) = ( csite%dmean_qstar              (recp)   &
  4841)                                                  * csite%area                     (recp)   &
  4842)                                                  + csite%dmean_qstar              (donp)   &
  4843)                                                  * csite%area                     (donp) ) &
  4844)                                                *   newareai
  4845)          csite%dmean_cstar              (recp) = ( csite%dmean_cstar              (recp)   &
  4846)                                                  * csite%area                     (recp)   &
  4847)                                                  + csite%dmean_cstar              (donp)   &
  4848)                                                  * csite%area                     (donp) ) &
  4849)                                                *   newareai
  4850)          csite%dmean_carbon_ac          (recp) = ( csite%dmean_carbon_ac          (recp)   &
  4851)                                                  * csite%area                     (recp)   &
  4852)                                                  + csite%dmean_carbon_ac          (donp)   &
  4853)                                                  * csite%area                     (donp) ) &
  4854)                                                *   newareai
  4855)          csite%dmean_carbon_st          (recp) = ( csite%dmean_carbon_st          (recp)   &
  4856)                                                  * csite%area                     (recp)   &
  4857)                                                  + csite%dmean_carbon_st          (donp)   &
  4858)                                                  * csite%area                     (donp) ) &
  4859)                                                *   newareai
  4860)          csite%dmean_vapor_gc           (recp) = ( csite%dmean_vapor_gc           (recp)   &
  4861)                                                  * csite%area                     (recp)   &
  4862)                                                  + csite%dmean_vapor_gc           (donp)   &
  4863)                                                  * csite%area                     (donp) ) &
  4864)                                                *   newareai
  4865)          csite%dmean_vapor_ac           (recp) = ( csite%dmean_vapor_ac           (recp)   &
  4866)                                                  * csite%area                     (recp)   &
  4867)                                                  + csite%dmean_vapor_ac           (donp)   &
  4868)                                                  * csite%area                     (donp) ) &
  4869)                                                *   newareai
  4870)          csite%dmean_throughfall        (recp) = ( csite%dmean_throughfall        (recp)   &
  4871)                                                  * csite%area                     (recp)   &
  4872)                                                  + csite%dmean_throughfall        (donp)   &
  4873)                                                  * csite%area                     (donp) ) &
  4874)                                                *   newareai
  4875)          csite%dmean_runoff             (recp) = ( csite%dmean_runoff             (recp)   &
  4876)                                                  * csite%area                     (recp)   &
  4877)                                                  + csite%dmean_runoff             (donp)   &
  4878)                                                  * csite%area                     (donp) ) &
  4879)                                                *   newareai
  4880)          csite%dmean_drainage           (recp) = ( csite%dmean_drainage           (recp)   &
  4881)                                                  * csite%area                     (recp)   &
  4882)                                                  + csite%dmean_drainage           (donp)   &
  4883)                                                  * csite%area                     (donp) ) &
  4884)                                                *   newareai
  4885)          csite%dmean_sensible_gc        (recp) = ( csite%dmean_sensible_gc        (recp)   &
  4886)                                                  * csite%area                     (recp)   &
  4887)                                                  + csite%dmean_sensible_gc        (donp)   &
  4888)                                                  * csite%area                     (donp) ) &
  4889)                                                *   newareai
  4890)          csite%dmean_sensible_ac        (recp) = ( csite%dmean_sensible_ac        (recp)   &
  4891)                                                  * csite%area                     (recp)   &
  4892)                                                  + csite%dmean_sensible_ac        (donp)   &
  4893)                                                  * csite%area                     (donp) ) &
  4894)                                                *   newareai
  4895)          csite%dmean_qthroughfall       (recp) = ( csite%dmean_qthroughfall       (recp)   &
  4896)                                                  * csite%area                     (recp)   &
  4897)                                                  + csite%dmean_qthroughfall       (donp)   &
  4898)                                                  * csite%area                     (donp) ) &
  4899)                                                *   newareai
  4900)          csite%dmean_qrunoff            (recp) = ( csite%dmean_qrunoff            (recp)   &
  4901)                                                  * csite%area                     (recp)   &
  4902)                                                  + csite%dmean_qrunoff            (donp)   &
  4903)                                                  * csite%area                     (donp) ) &
  4904)                                                *   newareai
  4905)          csite%dmean_qdrainage          (recp) = ( csite%dmean_qdrainage          (recp)   &
  4906)                                                  * csite%area                     (recp)   &
  4907)                                                  + csite%dmean_qdrainage          (donp)   &
  4908)                                                  * csite%area                     (donp) ) &
  4909)                                                *   newareai
  4910)          csite%dmean_smoist_gg        (:,recp) = ( csite%dmean_smoist_gg        (:,recp)   &
  4911)                                                  * csite%area                     (recp)   &
  4912)                                                  + csite%dmean_smoist_gg        (:,donp)   &
  4913)                                                  * csite%area                     (donp) ) &
  4914)                                                *   newareai
  4915)          csite%dmean_transloss        (:,recp) = ( csite%dmean_transloss        (:,recp)   &
  4916)                                                  * csite%area                     (recp)   &
  4917)                                                  + csite%dmean_transloss        (:,donp)   &
  4918)                                                  * csite%area                     (donp) ) &
  4919)                                                *   newareai
  4920)          csite%dmean_sensible_gg      (:,recp) = ( csite%dmean_sensible_gg      (:,recp)   &
  4921)                                                  * csite%area                     (recp)   &
  4922)                                                  + csite%dmean_sensible_gg      (:,donp)   &
  4923)                                                  * csite%area                     (donp) ) &
  4924)                                                *   newareai
  4925)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  4926) 
  4927) 
  4928) 
  4929)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  4930)          !      Now we find the derived properties for the canopy air space.               !
  4931)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  4932)          can_exner                   = press2exner (csite%dmean_can_prss(recp))
  4933)          csite%dmean_can_temp (recp) = extheta2temp(can_exner,csite%dmean_can_theta(recp))
  4934)          csite%dmean_can_rhos (recp) = idealdenssh ( csite%dmean_can_prss  (recp)          &
  4935)                                                    , csite%dmean_can_temp  (recp)          &
  4936)                                                    , csite%dmean_can_shv   (recp)          )
  4937)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  4938) 
  4939) 
  4940) 
  4941)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  4942)          !      Find the soil mean temperature, liquid water fraction, and matric          !
  4943)          ! potential.                                                                      !
  4944)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  4945)          do iii=lsl,mzg
  4946)             nsoil = ntext_soil(iii)
  4947)             call uextcm2tl( csite%dmean_soil_energy(iii,recp)                              &
  4948)                           , csite%dmean_soil_water (iii,recp) * wdns                       &
  4949)                           , soil(nsoil)%slcpd                                              &
  4950)                           , csite%dmean_soil_temp  (iii,recp)                              &
  4951)                           , csite%dmean_soil_fliq  (iii,recp))
  4952) 
  4953)             csite%dmean_soil_mstpot(iii,recp)  =                                           &
  4954)                                    matric_potential(nsoil,csite%dmean_soil_water(iii,recp))
  4955)          end do
  4956)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  4957) 
  4958) 
  4959)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  4960)          !     Find the temporary surface water properties.  They may not be available at  !
  4961)          ! all times, so we must check.                                                    !
  4962)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  4963)          !----- Temporarily make energy extensive [J/m2]. ---------------------------------!
  4964)          csite%dmean_sfcw_depth         (recp) = ( csite%dmean_sfcw_depth         (recp)   &
  4965)                                                  * csite%area                     (recp)   &
  4966)                                                  + csite%dmean_sfcw_depth         (donp)   &
  4967)                                                  * csite%area                     (donp) ) &
  4968)                                                *   newareai
  4969)          csite%dmean_sfcw_energy        (recp) = ( csite%dmean_sfcw_energy        (recp)   &
  4970)                                                  * csite%dmean_sfcw_mass          (recp)   &
  4971)                                                  * csite%area                     (recp)   &
  4972)                                                  + csite%dmean_sfcw_energy        (donp)   &
  4973)                                                  * csite%dmean_sfcw_mass          (donp)   &
  4974)                                                  * csite%area                     (donp) ) &
  4975)                                                *   newareai
  4976)          csite%dmean_sfcw_mass          (recp) = ( csite%dmean_sfcw_mass          (recp)   &
  4977)                                                  * csite%area                     (recp)   &
  4978)                                                  + csite%dmean_sfcw_mass          (donp)   &
  4979)                                                  * csite%area                     (donp) ) &
  4980)                                                *   newareai
  4981)          !----- Check whether there is enough surface water. ------------------------------!
  4982)          if (csite%dmean_sfcw_mass(recp) > tiny_sfcwater_mass) then
  4983)             csite%dmean_sfcw_energy     (recp) =   csite%dmean_sfcw_energy        (recp)   &
  4984)                                                /   csite%dmean_sfcw_mass          (recp)
  4985)             call uint2tl( csite%dmean_sfcw_energy(recp)                                    &
  4986)                         , csite%dmean_sfcw_temp  (recp)                                    &
  4987)                         , csite%dmean_sfcw_fliq  (recp) )
  4988)          else
  4989)             csite%dmean_sfcw_mass  (recp)  = 0.
  4990)             csite%dmean_sfcw_depth (recp)  = 0.
  4991)             csite%dmean_sfcw_energy(recp)  = 0.
  4992)             csite%dmean_sfcw_temp  (recp)  = csite%dmean_soil_temp(mzg,recp)
  4993)             csite%dmean_sfcw_fliq  (recp)  = csite%dmean_soil_fliq(mzg,recp)
  4994)          end if
  4995)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  4996) 		end if
  4997)       end if
  4998)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  4999) 
  5000)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------! 
  5001)       !    Monthly means.                                                                  !
  5002)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------! 
  5003)       if (writing_eorq .and. (.not. fuse_initial)) then
  5004)         if( all(csite%mmean_can_prss > 10.0) ) then
  5005) 
  5006)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  5007)          !    First we find the mean sum of squares, because they depend on the means too, !
  5008)          ! and the receptor values are lost after fusion.  All variables are intensive at  !
  5009)          ! the patch level.                                                                !
  5010)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  5011) 
  5012)          csite%mmsqu_rh         (recp) = fuse_msqu( csite%mmean_rh         (recp)          &
  5013)                                                   , csite%mmsqu_rh         (recp)          &
  5014)                                                   , csite%area             (recp)          &
  5015)                                                   , csite%mmean_rh         (donp)          &
  5016)                                                   , csite%mmsqu_rh         (donp)          &
  5017)                                                   , csite%area             (donp)          &
  5018)                                                   , corr_patch, .false.)
  5019)          csite%mmsqu_cwd_rh     (recp) = fuse_msqu( csite%mmean_cwd_rh     (recp)          &
  5020)                                                   , csite%mmsqu_cwd_rh     (recp)          &
  5021)                                                   , csite%area             (recp)          &
  5022)                                                   , csite%mmean_cwd_rh     (donp)          &
  5023)                                                   , csite%mmsqu_cwd_rh     (donp)          &
  5024)                                                   , csite%area             (donp)          &
  5025)                                                   , corr_patch, .false.)
  5026)          csite%mmsqu_nep        (recp) = fuse_msqu( csite%mmean_nep        (recp)          &

  5028)                                                   , csite%area             (recp)          &
  5029)                                                   , csite%mmean_nep        (donp)          &
  5030)                                                   , csite%mmsqu_nep        (donp)          &
  5031)                                                   , csite%area             (donp)          &
  5032)                                                   , corr_patch, .false.)
  5033)          csite%mmsqu_rlongup    (recp) = fuse_msqu( csite%mmean_rlongup    (recp)          &

  5046)                                                   , corr_patch, .false.)

  5109)                                                   , corr_patch, .false.)

  5111)                                                   , csite%mmsqu_sensible_gc(recp)          &

  5116)                                                   , corr_patch, .false.)
  5117)          csite%mmsqu_sensible_ac(recp) = fuse_msqu( csite%mmean_sensible_ac(recp)          &

  5123)                                                   , corr_patch, .false.)
  5124)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------! 
  5125) 
  5126) 
  5127)          csite%mmean_rh                 (recp) = ( csite%mmean_rh                 (recp)   &

  5131)                                                *   newareai
  5132)          csite%mmean_cwd_rh             (recp) = ( csite%mmean_cwd_rh             (recp)   &

  5135)                                                  * csite%area                     (donp) ) &
  5136)                                                *   newareai
  5137)          csite%mmean_nep                (recp) = ( csite%mmean_nep                (recp)   &
  5138)                                                  * csite%area                     (recp)   &
  5139)                                                  + csite%mmean_nep                (donp)   &
  5140)                                                  * csite%area                     (donp) ) &
  5141)                                                *   newareai
  5142)          csite%mmean_rk4step            (recp) = ( csite%mmean_rk4step            (recp)   &

  5145)                                                  * csite%area                     (donp) ) &
  5146)                                                *   newareai

  5406)                                                *   newareai
  5407)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  5408) 
  5409) 
  5410) 
  5411)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  5412)          !      Now we find the derived properties for the canopy air space.               !
  5413)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  5414)          can_exner                   = press2exner (csite%mmean_can_prss(recp))
  5415)          csite%mmean_can_temp (recp) = extheta2temp(can_exner,csite%mmean_can_theta(recp))
  5416)          csite%mmean_can_rhos (recp) = idealdenssh ( csite%mmean_can_prss  (recp)          &
  5417)                                                    , csite%mmean_can_temp  (recp)          &
  5418)                                                    , csite%mmean_can_shv   (recp)          )
  5419)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  5420) 
  5421) 
  5422) 
  5423)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  5424)          !      Find the soil mean temperature, liquid water fraction, and matric          !
  5425)          ! potential.                                                                      !
  5426)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  5427)          do iii=lsl,mzg
  5428)             nsoil = ntext_soil(iii)
  5429)             call uextcm2tl( csite%mmean_soil_energy(iii,recp)                              &
  5430)                           , csite%mmean_soil_water (iii,recp) * wdns                       &
  5431)                           , soil(nsoil)%slcpd                                              &
  5432)                           , csite%mmean_soil_temp  (iii,recp)                              &
  5433)                           , csite%mmean_soil_fliq  (iii,recp))
  5434) 
  5435)             csite%mmean_soil_mstpot(iii,recp) =                                            &
  5436)                                    matric_potential(nsoil,csite%mmean_soil_water(iii,recp))
  5437)          end do
  5438)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  5439) 
  5440) 
  5441)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  5442)          !     Find the temporary surface water properties.  They may not be available at  !
  5443)          ! all times, so we must check.                                                    !
  5444)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  5445)          !----- Temporarily make energy extensive [J/m2]. ---------------------------------!
  5446)          csite%mmean_sfcw_depth         (recp) = ( csite%mmean_sfcw_depth         (recp)   &
  5447)                                                  * csite%area                     (recp)   &
  5448)                                                  + csite%mmean_sfcw_depth         (donp)   &
  5449)                                                  * csite%area                     (donp) ) &
  5450)                                                *   newareai
  5451)          csite%mmean_sfcw_energy        (recp) = ( csite%mmean_sfcw_energy        (recp)   &
  5452)                                                  * csite%mmean_sfcw_mass          (recp)   &
  5453)                                                  * csite%area                     (recp)   &
  5454)                                                  + csite%mmean_sfcw_energy        (donp)   &
  5455)                                                  * csite%mmean_sfcw_mass          (donp)   &
  5456)                                                  * csite%area                     (donp) ) &
  5457)                                                *   newareai
  5458)          csite%mmean_sfcw_mass          (recp) = ( csite%mmean_sfcw_mass          (recp)   &
  5459)                                                  * csite%area                     (recp)   &
  5460)                                                  + csite%mmean_sfcw_mass          (donp)   &
  5461)                                                  * csite%area                     (donp) ) &
  5462)                                                *   newareai
  5463)          !----- Check whether there is enough surface water. ------------------------------!
  5464)          if (csite%mmean_sfcw_mass(recp) > tiny_sfcwater_mass) then
  5465)             csite%mmean_sfcw_energy     (recp) =   csite%mmean_sfcw_energy        (recp)   &
  5466)                                                /   csite%mmean_sfcw_mass          (recp)
  5467)             call uint2tl( csite%mmean_sfcw_energy(recp)                                    &
  5468)                         , csite%mmean_sfcw_temp  (recp)                                    &
  5469)                         , csite%mmean_sfcw_fliq  (recp) )
  5470)          else
  5471)             csite%mmean_sfcw_mass  (recp)  = 0.
  5472)             csite%mmean_sfcw_depth (recp)  = 0.
  5473)             csite%mmean_sfcw_energy(recp)  = 0.
  5474)             csite%mmean_sfcw_temp  (recp)  = csite%mmean_soil_temp(mzg,recp)
  5475)             csite%mmean_sfcw_fliq  (recp)  = csite%mmean_soil_fliq(mzg,recp)
  5476)          end if
  5477)          !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  5478) 		end if
  5479)       end if
  5480)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  5481) 
  5482) 
  5483) 
  5484) 
  5485)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------! 
  5486)       !    Mean diel.                                                                      !
  5487)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------! 
  5488)       if (writing_dcyc .and. (.not. fuse_initial)) then
  5489)         if( all(csite%qmean_can_prss > 10.0) ) then
  5490)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  5491)          !      First we solve the mean sum of squares as they depend on the mean and the  !
  5492)          ! original receptor data is lost after fusion takes place.                        !
  5493)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  5494)          do t=1,ndcycle
  5495)             csite%qmsqu_rh         (t,recp) = fuse_msqu( csite%qmean_rh         (t,recp)   &
  5496)                                                        , csite%qmsqu_rh         (t,recp)   &
  5497)                                                        , csite%area               (recp)   &
  5498)                                                        , csite%qmean_rh         (t,donp)   &
  5499)                                                        , csite%qmsqu_rh         (t,donp)   &
  5500)                                                        , csite%area               (donp)   &
  5501)                                                        , corr_patch, .false.)
  5502)             csite%qmsqu_cwd_rh     (t,recp) = fuse_msqu( csite%qmean_cwd_rh     (t,recp)   &
  5503)                                                        , csite%qmsqu_cwd_rh     (t,recp)   &
  5504)                                                        , csite%area               (recp)   &
  5505)                                                        , csite%qmean_cwd_rh     (t,donp)   &
  5506)                                                        , csite%qmsqu_cwd_rh     (t,donp)   &

  5827)                                                  * csite%area                     (recp)   &
  5828)                                                  + csite%qmean_transloss      (:,:,donp)   &
  5829)                                                  * csite%area                     (donp) ) &
  5830)                                                *   newareai
  5831)          csite%qmean_sensible_gg    (:,:,recp) = ( csite%qmean_sensible_gg    (:,:,recp)   &
  5832)                                                  * csite%area                     (recp)   &
  5833)                                                  + csite%qmean_sensible_gg    (:,:,donp)   &
  5834)                                                  * csite%area                     (donp) ) &
  5835)                                                *   newareai
  5836) 
  5837) 
  5838)          do t=1,ndcycle
  5839)             !------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  5840)             !      Now we find the derived properties for the canopy air space.            !
  5841)             !------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  5842)             can_exner                     = press2exner (csite%qmean_can_prss(t,recp))
  5843)             csite%qmean_can_temp (t,recp) = extheta2temp( can_exner                        &
  5844)                                                         , csite%qmean_can_theta(t,recp))
  5845)             csite%qmean_can_rhos (t,recp) = idealdenssh ( csite%qmean_can_prss (t,recp)    &
  5846)                                                         , csite%qmean_can_temp (t,recp)    &
  5847)                                                         , csite%qmean_can_shv  (t,recp) )
  5848)             !------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  5849) 
  5850) 
  5851) 
  5852)             !------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  5853)             !      Find the soil mean temperature, liquid water fraction, and matric       !
  5854)             ! potential.                                                                   !
  5855)             !------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  5856)             do iii=lsl,mzg
  5857)                nsoil = ntext_soil(iii)
  5858)                call uextcm2tl( csite%qmean_soil_energy(iii,t,recp)                         &
  5859)                              , csite%qmean_soil_water (iii,t,recp) * wdns                  &
  5860)                              , soil(nsoil)%slcpd                                           &
  5861)                              , csite%qmean_soil_temp  (iii,t,recp)                         &
  5862)                              , csite%qmean_soil_fliq  (iii,t,recp) )
  5863) 
  5864)                csite%qmean_soil_mstpot(iii,t,recp) =                                       &
  5865)                                  matric_potential(nsoil,csite%qmean_soil_water(iii,t,recp))
  5866)             end do
  5867)             !------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  5868) 
  5869) 
  5870)             !------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  5871)             !     Find the temporary surface water properties.  They may not be available  !
  5872)             ! at all times, so we must check.                                              !
  5873)             !------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  5874)             !----- Temporarily make energy extensive [J/m2]. ------------------------------!
  5875)             csite%qmean_sfcw_depth       (t,recp) = ( csite%qmean_sfcw_depth    (t,recp)   &
  5876)                                                     * csite%area                  (recp)   &
  5877)                                                     + csite%qmean_sfcw_depth    (t,donp)   &
  5878)                                                     * csite%area                  (donp) ) &
  5879)                                                   *   newareai
  5880)             csite%qmean_sfcw_energy      (t,recp) = ( csite%qmean_sfcw_energy   (t,recp)   &
  5881)                                                     * csite%qmean_sfcw_mass     (t,recp)   &
  5882)                                                     * csite%area                  (recp)   &
  5883)                                                     + csite%qmean_sfcw_energy   (t,donp)   &
  5884)                                                     * csite%qmean_sfcw_mass     (t,donp)   &
  5885)                                                     * csite%area                  (donp) ) &
  5886)                                                   *   newareai
  5887)             csite%qmean_sfcw_mass        (t,recp) = ( csite%qmean_sfcw_mass     (t,recp)   &
  5888)                                                     * csite%area                  (recp)   &
  5889)                                                     + csite%qmean_sfcw_mass     (t,donp)   &
  5890)                                                     * csite%area                  (donp) ) &
  5891)                                                   *   newareai
  5892)             !----- Check whether there is enough surface water. ---------------------------!
  5893)             if (csite%qmean_sfcw_mass(t,recp) > tiny_sfcwater_mass) then
  5894)                csite%qmean_sfcw_energy   (t,recp) =   csite%qmean_sfcw_energy   (t,recp)   &
  5895)                                                   /   csite%qmean_sfcw_mass     (t,recp)
  5896)                call uint2tl( csite%qmean_sfcw_energy(t,recp)                               &
  5897)                            , csite%qmean_sfcw_temp  (t,recp)                               &
  5898)                            , csite%qmean_sfcw_fliq  (t,recp) )
  5899)             else
  5900)                csite%qmean_sfcw_mass  (t,recp)  = 0.
  5901)                csite%qmean_sfcw_depth (t,recp)  = 0.
  5902)                csite%qmean_sfcw_energy(t,recp)  = 0.
  5903)                csite%qmean_sfcw_temp  (t,recp)  = csite%qmean_soil_temp(mzg,t,recp)
  5904)                csite%qmean_sfcw_fliq  (t,recp)  = csite%qmean_soil_fliq(mzg,t,recp)
  5905)             end if
  5906)             !------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  5907)          end do
  5908)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  5909) 		end if
  5910)       end if
  5911)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  5912) 
  5913) 
  5914) 
  5915)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  5916)       !    We now update the canopy thermodynamic propeties:                               !
  5917)       ! + csite%can_temp(recp)                                                             !
  5918)       ! + csite%can_rhos(recp)                                                             !
  5919)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  5920)       call update_patch_thermo_props(csite,recp,recp,mzg,mzs,ntext_soil)
  5921) 
  5922)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  5923)       !     Now we need to adjust the densities of cohorts. Because the patch area         !
  5924)       ! increased we want to retain the same total amount of mass and energy.              !
  5925)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  5926)       !----- 1. Adjust densities of cohorts in recipient patch ----------------------------!
  5927)       cpatch => csite%patch(recp)
  5928)       nrc = cpatch%ncohorts
  5929)       area_scale = csite%area(recp) * newareai
  5930)       call update_cohort_extensive_props(cpatch,1,nrc,area_scale)
  5931)       !----- 2. Adjust densities of cohorts in donor patch --------------------------------!
  5932)       cpatch => csite%patch(donp)
  5933)       ndc = cpatch%ncohorts
  5934)       area_scale = csite%area(donp) * newareai
  5935)       call update_cohort_extensive_props(cpatch,1,ndc,area_scale)
  5936)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  5937) 
  5938) 
  5939)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  5940)       !    Fill a new patch with the donor and recipient cohort vectors.                   !
  5941)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  5942)       !----- Allocate the temporary patch with room for all cohorts. ----------------------!
  5943)       if (ndc + nrc > 0 ) then
  5944)          nullify(temppatch)
  5945)          allocate(temppatch)
  5946)          call allocate_patchtype(temppatch,ndc + nrc )
  5947)          !----- Copy the recipient and donor cohorts to the temporary patch. --------------!
  5948)          call copy_patchtype(csite%patch(recp),temppatch,1,nrc,1,nrc)
  5949)          call copy_patchtype(csite%patch(donp),temppatch,1,ndc,nrc+1,nrc+ndc)
  5950)          !----- Reallocate the current recipient patch with all cohorts -------------------!
  5951)          call deallocate_patchtype(csite%patch(recp))
  5952)          call allocate_patchtype(csite%patch(recp),ndc+nrc)
  5953)          !----- Copy the temporary patch back to the recipient patch. ---------------------!
  5954)          call copy_patchtype(temppatch,csite%patch(recp),1,nrc+ndc,1,nrc+ndc)
  5955)          !----- Get rid of the temporary patch --------------------------------------------!
  5956)          call deallocate_patchtype(temppatch)
  5957)          deallocate(temppatch)
  5958)          !----- Sort cohorts in the new patch ---------------------------------------------!
  5959)          cpatch => csite%patch(recp)
  5960)          call sort_cohorts(cpatch)
  5961)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  5962)          !    We just combined two patches, so we may be able to fuse some cohorts and/or  !
  5963)          ! eliminate others.                                                               !
  5964)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  5965)          if (cpatch%ncohorts > 0 .and. maxcohort >= 0) then
  5966)             call fuse_cohorts(csite,recp,lsl,fuse_initial)
  5967)             call terminate_cohorts(csite,recp,elim_nplant,elim_lai)
  5968)             call split_cohorts(cpatch,green_leaf_factor)
  5969)          end if
  5970)          !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  5971)       end if
  5972) 
  5973)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  5974)       !    Now we update some variables that depend on cohort statistics, namely:          !
  5975)       ! + csite%veg_height(recp)                                                           !
  5976)       ! + csite%veg_displace(recp)                                                         !
  5977)       ! + csite%disp_height(recp)                                                          !
  5978)       ! + csite%veg_rough(recp)                                                            !
  5979)       ! + csite%total_sfcw_depth(recp)                                                     !
  5980)       ! + csite%snowfac(recp)                                                              !
  5981)       ! + csite%opencan_frac(recp)                                                         !
  5982)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  5983)       call update_patch_derived_props(csite,recp)
  5984)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  5985) 
  5986)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  5987)       !    Now we update the budget variables:                                             !
  5988)       ! + csite%wbudget_initialstorage(recp)                                               !
  5989)       ! + csite%ebudget_initialstorage(recp)                                               !
  5990)       ! + csite%co2budget_initialstorage(recp)                                             !
  5991)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  5992)       call update_budget(csite,lsl,recp)
  5993)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  5994) 
  5995)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  5996)       !    This subroutine will update the size profile within patch.                      !
  5997)       ! + csite%cumlai_profile(:,:,recp)                                                   !
  5998)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  5999)       call patch_pft_size_profile(csite,recp)
  6000)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  6001) 
  6002)       !----- Last, but not the least, we update the patch area ----------------------------!
  6003)       csite%area(recp) = newarea
  6004) 
  6005)       return
  6006) 
  6007)    end subroutine fuse_2_patches
  6008)    !=======================================================================================!
  6009)    !=======================================================================================!
  6010) 
  6011) 
  6012) 
  6013)    !=======================================================================================!
  6014)    !=======================================================================================!
  6015)    !     This subroutine combines the mean sum of squares of two quantities (x and y).     !
  6016)    !                                                                                       !
  6017)    ! xmean, ymean -- the mean values of x and y                                            !
  6018)    ! xmsqu, ymsqu -- the mean sum of squares of x and y                                    !
  6019)    ! xwght, ywght -- the weights for x and y                                               !
  6020)    ! r_xy         -- correlation between x and y                                           !
  6021)    !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  6022)    real(kind=4) function fuse_msqu(xmean,xmsqu,xwght,ymean,ymsqu,ywght,r_xy,extensive)
  6023)       use rk4_coms       , only : tiny_offset              ! ! intent(in)
  6024)       implicit none
  6025)       !----- Arguments. -------------------------------------------------------------------!
  6026)       real(kind=4), intent(in) :: xmean
  6027)       real(kind=4), intent(in) :: xmsqu
  6028)       real(kind=4), intent(in) :: xwght
  6029)       real(kind=4), intent(in) :: ymean
  6030)       real(kind=4), intent(in) :: ymsqu
  6031)       real(kind=4), intent(in) :: ywght
  6032)       real(kind=4), intent(in) :: r_xy
  6033)       logical     , intent(in) :: extensive
  6034)       !----- Local variables. -------------------------------------------------------------!
  6035)       real(kind=8)             :: xwmean
  6036)       real(kind=8)             :: xwmsqu
  6037)       real(kind=8)             :: ywmean
  6038)       real(kind=8)             :: ywmsqu
  6039)       real(kind=8)             :: w2sumi
  6040)       real(kind=8)             :: xwpywp
  6041)       real(kind=8)             :: r_xy8
  6042)       real(kind=8)             :: fuse_msqu8
  6043)       !----- External function. -----------------------------------------------------------!
  6044)       real(kind=4)    , external      :: sngloff     ! Safe double -> single precision
  6045)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  6046) 
  6047) 
  6048)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  6049)       !      Correct the scales.  If the property is extensive, we aggregate them, other-  !
  6050)       ! wise we find the weighted sum of squares.                                          !
  6051)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  6052)       if (extensive) then
  6053)          xwmean = dble(xmean)
  6054)          xwmsqu = dble(xmsqu)
  6055)          ywmean = dble(ymean)
  6056)          ywmsqu = dble(ymsqu)
  6057)          w2sumi = 1.d0
  6058)       else
  6059)          xwmean = dble(xmean) * dble(xwght)
  6060)          xwmsqu = dble(xmsqu) * dble(xwght) * dble(xwght)
  6061)          ywmean = dble(ymean) * dble(ywght)
  6062)          ywmsqu = dble(ymsqu) * dble(ywght) * dble(ywght)
  6063)          w2sumi = 1.d0 / ( (dble(xwght) + dble(ywght)) * (dble(xwght) + dble(ywght)) )
  6064)       end if
  6065)       r_xy8     = dble(r_xy)
  6066)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  6067) 
  6068) 
  6069)       !----- Find the terms. --------------------------------------------------------------!
  6070)       xwpywp = r_xy8 * sqrt( ( xwmsqu + xwmean*xwmean) * (ywmsqu + ywmean*ywmean) )
  6071)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  6072) 
  6073) 
  6074)       !----- Add the terms to the answer. -------------------------------------------------!
  6075)       fuse_msqu8 = ( xwmsqu + ywmsqu + 2.d0 * ( xwmean * ywmean + xwpywp ) ) * w2sumi
  6076)       fuse_msqu  = sngloff(fuse_msqu8,tiny_offset)
  6077)       !------------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  6078) 
  6079)       return
  6080)    end function fuse_msqu
  6081)    !=======================================================================================!
  6082)    !=======================================================================================!
  6083) 
  6084) 
  6085) end module fuse_fiss_utils
